/ /bya bral rgan po'i 'dir snang 'khrul pa'i gtam/ /rtogs brjod tshul du mi 'grigs bzhin bsgrigs pa/ /blo gsal sgeg mo'i me long zhes bya ba/ /gzhan snang 'brid pa'i 'chal
gtam 'di na dge/ //

/ /mkhyen brtse'i bdag nyid rtsa brgyud bla ma dang / /mchog thun dngos grub kun stsol yi dam lha/ /phyi nang bar chad kun sel srung ma'i tshogs/ /'phral dang yun du shis pa'i
dge legs stsol/ /khyad par ma nor lam ston rje btsun mchog /'khrul bral sa skya'i 'jam mgon yab sras dang / /'gran zla kun bral drin can mkhyen rab rjer/ /snying nas
'dud do byang chub bar du skyongs/ /mchog thun dngos grub myur stsol he badzra/ /khams gsum dbang sdud lha mchog dmar po gsum/ /dran pas bdud dpung tshar gcod mahA kA las/
/bdag gi 'dod pa'i don kun sgrub par mdzod/ /de ltar dam pa rnams la gus btud nas/ /bya bral 'khyams po'i 'di byas 'di byung rnams/ /yi ger bkod la dgos pa ci yang med/
/de bas bsam gtan thun gcig bsgoms pa dga'/ /'on te dad ldan slob bus nan ches pas/ /mi tshud bzhin du dam pa'i gral ring

du/ /rgyu skar phreng bar du ba mjug ring bzhin/ /snyegs 'di mkhas rmongs kun gyi spyi srol yin/ /de phyir yon tan nyin mo'i skar ma tsam/ /skyon ni sa chen rdul ltar gyur
mod kyang / /skyon rnams rkun po'i nor ltar rab sbas nas/ /yon tan gang yod lhug par bri bar bya/ /de'ang mkhas grub dam pa mang po'i zhabs pad bsten pa'i sku drin las yon
tan gyi cha cung zad yod pa'ang srid mod/ gzhan shes rab dang brtson 'grus ni shin tu chung / snyom las dang le lo ni che rab che bas skyon yon mgo ma snyoms pa'i stobs
kyis 'di byas dang 'di byung gi ngo mtshar ba'i yon tan gyi cha ni zhu rgyu til 'bru tsam yang med/ ba ma lang tho cho'i spyod pa ni rtsis grangs gdab tu med pa zhig byas
pa dang / byed 'gyur/ byed bzhin pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab pas brir yang ma langs/ bris pa la dgos don yang mi 'dug la/ thams cad dran pa'ang mi gda' bas na/ skyes nas da
lta'i bar

lung du ma bstan pa'i spyod pa thams cad sba gsang med par cho le smras gtong bas de la dgyes pa yod na'ang legs/ mi dgyes pa yod na'ang legs pas gsan par zhu/ de'ang sngon
gyi skyes bu dam pa rnams kyi rtogs brjod du sku tshe mang po'i skyes rabs kyi phreng ba tshad las 'das pa 'byung mod kyang / blun po bdag gis kha sang gi bya byed de ring
mi dran pa 'dug pas/ skye ba sngon ma gang yin gyi cha rgyus ni cir yang mi dran pa gda'/ 'on kyang dal 'byor gyi ming tsam thogs lugs la dpag na mi dge ba rngam po che
rang ni byas pa min tshod du 'dug /tshe 'di'i dbang du byas na bod 'dir ni rus che che mo dang / skye ba brgyud brgyud mo nyid kham po cher byed par snang yang / rang gi
tshul dang ldan pa ma byung na rus dang skye bas pho skyes pa rang 'ong ba'i nges pa mi 'dug kyang / rang gi ngos skal nas rus chen gyi gral du ma tshud kyang ngo sbed
mi dgos tsam gyi khungs gleng na/ bdag gi pha'i rigs ni sngon gyi dus su chos rgyal khri srong lde'u btsan gyi dus su sman pa mkhas pa mi dgur grags pa'i nang nas stod na
cher che 'ug pa brang ti gsum zhes pa'i nang tshan cher cha'i brgyud pa rim par mched pa byang bdag po'i sman pa sgog sprod pa zhes bya ba'i rigs las sman pa shin tu mkhas
pa dwags brgyud pa'i bya bral ba'i cha lugs can zhig bde chen chos 'khor du bzhugs pa nang don gyi rtogs pa shin tu mtho ba yin 'dug kyang / sngon gyi las 'brel zhig gis
'brog pa bkab tshes kyi rigs kyi bud med zhig la dbang gsum pa'i dus dga' ba nyams su myong ba las bdag gi pha rgan de byung ba yin 'dug /bdag gi ma zhang gi rigs ni sngon
gyi dus su dwangs ma 'o mtsho'i glu mo dang gnam lha gnyis khye'u pho mor byas te ya 'brog na dmar gyi thang la babs pa 'brel ba las sgo

nga gsum byung ba pha ni lha yul du song / ma ni rgya mtshor song zhing sgo nga der lus pa/ sha ba yu mo zhig gi drod kyis bskyangs pa las khye'u shin tu mdzes shing ying du
'ong ba gsum byung ba che ba pha'i rjes su lha yul du song / chung ba ma'i rjes su mtsho nang du bros/ 'bring po de nyid duu lus pa 'di 'dra mi yul du dkon zhes smras pas
she'u dkon pa dar du btags pa de 'dra'i rigs las mched pas lum pa dpon chen gyi brgyud du grags pa'i rigs she'u lo tsA ba'i dbon brgyud dpon lhun grub ces pa'i sras mo
de bdag gi ma yin zhing / pha rgan ni gso ba rig pa'i gzhung lugs phul phyin zhig yin cing / ma de'ang byams snying rje dang ldan pa de gnyis kyi bur 'phags pa'i yul du
dza ya zhes 'bod pa rgyal ba/ bod gangs can gyi ljongs 'dir shing pho rta'i lo gro bzhin can gyi dmar phyogs bzang po gsum pa/ res gza' lha'i bla ma dang / rgyu skar rgyal
dgyes dgur spyod pa'i 'grub sbyor yod pa'i tshes nyer bdun gyi nyi shar gyi dus su sbugs stong rab brtan chos 'khor gling bla brang du ma las bdag skyes pa yin 'dug cing
/ bu chung 'bras bzang mdzes pa mthong na dga' ba zhig yod ces gleng / pha ma gnyis gces shing 'byor pa'ang dga' rab yod pas dkar gsum mngar gsum sogs kyis bskyed bsrengs/
de'i tshe zhang po 'jam dbyangs rgyal mtshan shin tu brtse ba zhig yod pa des byams par mdzad/ khong pa shes rab kyi rtsal gzhan dang mi 'dra ba'i rtsom pa thogs med
du 'ong ba yin pas ka smad sum bcur spel ba'i rtsom pa 'phral 'phral mdzad/ byis pa chung ngu'i kha nas ci zer med kyang cal col 'ga' re smras 'dug par/ 'di yol mkhan chen
gyi sku skye nges par yin par 'dug /ming yang gzhon nu blo gros thogs gsung / de nas rang lo lnga lon dus pha drin can des sgrig la bcur nas mal gru bzhir bzos/ mgo

sngas su 'jog mi 'jug /kha ton kyang ngag sprod gnang ba'i gong ma lnga bstod dang / rnam rgyal gyi bstod pa 'chi med dpal sbyin ma la sogs pa kha yar shes shing / klog kyang
'byor klog pher ba yod/ de nas sa khyi hor zla lnga pa'i yar tshes gsum la dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams bkra shis grags pa rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang po dbus phyogs su chibs kha bsgyur nas thub bstan ra ba smad du pheb/ pha ma gnyis sogs thams cad pheb pa'i sta gon mdzad 'dug par shin tu spro bar byung
shing / nga la paN chen ga ya dha ra'i dbu zhwa 'dra ba zhig bzo rogs dgos byas par de 'dra ba bzos/ ring 'gag dmar po gyon/ ras gzan dmar po zhig la gzan khyer byas pa'i
btsun gzugs kyi khungs yin khul byas/ de dus khro spos 'dzin gyi glang gzugs shig yod pa la po ti chung ngu zhig bkal te 'khrid pa'i khungs byas/ rang gi pha ma/ sru
mo/ zhang po sogs du ma dang mnyam du phyin/ byed lugs la dpag na a tsArya ltogs 'khyams pa zhig gi bag chags 'dra ba'ang yod/ de nas ra ba smad slebs pa'i nyin sngags 'chang
bla ma chibs bsgyur gnang byung ba sngar 'dris lta bu'i dga' spro dang bcas gzims chung du mjal dus/ pha rgan gyis nged la phyag rten dzi kShiM las grub pa'i ston pa'i
sku mkhyid gang ba/ gsung rten 'khrungs rabs brgya pa'i glegs bam/ thugs rten gdung rten lcags rtse ma/ bsod nams kha btags bcas bsgrigs nas gnang byung ba mgron gnyer
gyis blangs kyang gtad par sku zhabs rang gi phyag tu phul/ zhal 'dzum pa dang bcas phyag tu bzhes pa gnang / mjal mi dpag tu med pa 'dug kyang bzhugs khri'i

sku mdun de khar o lo rang 'di khar sdod cig ces bka' stsal/ nga rang la brtse ba'i sru mo dge tshul ma zhig yod pa de'ang nga'i drin las bzhugs khri'i mdun rang du 'jog par
gnang / sku zhabs gzims chung gi ka ba la zhabs 'chag gnang ba'i dus su'ang bdag gi mgo la phyag rjen par 'jog pa yang yang stsal/ skra phud phul bas ming kun dga' lhun
grub tu 'dogs pa gnang / chos grwa de nyid du grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe dbang / gur mgon khro bcu'i rjes gnang / rdo rje sems dpa'i bsgom lung / rong ston gyis mdzad pa'i
sher phyin bka' babs drug gi khrid sogs thob yig tu gsal ba ltar sku drin du stsal/ chibs kha bsgyur gdong o lo 'di gong dkar du khrid shog /gre ba bde mo byung na chos
mang tsam 'chad rgyu yin pheb pa ltar gong dkar du'ang zhabs phyir 'brengs pas rdo rje phur pa'i stod las byang chub sgrub pa'i dbang / sgrub thabs brgya rtsa lung bcas/
'chi med dpal ster gyi tshe dbang sogs rnam grangs mang du stsal/ de nas dpal sa skya pa gtsang du chibs kha bskyod/ bdag rnams ra ba smad du 'ongs/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas
bzang pos 'jam mgon sa skya pas bka' dbang gnang ba'i tshe bum gyi steng nas grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe dbang gnang / rnam 'grel dang rigs gter rtsa ba'i dpe gnyis gnang
nas byis pa 'di grwa tshang du cis kyang thong / dpe 'di gnyis 'dzin chug ces bslab bya gnang sbyin rgyas par byung / de nas rang gnas su log nas rang lo bdun gyi bar du
klog yig sbyangs/ rang lo bdun thog tu slebs 'phral rtsa rgyud brtag gnyis blo la byang bar byung zhing / gzhan yang 'jam dpal mtshan brjod sogs chos spyod che phra nyi shu
rtsa gcig

tsam blo la yod cing / pha drin chen des nyin bstar kye rdor rgyud gsum gyi klog khrol dang / snga dgong sgrig ltar gyis rgyud dang chos spyod chag med du byed pa sogs las
tha mal du lus ma bcug pas de dus ni khag sbyong che bar byung kyang deng sang dbu shar gang la'ang ma thogs tsam 'ong ba 'di gcig pu'i drin la'ang bsam las 'das/ lo de nang
du kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ges mdzad pa'i kye rdor man ngag rnam bshad dpe 'dzin gyi thog nas 'gril/ zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i nang du kun mkhyen rong ston chen po dang
/ rje grags 'byor shes rab sogs kyis gdan sa smon dga' rin chen bsam gtan gling gi dgon gnas dam par phyin/ drin can pha ma rnams kyis gral ston sogs rgyas par mdzad/ byis
pa hams can zhig yin pas tshogs kyi dbus su rtse zhwa phrag la bzhag /langs nas kye rdor rnam bshad ma rdzogs bar nyin bstar tshogs pa ja thug mchod pa'i gseng thams cad
la skad che bar bton pas grwa pa thams cad dgyes rtser son/ gral gong du gdan bzos dang bcas skyel bar mdzad/ nged rang gi kun dga' chos 'phel zhang po bla ma yin cing
brtse bar yod pas 'phags pa'i gser sku zhig dang / ngor chen gyi bris sku phyag nas ma 'khrul med sogs ster bar mdzad byung / de nas bla brang du zhang po'i rtsar bcar sdod
byas/ na so gzhon kyang pha ma sogs dran pa dang sdod mi tshugs pa ma byung / rang lo dgu par rmor gyi dbu mdzad kun dga' dpal ldan sar gnas kyi slob dpon zhus/ thog
mar kun rig gzhan phan mtha' yas blo 'dzin byas nas phyag len phra rags thams cad la phyag khrid mtha' chod pa/ de nas rim gyis stong ra chos rje kun dga' legs

grub kyis mdzad pa'i tshe dpag med lha dgu'i cho ga 'dzugs khrid slob dpon dang lhan cig tu zla ba gcig gi bar rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor bzhengs nas nyin re bzhin cho ga tshar
gsum re blo thog nas btang / de nas rang lo bcur slebs dus zhang po dang slob dpon gnyis char nas kye rdo rje zhag bcu gcig la 'gril ba byung na tshar kha ster gsung
bar brten/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i mngon rtogs bya bral ma/ dbang chu gsal ba'i me long mus chen nam mkha' dbang phyug gis mdzad pa'i lhan thabs/
bstod pa nyi shu pa dang daNDa ka gnyis/ gtor chog dgra las rnam rgyal bkra shis mtshungs med ma'i bar bde thogs med par shes rab kyi stabs zhag bcu gcig song thog rgyug
phul bas shin tu mnyes/ zhang po lags kyis rje sa chen gyi bris sku byin can zhig dang / slob dpon gyis dpe cha tshang ba gnang nas/ ha'u a/ shes rab la a gsungs dgyes
tshor chen por mdzad/ de nas rim bzhin kye rdo rje'i kun tu dgos pa'i gzhung bdun/ rnam 'grel gyi rtsa ba/ rigs gter/ sdom gsum bcas lo bcu gsum tshun la blo la byang bar
byas/ me rta shar nas rang lo bcu gsum gyi steng stag tshang ra ba smad du mtshan nyid kyi slob gnyer la 'gro ba'i sgo dod yang / zhang po nas 'di kha'i tshogs 'don yin
pas mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho rgyug ma sprad par phyin na mi 'ong gsung / bla brang du dpe mtshams byas nas nub so byas pas zhag nyi shu rtsa lnga'i khongs su ngor chen gyis
mdzad pa'i mngon rtogs dkyil chog /mchod phreng / gung rus mdzad pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi bstod pa 'dul 'dzin ma dang bcas pa gtsang sing rgyug

sprad/ lo de'i hor zla bcu gcig pa'i tshes bco lnga la ra ba smad grwa tshang du phyin/ gza' tshes kyi khyad de nub nas sku rim gyi tshogs su phyin pas chos spyod gzhung bsgyur
gyi mtshams rang du slebs 'dug par mkhan chen kun dga' gsang sngags kyi zhal nas khyod kyi snga sor nas sangs rgyas bstan nyi ma bzung tshar 'dug pas rten 'brel khyad
do nub de kha rgyug phul gnang byung bas skad shugs chen pos rong ston gyis mdzad pa'i g.yag ston gyi rnam thar bstod pa sangs rgyas bstan nyi ma dge skos kyis da chog
gsungs kyang ma nyan par yongs rdzogs mdzad byang dang bcas pa bton pas tshogs pa thams cad bzhad gad thig ge byung song bas rten 'brel legs po byung zhes gnang mi mang po
byung kyang rten 'brel legs nyes ji ltar yang nged rang stod ba de song nge ba byung / de nas sku drin 'khor thabs med pa'i mkhan chen kun dga' gsang sngags kyis brtse
bas skyong ba'i mgo tshugs/ pha rgan gyis grwa tshang la gral ston legs por mdzad song / gzhung sa rab 'byams pa chos skyong bzang pos gnas kyi slob dpon mdzad/ mkhan chen
nyid kyis nyin mo chos ra'i rtsi bzhag thog srod tho rengs gnyis su'ang gzims chung du rtsi shag re bka' drin bskyangs/ gza' tshes legs par dge tshul gyi sdom pa stsal/
shes rab ni a tho yod pas kha dog dkar dmar bsdus chung dang bcas par zla gcig las sdod ma dgos/ de nas rim gyis bsdus pa rnams lo phyed gnyis tsam la dga' rab byung zhing
/ sa sprel ra ba smad pa'i dus mchod grub nas mkhan chen kun dga' gsang sngags kyis 'chad nyan khur phog bye rdzing tshogs su thegs/ de 'phros kyi bsdus ra dang pod chen
drug sogs mkhan chen

ngag dbang don grub kyi drung du tshang bar zhus/ grwa tshang gi 'chad nyan du bsam yas pa dge ba'i dbang po pheb/ sger du chos ra 'phel ba rang ni byung ma song kyang gra
tshogs shin tu che bas rgyun du phyed nyis brgya ma chag par byung / rang lo bco brgyad par sgrig skyur byas/ bcu dgur gling bsre dang / nyi shur bka' bcu'i ming btags byas/
nyer gcig la rtses dong du grwa bskor la phyin/ zhor la gdan sa mthil dang yar klungs rten gsum yang rgyas par mjal/ nyi shu rtsa gnyis sa yos lo la gtsang du grwa bskor
la phyin pas yar lam ru mtshams kha reg gi shar dbus smad du pha rig 'dzin chen po dang mjal/ lam du song gshis zhib par ma byung kyang shin tu dgyes pa'i bka' stsal
lhug par gnang bas mi ring bar bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i mkhan por gsol ba btab pa ltar dgyes bzhin du zhal gyis bzhes/ yar lam snye mo brgyud sa skya'i grwa bskor ma tshugs
par 'jad thub bstan yangs pa can du mus chen bkra shis lhun grub zhabs drung du slob bshad snang gsum rdzogs pa dang / sbyong rgyud kyi bshad bka' gung ru'i zin bris dang
gzhan phan mtha' yas sbyar ba'i gsung bshad/ phyag rgya'i 'ching lugs sogs phyag khrid lung bcas dang / kye rdor rgyu dbang / kun rig gi dbang / tshe dpag lha dgu'i dbang
/ rnam rgyal dang rnam 'joms kyi rjes gnang lung sogs mang du zhus/ zla ba phyed gnyis bar bsdad/ de nas gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa skya'i dgun chos kyi thog bstan pa'i
rnam gzhag sa bcu gsum tsam byung zhing bdag chen yab sras kyi zhabs drung nas bdag rkyen la sogs pa

phul du phyin pa byung / bshad pa dang 'bel gtam sogs thag thogs med pas mkhas pa rnams dgyes pa bskyed nus pa byung ba de dus kyi 'dus tshogs thugs mi khrel ba yod/ phyi nang
gi rten mchod rnams dang khyad par bse mgon yid bzhin gyi nor bu sogs zhib par mjal/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dar ba'i smon lam rgyas par btab/ sngags 'chang kun dga'
bkra shis kyi zhabs drung du 'jam dbyangs a ra pa tsa na'i rjes gnang dbu rtse chen mo'i 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od 'bar ba'i sku mdun du thob pas/ 'jam dpal dbyangs dngos kyis
'jam dpal dbyangs dngos dang dbyer ma mchis pa'i zhabs drung du 'jam dbyangs kyi rjes gnang thob pas skal ba bzang ba'i yang rtser son/ de grol nas lha rtse gzhung brgyud
pha bla ma tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i bsti gnas rmuu gshongs dge ba'i tshal dang / mang mkhar mu gu lung thub bstan dge 'phel/ cha lung / 'dar stod bla ma'i gdan sa
rnams mjal/ rim gyis rngos la brgyud ngams rings dga' ldan byams pa'i gling gi chos sde chen por slebs/ mkhan chen ngag dbang don grub kyi sku mched chos rje bsod nams
zer ba'i brang khang du gnas tshang byas/ sang nyin rang nas grwa bskor tshugs pas zla ba phyed gnyis kyi bar bshad pa rig lung sogs nas khyag nges byas pa'i khul yin/ nged
rang gi zla grogs la rgyal gling pa phyis ra ba smad kyi bla ma yud tsam byas pas mkhas mchog chos rgyal yod pa khong pa gnas mjal sogs la dgyes po med kyang bdag rang
de dus dad mos dga' rab yod cing / rogs kyang gang nyan byas pas blo mthun yod cing grwa bskor grol nas rje sa skya pa chen po sku'i bkod pa bsdus pa'i gnas

skya bo kha gdangs/ sgye chu stag ris rgya mkhar/ bde grol sogs mjal/ smon lam btab/ bya bral bar song gshis mchod pa dang snyan dar rang ni shog chen ma byung / mar lam mdog
brgyud se mkhar chung / mdog gi jo bo chen po'i gtsug lag khang / jo nang / brag ram/ mus stag mo gling kha sogs dang / zhe dgon/ lung phu sogs kyang chad med mjal/ sna
thag mi la ma shor ba'i rang snang bar gang shar lag tu blangs chog pa'i stabs nas sngon gyi skyes chen dam pa rnams kyi sgrub gnas na bza' brag phug pa dang / tsha mo
rong / kha'u/ byas 'gyur/ spun gsum 'ong kha/ snar thang byang chen/ dar lung sogs lus med du mjal/ thub bstan gong 'og /bzhad grwa tshang chen mo/ gser mdog can sogs bshad
grwa rnams su dam bca' sgros gleng kyang kho thag chod par snang / zos bde ba'i tshad cig byung / de nas bla ma'i gdan sa 'og min gnyis pa e waM chos ldan rdo rje'i pho
brang du slebs/ zhag bcu skor bsdad/ skal ba bzang khyad zla gam ser hrul zhig g.yar byung ba dang / grwa zhwa thar song zhig gyon/ lhung bzed nang du zan gong bcug nas
tshogs su lan kha yar phyin/ de dus mkhan chen lhun grub dpal ldan khri thog tu bzhugs par ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gi dbang khang du kye rdor gyi dbang rdul tshon la brten
pa/ lam dbang / mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs/ ngor lugs kyi mgon po'i bskang ba yongs rdzogs kyi lung sogs thob/ rten brten pa thams cad zhib par mjal/ spo 'bor ba'i khang
chung zhig tu gnas tshang byas/ ya mtshan pa'i rigs kyang 'ga' re snang / khro phu/ gangs can chos 'phel/ bkra shis lhun po rnams kyang legs par mjal/ gdan sa 'og dpal

rtse gdong du khri chen bsod nams bstan 'dzin dbang po'i zhabs drung du tshe dbang lcags sdong ma dang / sgrol dkar sogs chos bka' kha shas thob/ gdung brgyud rin po che sku
mched dang yang mjal/ bdag rkyen zur gsos sogs bla med bskyangs byung / de nas 'bras yul skyed tshal du zhag gsum bsdad/ ngo shes pa 'dra med kyang mtshan nyid pa'i dag
snang gi dges tshor yag po mdzad byung / dam bca' sgros gleng kyang dgong re bzhin byas/ yongs dril gtsang du lo phyed gnyis kyi bar du bsdad/ blo bskyed che zhing snang
bsod bde skyid pa'i tshad cig shar/ de nas rong chung brgyud mar lam chu bo rir mchog gi sprul sku rin po cher phyag dbang zhus/ zhag gnyis bsdad nas rang gnas thub bstan
ra ba smad du slebs/ ma drin can de dol du bzhugs yod pas der phyin/ yun ring ma mjal bas thugs yus pa'i spyan chab dang bcas dges tshor dpag med gnang / zhag nyi shu skor
pha rgan mon du thegs pa'i sku rim smar bar byas/ rang lo nyer lngar slebs pa sa pho rta lo snron zla ra bar thub bstan rdo rje brag gi gtsug lag khang chen por mkhan
po yongs rdzogs bstan pa rin po che'i gsal byed 'dul ba 'bum sde'i mnga' bdag blo bzang padma phrin las/ las kyi slob dpon rnam rab dwags po grwa tshang gi dpon slob bsod
nams rgya mtsho/ gsang ste ston pa gong dkar chos sde ba dpon slob ngag dbang o rgyan/ dus bsgo ba chos 'khor gnas pa smra ba'i dbang po phyogs las rnam rgyal/ kha skong
dge slong blo gsal/ grogs dan dge slong dge dbang bcas grangs tshang ba'i dbus su bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i sdom pa yang dag par nos/ brje ba rnam

gsum gyi skabs ming sngar gyi steng du ngag dbang 'jug pa gnang / khrims nyis brgya lnga bcu rtsa gsum mtha' dag phra zhing phra ba rang ma thub kyang 'chol bar ma song ba'i
ngo lkog med pa rang yid ches pa yod/ slar ra ba smad du slob gnyer gyi 'phros sngar bas kyang smar ba byas/ sems kyang spro ba bcas skyid par byung / de yan chad ni skyid
pa'i nyi ma shar ba'i skabs so/ /de nas rang lo nyer bdun lon pa lcags sprel zla ba dgu par bdag gi nu bo gcig nad babs lci bas na bar brten 'bod mi byung bas 'phral
du phyin kyang nad babs lod pas zhag gnyis nas lnga lam du gyur song / nu bo gzhon pa de'ang nad de nyid kyis 'phral du rkyen lam du gyur/ khyad par bdag las lo gnyis kyis
gzhon pa des gso rigs phul phyin shes shing gshis kha legs par zhig yod pa de'ang nad de nyid kyis btab nas zhag bdun thog tu 'das shing / de dus rig 'dzin chen pos gsung
ngag zhig 'dzugs pa gnang grabs kyis cis kyang 'ong thub par gyis zhes brtse ba'i bka' shog pheb pa dang / rang yang da lam cis kyang 'gro dgos bsam pa thun mong ma yin
pa yod kyang / las dbang gis mnar ba'i sprel lo zla ba bcu gcig pa'i nyer dgu nas nad kyis btab/ shin tu thu bar byung / pha rig 'dzin chen por gsung brtag zhus par kyang
gzhan gyis byad rbod kyi ltas shin tu che bar 'dug pheb pa'i rim gro rnams kyang 'bad rtsol gyi sgo nas bsgrubs kyang re zhig je lod la song / pha ma drin can gnyis thugs
brel la bkod/ nyin gcig zhang po'ang dgon pa nas pheb/ tshe 'di'i snang ba nub par nye/ yol ba sogs kyang nyer bsdogs grub/ gcig la gcig spyan hrig hrig tu gyur/ rang
gi 'di yin med pa'i snang ba 'gags pa zhig byung

mur/ btsun ma rgan mo dad mos che ba zhig yod pa des chang zhig khyer 'ongs pa nas phor chung gang byin 'dug pas cung zhig dran pa rnyed byung bar thams cad dga' ba thob/ de
nub rmi lam du pha rig 'dzin chen po dang mjal nas zhal du mid pa gnang / sku'i lto bar yun cung zhig bsdad pa'i snang ba shar/ sku'i gsang ba nas thon par rmis/ gnyid
sad 'phral lus kyi nad thams cad sbrul shun brjes pa ltar gar song med par song 'dug pas/ 'di rmi lam rang yin nam snyam pa'i ngang nas de snga phan lag pa nas 'then/ mdo
le'i steng la khyer dgos kyin yod kyang / har te langs/ phan tshun du phyin pas goms pa lnga drug la thogs med 'gro thub pa byung / nam 'di da ltar rang langs na dga' ba
snyam/ gnyid kyang ma byung ba'i ngang nas nam langs ma thag khyor khyor phyin pas skas gdang bu dgu tsam yod pa der yang thogs med du 'gro thub pa byung / pha ma gnyis
kyi dbu gnang ba thams cad nu bo 'das pa'i thugs khral yang bsangs/ blo lam du tshud pas shin tu dgyes pa'i gtang rag rgyas par gnang gin 'dug /bla ma thugs rje can gyi sku
drin las/ /'chi bdag kha ru tshud pa'i de'ur thar/ /da lta'i bar du bde bar gnas 'di yang / /skyabs mgon bslu ba med pa'i thugs rje lags/ /de'ang 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i
dbang phyug gi rnam thar du/ sdug po dngos su byung ba des chog gis/ /sdug gtam yi ger bris la dgos pa med/ /ces gsungs pa ltar dus 'di dag gi bsam mno btang na sdang
ba'i dgra'ang mchi ma 'chor ba yod na'ang dgos pa mi 'dug pas bskyur gzhag go /de nas rang lo nyer bdun pa'i mjug tu snga sor ni gsung ngag zhu ba'i spros pa ma byung
zhing / da bsams

na gsung ngag de dus byung na da lam zhu ba mi 'ong 'dug kyang da lam 'gro bar bskul ba 'di pha bla ma tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i thugs rjes bskul bar nges/ da ni
dal 'byor stong log ma byung ba zhig nges par bya dgos par 'dug /de'ang dpal ldan nA lendra na rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan
dpal bzang po nyid las gzhan med par thag chod de myur du 'gro dgos bsam pa las gzhan gang yang yid la ma dran/ de snga lo bcu dgu'i steng du dpal ldan rmor gyi bla
brang du kun rig gi dkyil 'khor yongs rdzogs kyi bsnyen pa zla ba bdun gyi bar bshad tshod dang mthun pa kha skong gi sbyin sreg kyang nyi ma bdun gyi bar byas shing / lo
'dir yang rta mgrin gsang sgrub kyi bsnyen pa zla ba bdun gyi bar byas/ de grol nas zla bo gnyis dang bcas 'phan yul du phyin/ bco brgyad bla brang du rje bla ma'i zhabs
drung du bsnyen/ gtso bor gsung ngag rin po che zhu ba'i snyan gsan dang / da lam gshed dmar gyi dbang sogs thugs rjes 'dzin dgos zhus par shin tu dgyes pa'i bka' las rmor
gyi bla ma rnams dang / khyad par she'u lo tsA ba bco brgyad dang thugs 'brel shin tu che bas de'i dbon brgyud yin par 'dug pas lam 'bras shin tu 'bul spro zhing / 'di
lo ston mjug tsam la rtse gdong zhabs drung sku mched la lam 'bras 'bul dgos yod pas de dus pheb pa dang / da lam thog mar tshar lugs dkar lha gsum gyi sgo 'byed pa yin
gsungs nas dang po tshe sbyin yid bzhin 'khor lo'i rjes gnang 'od zer drug sbrags thun mong ma yin pa mchod gshom sogs spros pa shin tu che ba'i

sgo nas bka' drin bskyangs pa rje bla ma las gsung gi bdud rtsi thob pa'i thog ma'ang 'di nyid yin pas tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i bstan pa la rang ngos nas bya ba
byas pa la blta ba'i rten 'brel 'grig cing / tshe'i rten 'brel yang 'grigs/ chag lugs tshe dpag med dkar po/ dbyangs can ma dkar mo gsum gyi rjes gnang / 'di sku zhang gi
chos yin zhes gshed dmar lha lnga'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang rgyas pa/ kye rdo rje'i rgyu lam gyi dbang rnams stsal zhing zhag lngar bsdad/ de nas 'phan yul nang
gi gnas mjal rgyas par byas/ chag la brgyud stag lung rwa sgreng rnams mjal/ tshur lam brag sgo mo mjal/ de'i la brgyabs nas yer pa'i gnas zhib par mjal/ rang gnas su slebs/
de'i dbyar gyi ring rnam rgyal 'joms/ sgrol dkar rnams kyi bsnyen pa bya rgyud spyi rnam gyi dgongs pa sor bzhag rung bar byas/ lo de'i zla ba dgu pa'i nang du ra ba
smad pa'i khams pa gnyis/ nged rang gi tsha bo blo gsal lo bcu 'gro ba bcas khrid nas slar yang nA lendrar phyin pas gsung ngag 'phral du ma tshugs kyang de bar sgrub thabs
brgya rtsa/ rgya mtsho/ grub chen brgyad cu/ zur bka' mang ba sogs chos bka' dpag tu med pa 'phral 'phral bka' drin bskyangs/ 'on kyang zla ba dgu tsam gyi bar chos
bsgugs la sdod dgos byung bar chas sogs rje bla mas bka' drin bskyangs/ gzhan yang rtse gdong yum drung sogs nas gnang bas phongs pa ma byung kyang / gsung ngag gi 'dod gdungs
kyis sems khral shin tu che bar byung / de bar du snye thang brag sna ba'i dge slong phan bde rgyal mtshan gyis skar rtsis kyi ri mo khrid pas

zhag mang ma 'gor bar shes/ deng sang zhag po re gnyis kyi rgyun yang sdod mi tshugs par chos 'phrog thob byed pa'i tshod na dga' rab yin snyam pa'ang byung / de nas hor zla
dang por gza' tshes bzang ba nas bzung gsung ngag rin po che 'dzugs pa gnang ba'i sgo dod/ de'ang rtse gdong zhabs drung sku mched la slob bshad dang / tshogs pa bying
la tshogs bshad dus gcig la gnang rtsis kyi snga dro gzims chung ka drug mar slob bshad/ phyi dro 'du khang chen mor tshogs bshad kyi thugs gra sgrig pa gnang / gong zhabs
rin po che nas slob bshad mi bcu gcig las mang bar mi 'gab bka' pheb par brten/ bco brgyad bla brang nas nged kyi rtsar bla ma bsam 'phel ba gnang nas sang nyin gsung ngag
tshugs rgyu yin/ de'ang babs 'di bzhin yin pas slob bshad rang du 'ong rtsis kyi bka' pheb bsgyur byung bas sa dang po thob pa lta bu'i dga' spro dpag med thob/ de'ang
sngon gyi kha skad cig la/ snga gru dang po kha drags su yod kyis khyer/ bar pa ni gru gla su yod kyis khyer/ bsam pa gtad pa mi bdag la gru'i skal ba med ces pa'i dpe
ltar/ 'phreng po gzhi ba dpon slob/ gsang phu mchod khang dpon slob/ chos sde srid gsum dpon slob rnams ni bla ma'i khur bzhes kyi dog 'tshangs mdzad/ bco brgyad rang gi
phyag mdzod kyis gtsos drung 'khor rnams ni kha drag ngoms nas dog 'tshangs mdzad 'dug /bya bral ba bdag ni tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i thugs rje'i 'od zer dang / pha
bla ma dam pa sku drin can des brtse bas ma bor bar snyan 'bul tsam zhu ma dgos par 'bad med du gnang ba ni bla ma'i thugs rjes bla lhag tu skyong ba'i sgo dang po'o/

/de'ang zhib tu brtags na deng sang gi dus pha bla ma sku drin can des bka' drin bskyangs pa'ang deng sang gi dus bcu gcig po de dag gi nang nas bdag gcig pu ma gtogs thams
cad kyi gsung ngag 'chad nyan gnang ba lta ci/ bsnyen pa tsam yang ma gnang bar pheb song ba thugs kyi me long du shar bar gdon mi za'o/ /a ho/ sngon bsags kyi las 'phros/
/tshar pa chos rje yi bstan la/ /rang byung 'bad med du zhugs 'di/ /sngon bsags kyi las 'phro rang yin pad/ /de'ang rang nyid snga mo nas tshar lugs la 'dris che ba med
par ma zad/ rtsa slob ngor pa rang yin gshis ngor pa rang gi kha 'dzin dam po byed pa zhig yod kyang / grwa tshang 'grim dus zhwa lu mkhan rin po ches lho mos su lam 'bras
gnang bar 'gro 'dod che bar byung kyang / rin chen chos kyang dkon la rtag tu 'tshe ba'ang mang / zhes gsungs pa'i don thog tu babs te dge rgan dang pha ma la sogs pas
slob gnyer gyi sgang la mi dran dgu dran mang po slob gnyer ma nus pa yin/ lam 'bras de'ang lugs gzhan zhig yin par 'dug /sdod tshugs na dga' gsungs byung bar/ lugs gang
yin rang dang rang gis shes te dbang med par 'gro rgyu ma byung / de nas phyag rten dang bcas bco brgyad bla brang du rje bla ma'i sku zhabs su bcar/ sor bcu snying gar
bkod/ dad mos kyi shugs drag po dang bcas thugs rtsa nas ma bor ba'i bka' slob rin po che spyi bor pheb pas rab dga'i sa thob pa lta bur gyur lags shing / bdag gis yang
yang thob pa zhig mi 'ong 'dug lags pas phyi dro'i tshogs bshad kyang bka' drin bskyang bar cis kyang tshud pa zhig thugs rjes 'dzin dgos zhus par/

ma gzhi de kha lags kyang / snying nas rang gi khrid bskyangs na da lam slob bshad mthar thon nyams khrid du bskyang / slar tshogs bshad zab pa rang re'i brgyud pa thun mong
ma yin pa zhig cis kyang 'bul thub pa byed pas thugs lhod pa gnang bar zhu/ zhes sku rtsed dang bcas zhal 'dzum dpag med gnang byung bas/ de ltar na thugs brtse ba nas
ma shor ba dgos tshul zhus/ de'i sang nyin snga dro nas mkhas grub gung ru shes rab bzang po sogs mkhas shing grub pa brnyes pa'i bla ma rim par byon pa'i gzims chung ka
drug mar rje bla ma seng ge'i khri la zhal nub phyogs su gzigs pa'i dbu thog tu gdugs/ g.yas su rgyal mtshan/ g.yon du ba dan/ sku mdun du chu bzhi sngon 'gro'i nyer spyod
sogs slob bshad pa'i phyag len 'khrul med ltar bkod mdzes su bshams pa'i mdun du gtso bo rtse gdong khri chen sku mched/ 'phreng po gzhi ba/ gsang phu mchod khang pa/ srid
gsum slob dpon bslab gsum bstan 'dzin/ bco brgyad rang gi phyag mdzod sogs mdor na tha chung bdag gis mtha' brten pa bcu gcig la/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug 'jigs bral dpal
ldan chos skyong gi bzhed gzhung gsung ngag rin po che slob bshad zab mo tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos legs par srol btod pa'i snang gsum gyi skabs 'jam dbyangs mkhyen
brtses mdzad pa'i gsung ngag byung tshul la ngor chen man gyi rnam thar rje bla ma'i thugs thog nas gnang ba'i ljags bshad/ zhi lhag gi ngo sprod dmigs su phug pa'i me tog
sngon po 'gyed pa sogs kyi phyag len phra rags thams cad sla chos su ma song bar/ bla ma lnga bcu pa'i 'grel par tshar chen rdo rje

'chang chen pos mdzad pa'i dngos grub sgo 'byed kyi steng nas sa gzhung spel ba'i zab bshad/ bdag chen rin po che'i yi ge'i steng nas brgyud pa'i khyad par gnyis ldan gyi sems
bskyed/ de nub slob ma rjes 'dzin slob bshad pa'i lugs ltar gnang ba nas rje bla ma kha gso'i ljags bsnyen la bzhugs/ 'phan yul gnya' gong nang sos mchod 'bru dang snum
sogs mthun rkyen sbyin byung bas zhag bdun gyi bar der sgrub pa'i maNDal tshom bu lnga pa bshams pa'i mdun du ci 'byor gyi mchod pa phul/ nyin bstar yang maNDal tshom
bu bdun pa stong phrag re dang / so bdun ma 'os 'tshams/ snga dgong brgya phyag re dang yig brgya lnga brgya re ma chag pa'i khungs byas/ dal bar ma bsdad par mig ltos la
phan re byas khul yin/ de nas sku mtshams grol 'phral bco brgyad bla brang gi dbang khang 'chi med pho brang du yab kyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dag bya dag byed kyi
dbang don ngo 'phrod pa/ khyad par slob dpon gyi dbang stegs steng slob ma re re nas gnang ba sogs slob bshad pa'i bzhed pa 'khrul med/ aShtA'i bzlas lung bcas stsal/ de'ang
rje bla ma 'di dbang gang dang gang gnang kyang gcig go gcig gis gcod pa 'di tshab 'dis 'ong sogs gtan mi gnang bar so so'i phyag len phra rags thun mong ba mi 'gal
zhing / thun mong ma yin pa ma 'dres pa'i sgo nas gsung bshad mtha' chod pa bka' drin bskyangs pas dbang thob lo tsam ma yin par so so'i grub mtha' 'di dang 'di'o snyam
pa'i nges pa brtan po rnyed pa 'ong bas deng sang dbang gi rigs spyi dang / khyad par slob bshad zab mo'i gnad la gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog pa'i spobs pa rnyed pa 'di gcig
pu'i sku drin yang gzhal bar nus pa'i tshad

ma mchis/ 'di skabs kyi dkyil 'khor thig dang tshon bkye ba sogs kyi zhabs phyir yang 'bod pa gnang / rje bla ma sgrub mchod gnang ba'i zhabs phyir yang sdod chog pa byung
bas skal ba mchog tu bzang ba'i bgo skal thob par gyur/ dkyil 'khor de nyid kyi steng nas tshogs bshad kyi bka' dbang yang gnang bas zhag nyi shu skor 'gor/ slob ma kha grangs
ma 'grigs pa'i skabs thams cad du phyin pas rgyu dbang tshar brgyad tsam song / de nas sngar lugs ltar tshogs slob so sor gnang ba'i 'khor 'das dbyer med kyi skabs
su bshad lung tsam ma yin par rig thog tu brdar sha chod pa slob bshad pa'i lugs ltar sems 'tshol gtong ba sogs gnang / bdag chen rin po ches mdzad pa'i 'khrul spong rab
gsal gyi steng nas sa gzhung spel ba'i bshad pa shin tu rgyas pa sngags lam la 'jug pa'i sngon du yum gyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs pa/ de
nas phyi nang gi khrid shin tu smin pa tshar chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa'i rnam bshad nyi ma'i 'od zer gyi steng nas sgro 'dogs gcod pa'i gsung bshad shin tu rgyas pa
ljags thog nas stsal/ gsang dbang gi khrid kyi thog mar sindhU ra'i dal la brten pa'i rje btsun yab yum gyi byin rlabs rgyas par stsal nas/ khrid dngos gzhi rgyal dbang
rdo rje 'chang chen pos mdzad pa la thams cad mkhyen pa klu sgrub rgya mtsho'i khrid yig nas kha 'gengs pa gnang ba'i dbang gong ma gsum gyi khrid gtum mo'i dmigs rkang
bco brgyad/ yan lag lnga sbyong / lus sbyong nyi shu pa/ phrin las so gnyis pa sogs so sor phyag khrid mdzub sprod/ zhar byung bar

do/ rmi lam/ sgyu lus/ 'od gsal/ 'da' ka ma dang bcas pa dbang bzhi so so'i mjug tu cha tshang ba slob bshad pa'i lugs ma 'khrul ba/ lung gi rim pa snang gsum gyi skabs bla
ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar tshang ba/ sngags lam tshugs nas lam 'bras glegs bam pod ser/ las dang po pa'i chos sna bdun dang bcas pa/ glegs bam pod dmar/ pod khra/ pod nag
/mngon rtogs lus dkyil/ dkyil chog bya bral ma/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos mdzad pa'i lhan thabs slob bshad la dgos pa cha tshang / bla ma'i rnal 'byor thun mong
dang thun mong ma yin pa/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi bsrung ba thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i byin rlabs/ bla ma rin 'byung / tshar gsum khug pa/ brda don gsal ba/
brda chig brgyud/ sgrub pa lung sbyin/ gsang bcu'i rgyas gdab/ rten 'brel gyi byin rlabs/ mgon rkyang gi rjes gnang gi bar cha lag yongs su rdzogs pa zla ba phyed bzhi'i
bar du stsal/ de mthun shod kyi tshogs bshad kyang grol/ gtso bor gsung ngag rin po che dang bar gseng thams cad du gsang ba 'dus pa lugs gsum/ bde mchog lU nag dril gsum/
bong zhal can/ mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho sogs dang / 'jigs byed/ gshed dmar lugs gnyis sogs zur bka'i rigs kyang dpag med stsal/ grangs bcad 'di thams cad la bdag nges par
tshud pa bka' drin bskyangs par 'ga' re nas phrag dog gi rnam pa byed mkhan yang byung song rung rje bla ma dus gsum sgrib med du gzigs pa des tha chung bdag gis da lta'i
lan skyel ba 'di lta bu 'byung ba la dgongs par snang / gsung ngag grol nas sku zhabs su 'bod pa gnang / re zhig 'gro'am

sdod bka' pheb par/ da lam rgyun yang lo gcig lhag par song gshis pha ma gnyis 'phrad pa sogs kyi stabs nas dgongs pa zhus/ slar mi 'gyang bar sku zhabs su 'ong chog pa dang
/ don gyi gtso bo gsung ngag tshogs bshad dang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i bka' khrid sogs thugs rtsa nas mi 'dor ba cis kyang mkhyen mkhyen zhus/ zhabs spyi bor bkod pa'i
phyag phul bas/ zhal 'dzum pa dang bcas shin tu 'ong bas re zhig pheb pa gnang kyang / yun ring por mi 'gor bar pheb dgos pa 'dug pas cis kyang thugs la gzhug dgos zhes
shin tu dgyes pa'i gsung dang bcas 'phags pa'i thugs dam rten gur mgon rgya nag ma mgor 'jog pa gnang bas bka' bsgo shin tu rgyas pa gnang / bdag grogs mched rnams kyi mig
mchi mas gang bzhin du 'bral mi phod pa'i tshul du phyi 'gros kyis 'ongs pas gzims chung gi sgo rgyab tu slebs dus/ bka' las/ da lam 'khor tsam pheb/ 'di'i ston 'jug tsam
la lam 'bras tshogs bshad nges par 'ong pas pheb pa zhu zhes bka' pheb byung bas dga' ba dang skyo ba lhan cig par de nub sdod gnas stong ra chos sde'i bla brang rdzogs
nub tu byed yod par der bsdad/ sang nyin shar la thon pas la chu sgang nas phyag mang du btsal/ myur du zhal dkyil mjal ba'i smon lam btab nas rang gnas su log /thog mar
pha ma drin can gnyis dang mjal bas dgyes tshor dpag med mdzad/ ngal bso dang sbrags zhag lnga drug bsdad/ de nas dben gnas rmor dgon du phyin/ chag med kyi rim pa bir
srung ma gtogs thun bzhi re ma chag pa dang / sgrub mchod kyi tshogs kyang rtag par phyin/ mkha' spyod ma'i gzhi bsnyen zhig bgyis/ blo gsal na

gzhon yang mtshams g.yog sogs bya nan par yod/ yang de ka'i ston dpal rgyun gyi dbang po'i chos grwa chen por phyin/ bla brang du slebs/ sku zhabs su shog gnang bar phyag rten
gya nom pa dang bcas mjal ma thag sngar bas kyang dad pa lhag par 'phel/ gsung gleng 'jam zhing bag pheb pa yun ring po'i bar du stsal bas re zhig rnam rtog rags pa thams
cad 'gags nas bde cham par gyur/ bka' las/ da re zhig bla brang rang du bzhugs/ chas kha'i spro bsdu sogs kyang mi 'tshal/ chos kyang zhor zhor du 'ong gnang bas dga'
ba dang spro ba stabs cig tu 'phel bar gyur/ 'di nas bzung chu spre'i bar lo bcu gsum gyi ring zla ba re gnyis ma gtogs rje bla ma'i zhabs pad dang mi 'bral bar bcar/ rje
btsun mi la'i zhal nas/ nor zang zing gi 'bul ba ma mchis kyang / sgyu lus kyi zhabs tog rdul du brlag /ces gsungs pa ltar zang zing gi zhabs tog rgya cher ma 'grub mod/
rje 'di nyid spyir zang zing la ma ltos pa'i thams cad la nye snyoms pa byang sems kyi mtshan nyid dang ldan nges yin par ma zad/ khyad par bdag la shin tu thugs brtse
bar yod/ lugs gnyis ka nas mchog tu bka' drin che bar bskyangs/ de'i lo ston mjug nas nA lendrar tshogs par gsung ngag tshogs bshad rgyas pa rgyab brten lung bcas tshang
bar stsal/ dgun rje bla ma cung zad sku ltem pa'i tshul bstan par sku rim sogs tshar grul che bar gnang bas zla ba gnyis tsam la sku dwangs/ phyogs kyi 'dus pa mang dag
la dam pa'i chos kyi dga' ston dpag med stsal/ de lo dbyar gyi ring ljags lung gi rigs shin tu mang ba brtse bas bskyangs/ de'i ston mjug kyang phyogs

'dus dang gnyug mar gnas pa bcas lnga brgya tsam la gsung ngag tshogs bshad mdzes rgyan gyi steng nas shin tu smin pa rgyab brten gyi lung / byin rlabs rags bsdus bcas rgyas
par stsal/ de'i dgun gyi bar rjes gnang zur bka'i rigs mang ba dang / sa skya'i bka' 'bum gyi lung rdzogs par gnang / de nas sos slob dpon a bha ya'i bzhed srol rdo rje
phreng ba bde legs su byed pa'i dkyil 'khor gsum bcas dkyil 'khor zhe lnga'i dbang bskur phyag len gtsang ma'i sgo nas gnang zhing / rgyab chos su phreng ba skor gsum gyi
dkyil chog rdor phreng mdzes rgyan gyi lung bcas bka' drin bskyangs shing / de'i phyi lo bdag rang lo nyi shu rtsa dgur slebs pa chu pho khyi lor da lta'i zhabs drung gdung
brgyud ngag dbang mkhyen brtse rab brtan dgung lo bdun bzhes pa'i thugs gnyer zhabs bskul zhu dgos tshul pheb pa'i bka' nan ldog ma nus par re zhig bar dgongs pa ltar
zhu zhus nas lo bdun gyi bar zhabs bskul zhus/ de nas lo 'di nang du'ang gsung ngag tshogs bshad 'bring po zhig stsal/ byi glang gnyis su 'phan yul gzhung dang nA lendrar
'brum pa mched stabs dbon rin po che'i zhabs phyir mnga' zhabs su tho btsun gnang ba'i btsun chung bcu gsum dang bcas bshes gnyen 'brom ston pa dang sku mched gsum gyi
zhabs kyis bcags pa'i bsam 'grub ri mkhar zhes da lta mkhar gdong du grags pa'i rdzong chung zhig yod pa der 'brum 'dzems gcad rgya gnang / de nas tho btsun rnams so sor
bkye ste nged dpon slob gsum gyis lo phyed gnyis tsam gyi bar bsnyen mtshams dam par gnang ba'i bdag gis gshed dmar/ 'jigs byed/

gur zhal sogs kyi bsnyen pa mthar phyin pa kha skang gi sbyin sreg dang bcas pa song / rje dbon rin po ches kyang gshed dmar sogs mang bar song / rje bla ma thugs brtse ba'i
stabs zhag bcu skor re la chibs kha lan re bskyod pas bzhugs zhag lnga drug re bzhugs stan 'jags ring rjes gnang dang lung gi rigs rgyun dkon zhing sngar ma gsan pa thams
cad rim gyis zhabs bskul zhus pa ltar dgyes pa'i sgo nas 'phral 'phral gnang / de bar du res 'ga' ni nA lendra dang yum bcas pas zhabs thog rgyas par gnang bas nged dpon
slob thams cad skyid du tshor ba'ang byung / dbyar dus su ni zhol gyi mi ser sa gtsang sa nas sgog btsong sogs blangs pa'i dka' thub se ba'ang dgos pa byung zhing / 'jig
rten pa'i kha skad la/ dpyid kyi gnam la grang gsum dro gsum 'ong zer ba dang mtshungs par byung / dbon rin po che'ang nged rang la thugs blo pheb pas thugs dam sogs mi
gnang kyang shin tu skyo ba'ang byung / 'brum thag chod nas nA lendrar pheb/ de lo pha stong ra ba chen po'i pod sngon ma sor bzhag gi steng nas lam 'bras shin tu rgyas
pa rgyab rten gyi lung dang bcas pa gnang / bka' las/ da lam gyi lam 'bras 'di nged rang sger gyi pha chos lta bu pha rgan rong ston chen po dang / mkhas grub gung ru shes
rab bzang po sogs brgyud par bzhugs pa'i 'gangs che ba rang yin pas do gal byed dgos/ zhes yang yang bslab don pheb/ de lo bdag gis rje bla ma mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang
po'i rnam thar dang / rje bla ma'i gsan yig sgrig pa sogs kyi zhabs phyi zhus/ de nas sa sbrul rang lo so drug pa'i dus gsang phu'i gling smad zhabs drung

dpal ldan grags pa sogs dang gnyug mar gnas pa gtsos lnga brgya skor la gsung ngag tshogs bshad thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyi mdzes rgyan sor bzhag steng nas
bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar ljags thog nas bka' drin bskyangs pa sogs ngor lugs thun mong ma yin pa sor bzhag snang gsum rdzogs mtshams su/ yar klungs bkra shis chos sde'i
dbon rin po che ngag dbang blo gsal mchog ldan dgyes mdzad rdo rje'i thugs kar sku'i bkod pa bsdus par rgyal dbang mchog gi bka' shog lam yig sogs stsal pheb ltar gsung
ngag snang gsum rdzogs nas yar klungs su chibs kha bskyod pa gnang / snyan brgyud bstan pa'i 'byung gnas bkra shis pa'i chos kyi sde chen por dbon rin po che'i sku gdung
drung du thugs dam gsal 'debs/ dbang bskur/ me mchod sogs rje bla ma'i mchod g.yog gi zhabs phyi bdag rang gis zhus/ phar phyin gyi pheb lam tshor yang sa lugs kyi dgon
pa thams cad nas spyan 'dren zhus/ bka' chos kyang nyin mtshan med par stsal ba'i phyag g.yog gang 'grub byas/ de nas gdan sa chen por pheb/ sngar gyi gsung ngag gi 'phros
smin rgyas su bka' drin bskyangs/ lo de nang du dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang rgyas pa dang / bde mchog mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i rdul tshon
la brten pa'i dbang / bde mchog nag po pa'i rdul tshon la brten pa'i dbang sogs dpag tu med pa stsal/ lcags rta zla ba dang por gtsang du chibs kha bskyod nas rim gyis
gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa skyar sngags 'chang thams cad mkhyen

pa chen po dang mjal/ 'bul nod bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang chos dung dkar po rgyang grags 'bud pa gnang / zla ba drug gi bar gzhi thog tu stan chags pa'i sngags 'chang bla ma
mchog gis dpal ldan sa skya pa'i yab chos rdo rje phur pa'i stod las byang chub sgrub pa'i dbang / smad las gdug pa sgrol ba'i rjes gnang / dpal kye rdo rje'i gtso che'i
chos sna sum cu rtsa dgu'i rgya gzhung gi ljags lung / dmar po skor gsum gyi be'u bum yongs rdzogs/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gyi bka' 'bum yongs
rdzogs kyi lung / dpyal lugs phag mo skor gsum gyi rjes gnang lung bcas/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs/ dkar bdud kyi rjes gnang / gur mgon khro bcu'i rjes gnang /
'chi med dpal ster gyi tshe dbang / rje bla mas phar sngags 'chang bla ma thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ thub bstan mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/
mkhan chen ngag dbang blo gsal bstan pa rab rgyas/ rje dbon ngag dbang mkhyen brtse rab brtan pa sogs la dpal dus kyi 'khor lo/ bde mchog mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho/ bde mchog
bong zhal can rnams kyi dbang rdul tshon la brten pa/ bka' gdams thig le bcu drug /phyag rdor 'gro bzang lha nyer gcig /rnam 'joms dkar po/ sgrol ma lha bcu bdun ma/ gur
rigs bsdus/ sambu Ta/ rdor dbyings rnams kyi dbang ras bris la brten pa/ rjes gnang zur bka' shin tu mang ba/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i bka' 'bum pod bzhi ma/ mus
chen sangs rgyas rin chen gyi bka' 'bum/ rnam sras kyi be'u bum pusti gnyis/ bsam gtan

gling pa'i a ti yongs rdzogs kyi lung sogs chos bka' dpag tu med pa 'bul ba gnang / de mtshungs thub bstan mkhan chen gyis thun mong du ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub kyi bka'
'bum pu sti gsum gyi lung / rje dbon rin po cher sger du kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge'i sngags 'bum pusti gsum gyi lung / ku ru kulle gsang sgrub lha lnga'i byin rlabs/
ngag dbang blo gsal bstan pa rab rgyas kyis thun mong du lam sbas bshad kyi thugs rdo rje'i khrid/ klu sgrub rje'i yi ge'i steng nas byin rlabs lung dang bcas pa 'bul
ba gnang / gong gsal 'di thams cad tshang bar thob pa'i steng du bdag rang gis thub bstan mkhan chen drung du dmar po skor gsum gyi rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa dang /
'jigs byed rwa lugs bcu gsum ma'i dbang tshar lugs thun mong ma yin pa khrid bcas zhus/ ngag dbang blo gsal bstan pa rab rgyas drung du beg tse 'khor mang gi rjes gnang /
nai gu'i khrid tshar lugs/ tshar chen rin po che'i gsung 'bum phal che ba'i lung / mkhan chen don grub legs bzang gi drung du sems tsam lugs kyi sems bskyed/ rnam sras lnga
phrag gsum gyi rjes gnang sogs zhus/ mdor na zla ba de tsam gyi bar du chos de tsam thob pa skal pa bzang ba'i mchog gnas dang / dus/ ston pa/ chos/ 'khor te phun sum
tshogs pa lnga ldan du gyur/ de nas rje bla ma dpon slob rnams byang lam brgyud nA lendrar pheb/ dbon rin po che dpon g.yog hrags bsdus mdo khams phyogs su pheb/ kho bos
re zhig zhabs phyir bsdad/ de bar blo gsal gyis gsol dpon zhus nas zla ba bzhi tsam

song bstun dgongs khrol zhus par/ re zhig kye rdor bsnyen chen sogs kyi stabs nas de kha byas nas 'gab ces pheb/ mtshams kyi ring gi ja mar dang / nyer mkho thams cad dang
/ mi dang mi ma yin gyi 'gro ba thams cad kyi bar chad sel zhing mthun rkyen sgrub pa'i bka'i spring yig dang bar chad kyis mi tshugs pa'i bka' bsgo rgyas par stsal/ 'bral
mi phod pa lta bur byung kyang zhabs spyi bor bkod pa'i smon lam dang / khyad par skye ba dang tshe rabs thams cad du rjes su 'dzin par mdzad du gsol/ zhes mchi ma'i rgyun
char ltar 'babs bzhin pa dang bcas rang gnas su log ste/ de yan chad du lo bcu gsum bar mi 'bral bar zhabs pad bsnyen pa'i skabs so/ /de'ang rje bla ma 'di nyid kyi zhabs
drung du yun de tsam song kyang thugs cung zad khro ba'i rnam 'gyur tsam yang gnang ba mi dran/ bka' lung gi rim pa'ang gtso bor gsung ngag tshogs slob sdom pa tshar
bcu gnyis/ rdo rje phreng ba tshar brgyad sogs/ mdor na rje bla ma'i gsan yig nang bzhin bum pa gang byo'i tshul du bka' drin bskyangs/ zang zing gi gnang cha'ang snga phyir
rta mdzo pho mo/ ja/ gos dar/ dkar yol sogs dpag med dang / khyad par phyag dpe sogs thugs dkyil nas ma bor ba yang yang bka' drin bskyangs pa'i sku drin byang chub
bar du gzhal mi nus mod/ 'on kyang bka' lung gang thob thams cad bed med du ma bzhag par rang gis nyams len gang nus dang / gzhan don gnyer can rnams la'ang ngal sun med
par phul bas sku drin bsabs pa la phan nam snyam pa ni yod/ de dag gi snga phyir dam pa du ma las zab pa dang rgya

che ba'i chos bka' thob pa rnams rags rim phyogs gcig tu smos na/ rang lo bcu bzhi pa'i dus chos 'khor gnas mkhan chen blo gros brtan pa'i drung du kye rdo rje'i dbang ras
bris la brten pa/ gur lha brgyad/ zhal bsnyen dus/ khyung khra/ 'byung 'dul/ ri khrod ma ser mo/ grwa pa'i dzam dmar/ sa lo'i bla mchod/ sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen gyis
mdzad pa'i yi dam chos skyong gi gtor chog /des mdzad pa'i gtor ma brgya rtsa rnams kyi lung / kun rig gi dbang bcas zhus/ rang lo bco lnga pa'i steng gling stod pa chen
po dkon mchog dpal 'byor gyi drung du kye rdo rje'i dbang ras bris la brten pa/ 'byung 'dul/ ri khrod ma/ rta mgrin gsang sgrub kyi rjes gnang / tshe dbang 'chi med dpal
ster/ rngog lo'i bstod pa/ birWa pa'i bstod pa dad chu ma/ gong ma lnga bstod/ mtshan brjod/ ngor chen gyi bstod pa rab sde rba gsum/ sems dpa' chen po'i bstod pa thub
bstan gser khang ma/ g.yag rong rnam gnyis kyi bstod pa sha lo ka re/ 'chi med dpal sbyin ma bcas thob/ rang lo bcu bdun pa'i dus su dge rgan gyis khrid zhengs stegs su
nam mkha' rig 'dzin dbang drag pa'i drung du nyang grags rdo rje rtsal gyi dbang lung / dkon mchog spyi 'dus kyi dbang / tshe dbang bcas dang chos skor pusti yongs rdzogs/
grub mtha' mdzod dang theg mchog mdzod kyi lung bcas thob/ rang lo nyer bzhi pa'i dus 'jam mgon bsod nams dbang phyug yab sras dbus su chibs kha bsgyur/ ra ba smad du
pheb pa'i dus tshogs su jo bo rje nas brgyud pa'i sgrol ma nyer gcig gi rjes gnang / sme brtsegs dud ka'i

rjes gnang bkru byabs dang bcas pa/ mi g.yo ba dkar sngon gnyis kyi rjes gnang / sher phyin dkar ser gnyis kyi rjes gnang / grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe dbang rnams 'jam mgon bsod
nams dbang phyug gis stsal/ gong dkar chos sder kye rdor ras bris la brten pa'i dbang / lam dbang / yang dag zla gam dgu pa'i dbang / 'jam mgon kun dga' bkra shis kyi
drung du phur pa'i stod las byang chub sgrub pa'i dbang rnams zhus/ rtse gdong khri chen bsod nams bstan 'dzin dbang po'i drung du 'chi med dpal ster gyi tshe dbang / lcags
sdong ma'i tshe dbang rnams zhus/ gling smad zhabs drung rin po che phun tshogs rgyal mtshan par tshogs chos gling smad chos rar bka' gdams lha bzhi'i rjes gnang / seng
ge sgra/ sme brtsegs ljang nag /khro mo sme brtsegs/ ri khrod ma ser mo/ dzam ser nag /rnam 'joms rnams kyi rjes gnang / kye rdor gyi dbang rdul tshon la brten pa/ mkhan
chen ngag dbang don grub las kun rig gi dbang / 'byung 'dul dang / lha mo nam mkha'i gos can ma'i rjes gnang dang bcas pa zhus/ me rag slob dpon padma phrin las dbang
phyug par sgra mi snyan pa'i tshe dbang 'bri lugs/ dkon mchog spyi 'dus kyi khrid lung bcas/ gtum mo'i khrid/ tshe dbang lcags kyi pho brang / bka' thang gi lung bcas zhus/
rang lo nyer lnga'i dus dol mda' chos 'khor gnas kyi dgon par rab 'byams smra ba phyogs las rnam rgyal gyi drung du zhag nyi shu rtsa 'dren gyi bar du mdo skor pusti grags
chen bco brgyad sogs shin tu dkon pa'i lung gi rigs mang po zhus/ sngo gtso gyur gyi zhabs tog ha las par byung / smra

dbang phyogs las rnam rgyal 'di nyid la snga phyir 'jam dbyangs gang blo ma'i rjes gnang / beg tse lcam sring gi rjes gnang / tshe dpag med sprul sku'i rjes gnang gser chos/
dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed sogs rjes gnang shin tu dkon pa mang po dang / lung rgyun dkon pa rnams thugs khur che bzhes kyis srubs bar thams cad du rmor dang ra ba smad
sogs su'ang pheb nas stsal bas bka' drin che bar 'khums/ gong dkar chos sder slob dpon don grub chos gling pa bstan pa rgya mtshor dus 'khor 'grel chen bu ston rin po che'i
gsung mchan dang bcas pa/ khro phu ba'i man ngag brgya rtsa/ dus 'khor mngon dkyil chos rje bla mas mdzad pa sogs zhus/ de ltar rang lo so bdun yan chad du gong smos
ltar rje bla ma'i zhabs drung du chos dang zang zing gis bskyangs te dga' bde'i dpal la spyod pa'i skabs so/ /skabs 'dir 'di 'dra zhig thon te/ dam pa'i zhabs pad yun du
bsten pa'i mthus/ /dam pa'i spyod tshul shugs 'byung tshul du shes/ /dam pa min rnams phrag dog gis myos kyang / /dam pa rnams ni gting nas khrel ba'i rgyu/ /sngon nas dpal
ldan ngor pa'i bstan zhugs kyang / /sngon gyi las 'phros tshar pa chos rje'i lugs/ /sngon chad gzhan gyis ma rnyed snyan brgyud rnams/ /sngon du gyur 'di gzhan la smon
ma dgos/ /tshe rabs du mar bskyangs pa'i 'dren pa mchog /rdo rje 'chang dbang tshar pa chos kyi rje'i/ /snyan brgyud zab mos bdag rgyud yongs gang ba/ /deng sang dus na
kho bo min pa su/ /'ga' zhig 'di yis

'di 'dra mi 'ong zhes/ /'phya dmod 'thing slad byed pa 'ga' mthong mod/ /de dag rang gi de nyid ngom bzhin du/ /'jig rten pha rol gzigs mor gshegs te thal/ /de'ang rang gi
skyon rnams sbed gang thub dang / yon tan rnams ngom gang thub byed pa blun rmongs kun gyi phyag len du gda' na'ang / bdag la ni yon tan ngom par 'dod kyang bsam mno btang
na ngom rgyu 'ang mi 'dug /'on kyang grwa tshang du lo bcu gsum song kyang sgrig dang gang mthun las zhog pa gcig gi tshogs kyang gcog ma myong / grwa pa bgres pa lta ci/
tha na chab hril ba tshun la 'khrugs pa byed pa lta ci smos/ mig log tsam yang byed ma myong ba de dus kyi rgyus yod thams cad kyi thugs la mnga' ba de yin/ khyad par
gsang phu'i grwa tshang gzhan rnams byams pa yod/ rang ngos la de 'dra bsam pa yod kyang mi tsho ga 'dra bsam yod ni ci shes/ gang ltar de yan chad thos bsam byas tshul phran
bu gang yod sprug sprug gsig gsig byas nas bkod pa'i skabs so/ /de nas 'chad nyan gyi ming btags rang gi dpag tshod byas tshul 'god rin chog pa mi 'dug kyang / rje bla
ma'i gsung rgyun nyams pa med pa lan skyel ba'i rim pa rnams bkod na/ rang lo so brgyad la rang gnas rmor gyi dben gnas su gcad rgya shin tu dam pa'i sgo nas bcom ldan
'das kye rdo rje'i gzhi'i bsnyen pa zla ba brgyad kyi bar 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtses mdzad pa'i bsnyen yig sor bzhag gi zhar la yum gyi gzhi bsnyen dang bcas rung ba dang
/ mjug tu kha skong zhi ba'i sbyin sreg dang / rgyas dbang drag po gsum dang bcas nyin bdun bar rgyas par byas/ mtshams g.yog blo gsal rang gis byas pas khams bde zhing

dge sbyor 'phel la so bsod pa skyid par byung / de grol bstun gra pa rnams kyis nan gyis dgos gsungs par brten/ kye rdor gyi dbang rdul tshon la brten pa rgyas par byas/ de'i
phyi lo yer pa nas dge slong ngag dbang bzang po pheb par/ 'khor lo bde mchog nag po lugs kyi dbang / nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin brlabs/ dmigs khrid rgyas pa sogs bzhed
pa dang mthun par byas/ 'di rnams chos 'chad kyi khul mi res pus mo la babs pa de byed pa'i thog ma yin/ de lo rmor rang gi gra pa rnams la mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dbang
rdul tshon la brten pa rgyas pa zhig byas/ 'di skabs dbang rdzas sogs gra 'grigs pa rang ma byung bar rdo rje brag nas g.yar po zhus/ dbang tshig rnams rje bla ma'i sku
zhabs nas 'khor 'phral gyi mgar lag ma lta bur song gshis bde thogs med pa'i byang bar byung / de'i dus rdo rje brag nas rig 'dzin chen pos thugs dam pheb pa'i chos bka'i
rigs dkon pa rnams dgos pheb 'dug par de rigs 'ong ba'i gnad dang bral ba zhig yin kyang bka' nan ma chogs par sku zhabs su bcar bar chos bka'i rigs mang bar dgos pa'i
bka' stsal ltar thog mar chags lugs tshe dpag med dkar po/ tshe sbyin yid bzhin 'khor lo/ dbyangs can ma dkar mo gsum ste dkar lha gsum gyi sgo phyes nas/ rjes gnang zur
bka'i rigs mang bar phul te rang gnas su 'byor thog gra thang nas mkhan rin po che rje dbon ngag dbang bstan 'dzin phun tshogs kyis phyag tham dang bcas 'ong dgos tshul gnang
bar bzhed pa ltar phyin/ zla gcig tsam gyi bar dmar po skor gsum gyi rjes gnang dgu/ be'u bum

gyi lung / rnam sras kyi rjes gnang lnga phrag gsum/ drag po'i rjes gnang bcas pa yongs rdzogs be'u bum pusti gnyis kyi lung sogs chos bka' mang ba sba ba sri med par phul
zhing / tshur yang chos nyid dngos ston gyi byin rlabs/ rtsa dbu ma'i nyams khrid sogs zhus/ rang ngos nas tshar chen yab sras kyi gsung rab la thos bsam byas pa'i stabs
kyis dam tshig gi spang blang ngo shes tsam yod pas shin tu mos par zhus/ kun bkras pa mi srun pa'i stabs kyis snyan phra phul bar brten/ bka' bkyon babs lci bar gnang 'dug
par lab mi mang du byung yang / spyir yang sems can thams cad pha mar shes pa dang / de'i nang nas kyang chos bka' thob pa'i bla mar mi mos pa rnam smin lci bas legs nyes
kyi bka' gnang thos pa thams cad sgra 'dzin gyi ltag lam tu btang bas 'dun ma'i yang rtser son/ gra thang nas yar zhor rje rig 'dzin chen po'i zhabs drung du nag zla'i
tshes bcu bzhi la sta gon dang / bco lnga la dngos gzhi/ bcu drug la gong ma gong chen/ bdag po chen po'i dbang dang bcas pa rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dpal dus kyi
'khor lo'i dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs par phyag len mtha' dpyod gong dkar lugs stsal/ dbang gsan par bkra shis chos sde'i dpon rin po che'ang pheb/ dbon rin po cher bdag
po chen po'i dbang gsan khyad tshes bco lnga'i tho rangs rig 'dzin chen pos mkhan po/ /bdag gi las slob zhus nas bsnyen par rdzogs par gnang / de dus dbon rin po cher rgyal
gdon zhig gi ltem gzhi babs lci ba byung ba ma dwangs pa'i mu nas chos sder pheb/ sku shin tu ltem pa byung bar 'ong dgos tshul byung

ba ltar phyin/ rang la lta ba'i gdengs med kyang bla ma'i byin rlabs kyis sku bsangs dwangs la song nas dbang dang rjes gnang lung sogs bka' gnang ltar phul/ mkha' 'gro rgya
mtsho'i cho ga grwa pa rnams la rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang cha gcig bskur/ zhag bco lnga skor bsdad/ slar rang gi bsam gtan khang bur mtshams dam par byas pa'i
tshe sbyin yid bzhin 'khor lo/ /rje btsun rig byed ma/ khro bo 'dod pa'i rgyal po bcas pa'i bsnyen pa dang / mjug tu lha mo shra ma Na'i sgo nas rmi lam brtag pa bdun phrag
gcig bgyis pas ngo mtshar ba'i brda rtags kyang 'ga' zhig byung kyang brjed de thal/ gzhan shes shes dang mthong mthong gi rigs ni ma byung bar byung zhes smras na mi
chos bla ma'i rdzun du 'gyur zhing / de rigs ni ci'ang zhu rgyu med/ de nas dgun stod thub bstan nas pha rig 'dzin chen pos bka' gnang ltar gsung ngag slob bshad smin rgyas
rgyab rten lung gi rigs de snga nas tshogs bshad rgyas par gsan cing ljags bsnyen dang snod ldan rnams la'ang lan gcig bka' drin bskyangs grub gshis sngar gsan pa rnams
bskyar ldab ma zhus shing / ma gsan pa rnams tshang mar phul/ gser dngul gyis gtsos pa'i gnang skyes dpag med stsal/ 'di lam 'bras bgyis pa'i thog ma yin/ me khyi zla
ba bcu gnyis pa'i nang du kun mkhyen rong ston chen pos zhabs pad yun ring du bcags shing / she'u grags 'phyor shes rab sogs skyes chen du mas byin gyis brlabs pa'i dben
gnas smon dga' rin chen bsam gtan gling gi 'khur len dgos tshul dang / gdan sa chen po dpal

ldan sa skya nas sngags 'chang thams cad mkhyen pa chen po'i bka' shog rin po che dang / sde srid chen mo'i bka' shog bcas pheb pa ltar lo de'i gza' tshes dge bar gdan sa chen
po nas mang ja gnang sbyin/ rdor brag nas thugs dam bka' shog mang bkol bsko 'ja' rgyas pa/ grwa mang so so nas tshan grangs bcas rgyas par byung ba ltar bla brang gi
khur len gyi khul bgyis/ de lo yar klungs bkra shis chos sde nas 'a zhwa'i rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dus pa'i sde dang bcas pas nan gyi
'ong dgos tshul pheb pa ltar snyan brgyud kyi bstan par bsams nas khas len zhus pas yar klungs su 'gro ba'i sta gon byas/ gza' tshes dge ba rang gi bsti gnas nas bskyod de
ra ba smad dgon par bsdad/ sang nyin spyi pa sogs kyis sgang stod bar skyel mar byon rim bzhin chos 'khor gnas gra phyi tshong 'dus tshogs su'ang zhabs tog bsnyen bkur
dpag med byung / mar lam khra 'brug tu chos rgyal gter bdag gling pa dang mjal/ shin tu legs so'i dbugs dbyung / bka' las/ chos sde'i nyi ma ma nub gong du 'byor pa rten
'brel legs pas brtson tsam 'gro dgos pheb pa ltar nyi ma ma nub gong du slebs/ de nas zhag gnyis song thog gtsug lag khang gi steng bla ma lha khang du 'a zhwa'i rdo rje
'dzin pa chen po kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ bka' 'gyur ba ngag dbang rab brtan/ rab 'byams pa ngag dbang bstan 'phel/ dge slong phun grags sogs ra ba
smad pa/ rab 'byams pa bsod nams rnam rgyal sogs chos 'khor gnas pa/ byang 'dren phrin las sogs tshong 'dus tshogs pa/

rtses dong 'bras spungs gling pa sogs phyogs 'dus sum cu skor dang / chos sde rang gi rdo rje slob dpon sogs gnyug mar gnas pa lnga bcu skor khyon dril brgyad cu skor la 'jigs
bral dpal ldan birWa pa'i bzhed srol dus gsum gyi bde bar gshegs pa thams cad kyi gshegs shul skal ldan smin grol gyi lam la 'khrid par byed pa'i gdams pa gsung ngag
rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams ngag slob bshad du grags pa shin tu rgyas pa snang ba gsum gyi dus gsung ngag rin po che'i zin bris gsang chen bstan pa rgyas
pa'i nyi 'od kyi gsung ngag byung tshul gyi zin bris kyi steng nas rtsa ba'i bla ma yan chad kyi rnam thar bshad pa yongs su rdzogs pa ngag thog nas phul/ dngos gzhi'i ma
dag pa'i snang ba/ nyams kyi snang ba/ dag pa'i snang ba gsum gyi khrid shin tu rgyas shing mtha' chod nges/ rgyab rten bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar ngo mtshar snang ba/
zhib mo rdo rje/ zhib mo rnam 'thag /brgyud pa so so'i rnam thar cha tshang ba bcas zhag nyi shu skor dang / de nas brgyud pa'i khyad par gnyis ldan gyi sems bskyed/ maNDal
tshom bu lnga pa la brten pa bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gi yi ge sor bzhag gi steng dang / tshar chen rin po che'i gsung rgyun zin bris steng nas slob ma rjes 'dzin phyag
len rgyas par phul/ de nyin kha ba shin tu che ba ri klungs thams cad dung dkar phyis pa lta bur babs pa snyan brgyud kyi bstan pa dar ba'i rten 'brel phun sum tshogs
par gyur/ de nas bdun phrag gcig gi bar bde ldan du bsnyen pa kha gso bum pa la brten pa slob bshad pa'i

phyag len ltar grub 'phral kye rdo rje'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dag bya dag byed ngo 'phrod pa'i sgo nas shin tu smin pa/ khyad par rdo rje slob dpon
gyi dbang gi skabs slob ma re re nas dbang stegs kyi steng du 'jog pa sogs kha'u brag rdzong pa'i bzhed pa 'khrul med dang / dbang gi mtshams sbyor yang brag phug pa dkon
mchog rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i dbang bshad dang / sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel gyis mdzad pa'i 'jigs byed kyi dbang bshad steng nas legs cha bsdus pa'i bshad pa
rgyas par byas/ sta gon gyi khyad chos phra mo rnams kyang slob bshad pa'i lugs srol 'khrul med ltar grwa pa yongs rdzogs la 'bul dgos stabs nas zhag bcu skor thogs/ dbang
grol nub nas 'khor 'das dbyer med kyi lta khrid shin tu smin pa/ sgro 'dogs gcod pa bdag chen rin po che'i 'khrul spong rab gsal la rtsa ba sbyar ba'i sa gzhung spel
nas gzabs bshad rgyas pa/ de grub nas yum gyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyi zin bris steng nas dbang bskur ba sngon du 'gro ba'i phyi
bskyed rim gyi dmigs khrid/ sgro 'dogs gcod pa tshar chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa'i phyi bskyed rim gyi rnam bshad legs bshad nyi ma'i 'od zer gyi steng nas bshad pa
shin tu rgyas shing mtha' chod pa blo thog nas byas/ de'ang rang nyid mig kha bye ma thag nas sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i sgor zhugs/ khyad par rje bla ma'i zhabs drung du gsung
ngag thog mar zhu ba'i dus ngor chen gyis mdzad pa'i bskyed rim gnad kyi zla zer dang / kun du dgos pa'i gzhung bdun blo la byang bar yod gshis gsung bshad rnams blo
la nges par byung stabs slob bshad 'chad ces dpa' dpa' mo byed pa rnams dang mi 'dra ba'i gdeng 'dra yod

mod/ phal cher ni grags pa'i rjes su 'brang zhing / 'jam mgon bla mas/ blun po'i yul du mkhas pa bas/ /spre'u 'dzin pa khyad par 'phags/ /mkhas pa lag pa stong par 'gro/ /sprel
'dzin zas dang nor gyis mchod/ /ces pa'i don thog tu babs par snang / de grol bstun rdo rje slob dpon gyi lus kyi dkyil 'khor du bdag chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i yi
ge'i steng nas phyag len mi 'khrul bar grangs bcad du byas pa bskur nas/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i khrid yig gi steng nas khrid shin tu smin pa sgro 'dogs gcod pa tshar
chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i skal bzang snying gi padma bzhad pa'i steng nas mtha' chod pa ngag thog nas btang / gzhan dbang bzhi so sor slob bshad pa'i khyad chos 'da'
kha ma/ bar do/ sgyu lus/ rmi lam/ 'od gsal bcas pa'i khrid/ de'ang bum dbang gi rmi lam yan chad 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i khrid yig sor bzhag dang / de man chad 'phror lus
pa rgyal dbang mchog gi zin bris la rje klu sgrub rgya mtsho'i khrid yig nas rgyas par blangs te smin pa/ sgro 'dogs gcod pa/ dbang chog /bsnyen pa/ rab gnas/ sbyin sreg
/dus tha ma bcas pa'i zin thun blo thog nas phul/ brda don gsal ba/ lab zab phyi nang / bir srung phyi nang / bla ma rin 'byung / tshar gsum khug pa/ brda chig brgyud/
sgrub pa lung sbyin/ gsang bcu'i rgyas gdab/ gces bsdus nas rten 'brel gyi byin rlabs/ mgon rkyang gi rjes gnang bcas tshang 'gril/ rgyab rten lung la pod ser/ pod dmar/
pod nag /slob bshad skor tshang 'gril bcas pa/ gzhan yang lam skor phyi ma brgyad kyi lung

/ gzims chung du dbon rin po che sku sger du bsam mi khyab dang / yi ge med pa'i byin rlabs bcas phul/ lam 'bras la mi gtogs pa mkha' spyod ma skor gsum gyi byin rlabs/ sgrub
thabs brgya rtsa/ rgya mtsho'i rgya gzhung dang pod gzhung gi lung / mchog mang khrod nas rigs gsum spyi/ ku ru kulle lha lnga/ kun rig /mi 'khrugs pa lha dgu/ tshe dpag
med lha dgu /bde mchog lU nag bcas pa/ gdugs dkar bcu bdun ma 'di rnams rdul tshon gyi steng nas phul/ rnam rgyal lha dgu/ rnam 'joms/ 'byung 'dul/ u tsArya/ rnam sras
rigs chen bco lnga/ dbyangs can ma/ khyung khra nag rnams kyi rjes gnang yi ge so so'i lung bcas phul zhing / grol dbang du 'chi med dpal ster gyi tshe dbang rnams rgyas
pa phul/ so so'i thugs kyi re ba yongs su khengs par byas/ spyi sger thams cad nas gser dngul/ gos dar/ ras snam sogs dpag tu med pa byung / rten brten pa thams cad dang
/ khyad par pha bla ma tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i sku brnyan thams cad dang / rdo rje 'chang gzhon nu blo gros kyi sku brnyan bcas pa snyan shal phul/ dmigs phug
gi smon lam rgyas par btab/ spyi bla brang thams cad nas chibs skyel dang bcas tshe chu 'bum pa mjal/ de nub bya sar bsdad/ da lam lam 'bras tshar gnyis pa yin zhing /
tshar pa'i bstan pa la bya ba byas pa'i thog ma yin pas thos bsam byas pa'i 'bras bu cung zad byung snyam sems shin tu spro bar byung / yar lam tshong 'dus tshogs pa dang
/ chos 'khor gnas sogs su zhabs tog rgyas par byung / de nas ra ba smad du zhag

gsum bsdad/ cho 'phrul smon lam dang thug pas mang ja/ /bzhes thug /'bul ba sne bzhag sogs dang / grwa pa re rer kha btags kyi phyag 'gyed/ tshogs gur bzo bar zhal 'degs sogs
phul/ de nas rmor pa rnams kyis lum pa lcang gseb tu thab bsu bcas rang gi bsti gnas su slebs/ de'i dbyar sos dge ldan nas a mdo khams pa sogs chos gsan mi pheb pa tshor
mkha' spyod ma'i khrid sogs bzhed pa ltar phul/ rdo rje brag tu rje rig 'dzin chen por mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dbang ras bris la brten pa dang / lam dbang sogs phul zhing
/ tshur yang 'chi med dpal ster gyi dbang brgya rtsa sogs zhus/ me glang zla ba bcu par rgyal dbang drug pa chen po blo bzang rin chen tshangs dbyangs rgya mtsho sna
dkar rtse nas chibs bskyod pa'i chibs bsu ser sbrengs zhal dkar 'bul ba sogs kyi brda 'grims bka' drin bskyangs pa'i grwa slob thams cad kyis snye thang du phyin nas rim
bzhin zhol mnga' zhabs dang lhan cig par pho brang chen por zhal dkar phyag rten 'bul ba sogs grub 'phral rang gnas su 'byor/ sa stag zla ba lnga par gdan sa chen po nas
sngags 'chang bla ma thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis dbus su chibs kha bskyod pa'i bsam yas brgyud lho kha phyogs su pheb zhor skyid gshongs ra ba smad
du pheb/ grwa slob thams cad kyis zhal mjal phyag dbang sogs zhu bar phyin/ gsang phu dbyar chos dang 'dzoms pa'i slob dpon mkhan chen kun dga' grags pa zhal mjal tsam ma
gtogs ma thub bar brten chibs bsu chibs skyel thams cad la phyin/ khrom la grub

rgyal lugs kyi tshe dbang dang / tshogs su 'jam dbyangs a ra pa tsa na'i rjes gnang dang / gong ma a mi drung gis mdzad pa'i sa skya'i rje btsun ma dang / phan bde kun 'byung
gi lung sogs kha shas stsal nas chibs kha bskyod/ shar phyogs pa'i dpon sa gshegs pa'i kun rig stong tshar grwa tshang dpon slob gsang phur pheb gshis gral dbur phyin/
byang zhu bsngo smon sogs rgyas par byas/ de nas grwa tshang gsang phur pheb/ nged kyis rang gnas su log /zla ba dgu pa nas gsang phu mchod khang dpon slob kun dga' dbang
rgyal yab sras/ 'phags bde nas dge slong phan bde rgyal mtshan dang / bka' bcu kun dga' dam chos/ grwa phyi tshogs nas dge slong dpal 'byor rgya mtsho/ ra ba smad nas shing
mang dang rnam ser bla mar pheb pa sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ rab 'byams pa sangs rgyas lhun grub/ rab 'byams pa ngag dbang / shel grong / gsang gling pa kun dga' rnam
rgyal grogs mched gsum sogs phyogs 'dus dang gnyug mar gnas pa bcas bzhi bcu skor la gsung ngag slob bshad shin tu rgyas pa rgyab rten lung dang bcas tshang ba slob bshad
pa'i phyag len dngos gtsang ba phul/ 'di skabs kyang sems bskyed kyi nyin kha bas dung mdog lta bur gyur/ rgyu dbang gi dus pha ma drin can gnyis dang / lum phreng gi
mi skya pho mo'ang shin tu mang bas zhag bco lnga skor thogs/ dbang gsum pa'i khrid tshugs pa zla ba bcu gcig par ra ba smad nas rab 'byams pa ngag dbang bstan 'phel dang
/ bka' bkra shis dpal bzang gnyis sa dbang mchog gi bka' shog bcas grwa tshang gi 'chad nyan la 'ong dgos tshul mol bar byung bas/ bdag gis chos

'jig rten gang sa nas grwa tshang gi bla ma 'ong ba med cing / shes 'dod kyang med nges/ da cha gsang sngags kyi chos gang thob 'di dag gi 'chad nyan 'dra e thub blta ba las
bstan nas mi 'ong bas dgongs khrol zhu ba las 'os med ces u tshugs kyis smras kyang / da lam 'os thor yang gzhan med pas grwa dmangs 'dod gcig ma yin gshis da lam khas
ma blangs pa'i thebs med ces nan che bar byung kyang / de dus gtan nas mi 'ong thag chod byas/ 'on kyang chos skyong 'di phrag dog che ba zhig yin pas 'di ma khrol na mi
'gab bsam/ sang nyin de kha blo gsal zhu yig dang bcas dgongs pa zhu bar btang bas/ da lam sa skya dge bshes kyis bstan pa spel ba'i dus la babs pas 'ong dgos 'dug /'dres
kyang rogs dan byed ces bka' shog dang bcas ma khrol/ grwa dmangs nas kyang rdor brag brgyud dgongs khrol zhus dogs sngon skor brgyabs nas snyan bgag zhus stabs/ rang gi
'phral phugs kyi bslab don thams cad rje bla ma dam pa dang sa khad 'gyang gshis rdor brag rang du zhus yod pa ltar mjal phyag la phyin par/ da lam dus mchod gcig po 'di'i
ring cis kyang byed dgos pheb/ de gang nas nged kyi chos 'tshol ba'i khyad 'dug pas de ring byung na dgongs khrol zhu rogs byed theb yod kyang / de skabs ga bsgyur nas
kho bos dge 'dun gyi bka' gcog mi nus pheb par brten zhu re dang bral zhing / nged kyi pha rgan de'ang gzhan las ngar ba zhig yod pa slob gnyer byas pa'i don yin pas byed
dgos gnang ba sogs rang la shes 'dod med kyang mtha' sgor mo nas 'grigs 'grigs

mang grags/ gang mi yog pa'i de'i dpe ltar khas len dgos shar/ de gang nas bla ma 'pho res sngon ma gnyis kyi skabs kyang 'os su byung mod/ de dus dus la ma babs pa dang /
rje bla ma mkhyen rab mtshan can gyis pho brang chen por dge slong 'jam grags sku zhabs su snyan bgag zhu ba gnang gshis tho phul kyang 'ong ba med/ de nas lam 'bras mjug
cung bsdus tsam byung kyang cha lag 'grigs par phul/ 'di lam 'bras 'chad thengs gsum pa yin/ de grol bstun sa stag zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i yar tshes bco lnga la ra ba smad
nas dbu hang ram pa dang / phun grags chos gnyis/ rmor pa'i dbu chos gnyer pa sogs dang nged rang gi nu bo sogs kyi rta skyel ba dang bcas nam gseng la thon pas gru khar
yang rab brtan pa'i btsun ma sogs g.yas g.yon nas 'ong mi mang tsam 'dug /gru thon nas ra ba smad kyi dbu chos gral mgo ba khams tshan mi tshan sogs dang / shar phyogs nas
sogs rta bsu ba mang ba dang bcas nyi dros thog chos grwa chen por slebs/ rten 'brel khyad nas thog mar gzims chung du dkar spro zhig 'dug cing / de nas tshogs su phyin
pa'i thog mar gzhung sa chen po'i bsko 'ja' gnang sbyin/ grwa dmangs la 'gyed bcas dang / rdo rje brag nas rje bla ma rigs 'dzin chen po'i chab shog bi brta bcas/ bsko
'ja'i gnang sbyin dgu tshan gsum/ 'dus tshogs la mang ja/ rmor pa spyi so'i mang ja 'bul ba/ dpon slob drung chen rin po che'i bsko 'ja' sogs zhag bcu skor gyi bar mang ja
'ar ma 'ur ma tshogs su 'gro nyag cig byed dgos byung / gza' tshes dge bar chos rar 'chad nyan brtsi shag thog mar btang / de la

g.yas g.yon yas mas thams cad grwa tshang gdan 'dren gyi bsnyen bkur bzhugs long med pa lta bu byung bas 'dod yon 'di kham ches pas spro sag sag byung / dbyar chos gang du
chos ra smar ba rang byed rgyu ma byung bas cung zhig blo kha khengs pa rang ni byung ma song / sngon sbyin gtong bgyis pa'i 'bras bu dang / /yas mas kyi sbyin bdag zhogs
'thabs pas/ /'dod yon gyi longs spyod 'ar ma 'ur/ /ltogs snying bcangs rnams la der rang mkho/ /de nas gsang phu'i dbyar chos bteg /nged rang gsang phu'i grwa rgan du song
gshis bla grwa thams cad 'dzoms sar zhum skrag ma dgos shing bshad pa dang rig lung sogs la 'tsher ngad ma dgos par bla gsar 'ga' zhig ltar sbugs 'thums kyi ra bar ma
tshud/ 'on kyang de lo zur sprul rin po che'i sku tshab tu me tog mchod pa'i rta hrags la 'gro dgos tshul rdor brag nas bka' pheb pa ma bzlog pas 'gro dgos shar/ yo byad
ni brel phongs med par gnang byung bas phyin/ bla ma so sos khri mtho ba'i steng du rgyan sprod gzabs 'chor dgos pa ltar bskor lam chen mor chibs hrags gang gzabs bcas zhang
g.yu brag pa'i chas su zhugs nas khri steng du sdod pa las ngag 'don gyi rigs ni tshig gcig kyang mi dgos pas ltad mo che la so bsod pa byung / smras pa/ lar 'jig rten

gar song ma shes pa zhig byung / gsang phur log pa'i dus ja zhig gis rkyen byas/ slebs nub nas nad gdos drag pa zhig gis btab pas re zhig khad nye nas sman pa 'dra la

ston pa'i sku brnyan sogs spyan drangs/ mchod pa'i bye brag dpag tu med pa dang bcas bya 'dul ba 'dzin pa'i khri'i steng nas ris su ma chad pa'i dge tshul slong brgya phrag

gyur/ tshes brgyad nas grwa tshang rnams so so'i gyes nas rang rang gi dgon gnas su pheb/ skyid gshongs su dbyar chos gnyis pa chos ra shin tu 'phel bar byung / ston chos

rdor rgyu dbang

dang / rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs khrid sogs ris su ma chad pa'i grwa pa mang dag la rgyas par phul/ rnam ser drung chen sangs rgyas bstan 'dzin/ ra ba smad drung chen kun
dga' grags pa gnyis la kye rdo rje'i lam dbang phul/ zul phur yang mkha' spyod ma'i khrid cig bya dgos byung / dbyar chos grol nas skyid gshongs su dbyar chos gnyis bar gling
stod zhabs drung rin po che kun dga' grags 'dzin sogs dwags po grwa tshang nas pheb mi dang / chos 'khor gnas pa/ deng sang ra ba smad kyi 'chad nyan las thog pa blo

shin tu che bas nA lendra nas dkyil thang g.yar po zhu ba sogs dka' ba khyad du bsad de rdor phreng gi dbang zhig byas nas bstan par phan pa gzhan dang mi 'dra ba 'ong
ba 'dug pas cis kyang byed dgos gsung ba ltar khas len zhus/ 'phreng po gzhi ba slob dpon phun tshogs bstan 'phel gshegs pa'i sku gdung zhugs 'bul la phyin pa 'khor 'phral

blo gros ye shes sogs bkra shis chos sde ba bdun/ deng sang rnam ser dpon slob kun dga' grags pa sogs rnam ser ba bdun/ bye rdzing tshogs pa bdun/ dol chos 'khor gnas pa
dgu/ dwags po grwa tshang ba dgu/ rtse thang lnga mchod pa dge slong gzhan phan/ dge ldan byang rtse ba dge slong sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ stag rtse rab

'byams sogs ser mo ba nyis brgyar nye ba dang / bdag gi pha rgan sogs skyes pho mo'i tshogs mang ba bcas la slob dpon chen po a bha yA ka ra'i bzhed srol dpal rdo rje 'phreng
ba kr-i ya sa munytsa chu bo gnyis 'dres kyi dkyil 'khor bcu phrag bzhi dang nyag ma lngas lhag pa'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dkyil chog rdor phreng
mdzes rgyan gyi steng nas mtha' chod par phul/ 'di skabs mchod g.yog deng sang grwa tshang gi dpon slob blo gsal bstan 'dzin yin pas khong thugs rab ches pas 'khrul med byung
zhing phyag len nges par yod/ nged rang gi mkhan po dpon slob sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan gyis slob dpon sogs mdzad nas chos sde'i dge slong ye shes pa sogs mang bar bsnyen
rdzogs bsgrubs/ nyin rer chos skyong ba'i sku rten pa'ang dbang gsan par yod pa dbang gral du sku pheb la khad nyin re bzhin byung / nyin gcig pheb lcogs nas spyan gzigs
'phan gdugs rgyal mtshan sogs dkyil 'khor gyi khor yug du bkram pa gnang / legs so mnyes pa'i rnam 'gyur dpag med mdzad/ ma nas chos skyong 'di gzhan dang mi 'dra ba
yod gshis gra tshang gi khur len thog ma nas phyi nang gi sgrig kun spyod rnams gnyer gtad zhus pas 'bad med du 'grub cing / nang gi zang zing gi bya byed thams cad blo

cig byung / dpon slob sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan gyi mal gro 'chad kha nas ched gtad kyis g.yar bar pheb pa'i dpon slob

rang dang bka' 'gyur ba ngag dbang rab brtan bcas la ngor chen gyi bka' 'bum pod bzhi ma'i lung yang cha tshang phul/ de'ang rje bla ma dam par snga phyi rdor phreng gsan pa
khri phrag brgal ba yod kyang rje dpon rin po che ma gtogs gzhan gnang mi su'ang byung ma song bas bka' 'bangs kyi tha shal ba bdag lta bus bgyid thub pa dga' rab yin snyam
pa'ang byung / de nas dbyar chos bteg par kye rdo rje'i dbang dang rnal 'byor ma'i khrid chag med lo lo bzhin dang / lo 'ga' rer gnyis re dgos pa'ang byung / dbyar chos

ma'i khrid byed par 'ong dgos tshul pheb pa ltar snyan brgyud kyi bstan pa la bsams nas 'ong ba'i khas len zhus/ dgun chos gnyis pa'i mjug nas yar klungs su phyin/ kun
dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan gtsor gyur gyi steng / chos 'khor gnas/ grwa phyi/ tshong 'dus/ rnam seng dpon slob dpal 'byor rgyal mtshan sogs dang / gnyug mar gnas pa brgyad
cu skor la 'khor lo bde mchog nag po lugs kyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur nas/ 'di nyid kyi byin rlabs sngon du 'gro ba'i rtsa dbu ma'i khrid/ zhal shes

mi 'khrugs pa'i dbang ras bris la brten pa dang / sambu Ti/ rdor dbyings kyi dbang rdul tshon la brten pa dbang char bcad pa/ dge tshul sum cu skor la sdom pa phog /zhag
nyi shu rtsa bdun song / de nas dpyid chos dang gnyis song nas dbyar chos la bteg /'di lo dus mchod sbyin bdag dwags po grwa tshang yin zhing rang lo zhe brgyad lcags
sbrul gyi lor dbyar chos la mkha' spyod ma'i khrid rjes gnang rigs mang ba ris med pa'i dge tshul slong mang por phul/ gzhan yang rgyu lam gyi dbang sogs mang bar byas/

nyi shu rtsa drug /dus ja gnyis kyi rtsis phul bar bal po'i kha ta bla brang nas byed rogs dang / yon lto sogs spyi sos 'ong gsung 'dug kyang / ra ma lug de 'dra byed
pa las kha gtsang rang dga' bsam byung ba zla ba gnyis kyis kyang dang dod kyis khur blangs pa'i bal po gnyis kyis zla ba phyed gnyis kyi bar du dung gshog spus legs sngar

gzabs bshad dang bcas pa dang / mjug gtor ma'i bka' bsgo'ang gsung dpangs shin tu mtho ba dang bcas/ chos skyong dngos su gtad pa lta bu'i zil che zhing byin rlabs gzhan

/ zhal 'dzum dpag med gnang 'dug par da ni bla ma 'di dang mjal ba zhig

'dug gshis shog yangs khyad nas 'du khang thog rang du bla brang nyis bcogs dgos tshul byung ba ltar kha 'don sogs mi 'gol ba 'ong 'dug kyang de kha byas chog byas nas
'di lo ar po btsugs/ blo gsal ar po'i do dam la bsdad/ nged blo ldan bcas pas dbyar chos la phyin/ tshur 'khor dus zhal ba tsam ma gtogs phal cher zin 'dug cing / brag can
sprul sku rta ra bar shog khra bkod nas gtad pa ltar bkod pa legs shing sdod spro bar byung 'dug /de nas dbyar chos grol/ zhal ba sogs kyang 'phro mthud zhabs su grub/
ston chos gnyis/ dgun chos/ dpyid chos grub nas dbyar chos bteg /'di lo sku zhabs pad dkar 'dzin pa'i zhal dkar legs 'bul la gong dkar mnga' khul rnams nyin dang por phul/
de skabs zhol sku rim khang du gter bdag gling pa dang mjal/ bka' gling shin tu smar bar byung / rtser grwa tshang gi grwa pa dge slong tshul khrims rgya mtsho lags sogs
kyi bka' gnang ltar nub dang po sta gon dang / gnyis par dngos gzhi phul ba'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du bde mchog zab don dril bu lha lnga'i dbang rgyas pa dang / dmar
po skor gsum gyi rjes gnang kha shas dang / nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs sogs grwa pa bcu gcig tsam la phul/

gser dngul gos dar sogs dpag med stsal/ dbyar chos skabs mi sna rnams dang bcas pas nyang rong pa'i phyag nas dus mchod rtsis len zhus/ hor zla lnga pa'i nang du gdan sa gong
nas gong ma chos kyi rgyal po dbus su chibs kha bskyed pas lho kha gzhung brgyud grwa tshang du spyan 'dren zhu ba'i snyan gsan lha sar phab par chos skyong gi stabs bcas
zhag gsum sdod ces zhal gyis bzhes pa ltar grwa slob thams cad kyis spyi sor dgongs pa zhus/ skyid gshongs su pheb/ bdag chen rin po che'ang dus thog la chibs kha bsgyur
bas so sa rdo khang gi thad du chibs bsu ba nyi shu tsam dang bcas rim gyis chibs kha bskyod/ zhal bzhes ltar zhag gsum bzhugs stan 'jag /spyi sger so so nas che 'byor
chung 'byor gyi 'bul ba/ gsol chas/ zur gsos/ nyin bstar gsol ston sogs rgyas par zhus/ bsam yas kyi lung pheb yin gnang bas chos bka' shin tu dogs/ khrom la grub rgyal
lugs kyi tshe dbang stsal/ sger du 'phral phugs kyi bslab don nar ma stsal/ sgrig lam skor la tshogs gtam bka' drin bskyangs/ de nas rgyal khung bar chibs skyel zhus nas
grwa slob thams cad gsang phur phyin nas dbyar chos kyi 'phros dang / zul phu'i dbyar chos kyi chos ra smar bar byung / de nas so sor gyes/ skyid gshongs su dbyar chos gnyis
par dge slong tshul khrims rgya mtsho lags pheb par dmar po skor gsum sogs rjes gnang gi rigs mang ba dang / dmar po skor gsum gyi be'u bum/ phyag drug pa'i be'u bum
gyi lung sogs rgya ma sku skye dang lhan du phul/ 'di lo dus mchod stabs ston chos mi dgos gshis rmor du bsdad cing shing rtsi sogs kyi 'phro bskyangs/ dgun chos kyi dus
rnam ser dpon slob dpal 'byor rgyal mtshan/ shing mang bla ma dam chos kun bzang / tshul khang bla ma bsod nams bzang po sogs

sum cu skor la lam 'bras slob bshad rgyab brten lung bcas smin par btang / 'di lam 'bras 'chad thengs lnga pa yin/ de nas dus mchod kyi grwa bsgrigs legs par grub/ 'di lo shel
grong gi nas bkar rgyar bcug cing dus mchod kyi 'khur kyang bla spyi mi sna thun mong nas byed par byas shing zla bo rnams ni khag sbyong che bar byung kyang nged rang
ni so bsod po byung / lo sngon ma phag lo zla ba lnga pa'i mjug tu bdag gi ma drin can ma bgres mo dgung lo brgyad cur pheb pa gshegs khar dbu sngas mgor slebs/ gsal 'debs
sogs zhus/ slar sku gdung gi zhabs phyi me mchod 'bul ba sogs kyang sbyor dngos rjes gtsang zhus/ dgongs rdzogs la grwa tshang rab brtan du spyan 'dren zhus thog rmor
pa dang rab brtan gyi btsun ma gang yod bcas pa zhabs tog sku yon sogs bla brang rang nas zhus pas sku drin bsabs par phan nam snyam ste/ ma drin can gyi drin de gzhal bar
dka' mor gda'/ de nas rang lo nga lnga pa sa byi zla ba gsum pa'i nyer bdun la dbyar chos bteg /mjug ston nas mang ja 'gyed sogs phun sum tshogs par byung / chos skyong
