chen pos kyang mang ja 'gyed bcas rgyas pa dang / ra ba smad kyi bla mar 'chad nyan gtso bor byed pa las 'gyed sogs zhal 'debs tsam las mi dgos par bca' yig ltar yin kyang
/ mang ja 'gyed sogs sprug sprug gsig gsig byed khul gyis skam 'gyed kyang dge 'dun stong phrag gnyis brgal bar dge 'dun re'i phyag tu sman kha bdun re 'bab nges phul
zhing / spyi so rang gi skam 'gyed logs su btang nas dus chen yan chad gegs med du 'grub pa'i gzhi

btsun rnams la'ang mang ja 'gyed/ chos skyong chen por gtang rag gi snyan shal rgyas par phul/ zul phur yang mang ja/ gzhung gi zhabs brtan/ dus mchod/ sku skal sogs sngar
rgyun ltar phul/ mar lam shel grong du gnyer pa grags pa dang dpal 'byor gyis kyang lha mchod phun sum tshogs par zhus/ 'di lo zla ba lnga pa'i nang du bdag gi pha drin can
de'ang dgung lo gya lnga'i steng du gshegs/ dus mchod kyi stabs nas nged rang sku gdung gi zhabs phyi sogs la 'ong ma thub kyang blo gsal gyis phyin/ dbyar chos grol ba'i
shel grong nas grwa tshang gdan 'dren zhus pa'i zhabs tog yon sogs gong mtshungs bzang nges bsgrubs/ bdag gi pha rgan 'di rgyun du gtsug tor rnam rgyal ma'i gzungs ring
tshar nyi shu rtsa gcig re dang / mtshan brjod tshar bdun re la nyung mtha' byas pa/ nA ro mkha' spyod sogs zhal 'don sgrig bcur mang po gnang ba zhig yin/ de nas skyid
gshongs su dbyar chos gnyis pa dang / ston chos snga rting kyang smar bar gtang / 'di lo yas mas phan tshun thams cad du 'brum nag mched drag gshis lho byang yas mas phan
tshun thams cad 'gro nyag cig nyin re la'ang gshin po drug bdun re'i rtsar 'gro dgos sogs rang la gdengs gang yang med pas yid 'byung bar gyur kyang / dkor nag 'di la
mi dgyes pa rang mi 'dug pas bla ma spyi'i lugs srol de bskyangs/ 'on kyang lhag bsam rnam dag gi brtse bas kun nas bslangs pas nyes pa cung zad chung ba ni los 'ong / bla
ma 'pho len gyi mtshams la slebs/

mi sna tshor rten bskul yang yang byas/ gzhung sar yang dgongs khrol zhus grub mod/ grwa pa rnams kyang 'dod yon gyi brel g.yeng stabs nas 'phral bkod ma thub par dgun chos
thug 'gor zla ba bcu pa'i nang du yar klungs bkra shis chos sde'i 'a zhwa'i rdo rje 'dzin pa sku 'brum gyis ltem pas dag zhing du gshegs pa'i thugs dam gsal 'debs rten skyel
ba dang / me mchod sogs la 'ong dgos tshul spyi so'i phyag tha ma nan che gshis dpon slob kyi dam tshig dang snyan brgyud kyi bstan pa rin po cher bsams nas khas len
zhus/ zla mjug tu yar klungs su phyin/ rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po'i sku gdung rin po cher dgyes mdzad rdo rje'i sgo nas dbang bskur ba/ gdung rin po che dkyil 'khor gyi gtso
bo dang dbyer med par mchod pa'i sprin gyi phung po dpag tu med pa dang / zhi ba las thams cad pa'i sgo nas bsreg blugs 'bul ba'i cho ga rgyas pa bstar/ gzims chung bde
ldan du sgres pa kha shas la 'khor ba dong sprug gi dbang phul/ 'dus tshogs la mang ja snyan shal/ gdung 'bul sogs gya nom pa phul/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i phyag dril
spus gtsang ba sogs stsal/ grwa pa 'brum pas rkyen pa rnams la dbang bskur lam ston sogs kyang rang gar 'gro'i gdengs med bzhin du/ pha bla ma tshar chen yab sras la gsol
ba btab nas gang smin bgyis nas zhag bdun bsdad/ chos sde'i sgres gsum dang rgyal po'i drung bcas pas re zhig chos sde'i 'khur byed dgos tshul u tshugs nan chen gnang
byung kyang khas len ma zhus/ yar lam grwa phyi tshogs dus su'ang gshin po mang por dbang bskur gsal 'debs byed dgos byung / spyir dad

zas 'dod yon gyi rigs 'di bdud kyi bslu khrid kho na las nye bar gzhigs na rang nyid 'ching ba'i thabs 'ba' zhig tu mchis mod/ gzhan nan gyis bkag nas brgya 'gugs stong gshags
kyi rtsis btang na dkon mchog gi thugs rjes shugs kyi byung ba yin snyam log 'tshor ma song ba ni byed khul yin/ de nas skyid gshongs su slebs/ bla ma'i skor 'os tho
bsdus nas brtag sgril gong thon la byed par byas/ brtag sgril phul bas thog mar nged rang la babs shing / chos skyong chen pos kyang byed dgos zhes bka' nan dang / gzugs
can rnams kyis kyang u tshugs mdzad byung mod/ da cha legs nyes ji ltar yang dus mchod gcig pu de ni gegs med du grub/ da phan tshun thams cad de kha rang brtan zhes khas
ma blangs par lag pa phyi g.yugs byas/ grwa tshang du mang ja dang 'gyed snga rting gnyis zla ba byung ngo cog gi tshes bcu bzhir dus ja'i thebs dngul srang bcu gsum phul/
grwa tshang gi khur len byas pa nas bzung 'di yan la blo bsam log pa skad cig tsam ma bgyes pas gtso bor dkon mchog gsum la ci mdzad khyed shes chig dril byas par brten
lo sngon ma cung zad bro 'tshal ba de ma gtogs rang 'khor dang bcas pa la nad med bde bar 'tsho ba dang / spyi sger thams cad du longs spyod kyang brel phongs med par byung
zhing / da cha lo bdun cur nye bar slebs kyang 'chad nyan sogs bstan pa'i bya ba dga' rab byed bzhin pa 'di ka lags pas dkon mchog la blos bkal rin kyang chog nges byung
bas bsam pa bzang ba 'di rang gal che bar gda'/ smras pa/ lar pher rgya can zhig ma

lags te/ /blo dkon mchog gsum la gtad pa'i mthus/ /don ci bsam 'bad med 'grub pa 'di/ /da bsam kyin las 'bras la yid rang ches/ /khong mkhyen mkhyen dang yong yong nga rgyal
gyi/ /tshig stong shog gi zhal po mang na yang / /don rang thog tu khrig ger slebs pa'i tshe/ /las dkar nag gi me long 'di gzigs mor che/ /de nas rtse thang sku mdun bsod
nams 'od zer la spyi mthun yin zhes zhus par bka' shog rin po che pheb 'phral khong rang gi rtsar snyan gsan 'bebs pa dang bka' shog sgrog pa bcas grwa pa gnyis phyin
par zla ba dang por 'ong zhes gsungs don ltar dus thog tu pheb/ zla ba dang po'i tshes bcu bzhi la rten mchod dpe sogs chad lhag med par rtsis phul/ nged rang gis bsam yas
shag tu spos/ dgon zhol thams cad nas pheb mi mang bar byung / chos skyong chen po spyan 'dren zhus/ sha dkar gyi ti ri sogs tshan grangs snyan dar gtang rag phul/ shin
tu dgyes pa'i bka' lung mdzod btags la tshig sgra legs pa'i tshigs bcad bris pa sogs stsal/ lus dang grib ma ltar mi 'bral bar phrin las sgrub par zhal gyis bzhes/ dpon
slob gdan sa la'ang bsko 'ja' 'bul ba gang legs zhus/ tshes bco lnga'i nyin zhol nas shar lcog pa/ bde ba can pa/ gzhal yas khang pa sogs dang / chos grwa nang gi dbu chos/
che sgres/ bla brang gi sku tshab sogs chibs skyel ba nyi shu tsam dang bcas dgon par g.yas skor gyis 'ongs nas dgon pa'i ltag chos 'khor sgang du grwa pa'ang phal cher
'dug /ja rgyug shin tu mang bar/ zhol pa'ang mang bar byung / tshan grangs slog kyang

zab par phul song / nged rang gi bsam par grwa tshang 'dir 'chad nyan sogs sa steng bgag thub tsam byung / skya ser 'di rnams kyang sngon las kyis 'brel ba yin mchis/ da dung
kun mkhyen go rams pa'i bstan pa la phan pa zhig 'ong bar shog ces yid kyis smon lam yang yang btab/ grwa pa rnams thugs 'phreng ba'i rnam par mdzad kha btags kyis g.yab
g.yugs mdzad 'dug par rta kha phyir bsgyur bar byas/ lum pa lcang gsham du rmor pa rnams kyis thab bsu bcas 'dug cing rang gnas rmor gyi dben gnas su slebs/ re zhig bar
'gol sdod byas/ skyid la so bsod pa byung / de nas rang lo nga drug pa sa glang zla ba gsum pa'i nang du 'phreng po gzhi pa grwa tshang gi dpon slob blo gros dpal 'byor
glo bur du gshegs pa'i dgongs rdzogs kyi bsngo rten skyel ba dang sbrags grwa pa gnyis gzhung sa'i bka' shog bcas de ring gza' tshes legs pa'i rten 'brel khyad 'ongs pa
yin gshis/ da lam sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i la rgyar bsams pas cis kyang 'khur len byed dgos zhes nan bskyed shin tu che ba dang / lhag tu rdor brag nas kyang byed dgos tshul
thugs dam rin po che pheb byung bar/ ma nas de 'dra'i rigs bdag rkyen lta bu yin 'dug pas bka' drin che 'dug na'ang / na so smin cing mig kyang mi gsal ba bcas ra ba smad
kyang dgongs khrol zhu dgos byung gshis grwa mang thugs mi khrel ba dang dgongs khrol zhu dgos 'dug lab par re zhig log song / blo ldan 'phral du zhu yig thems pa pakshi
lag brgyud btang kyang khong pa rnams thabs zab drags snyan bgag phul grub pas dgongs

khrol ma byung zhing / bskyar nas zhus pas phyi ma'i dus dgongs pa khrol tsam byung kyang / de thag chod 'phral yar klungs bkra shis chos sde nas blo bzang bsod nams can gnyis
gzhung sa chen po'i bka' shog spyi so'i phyag tham bcas snyan brgyud kyi bstan pa'i lar rgyar bsams pas da lam cis kyang ma 'ongs na mtshams rang du yod ces phrag skyur
ma zer byung bar/ ra ba smad gzhi ba grwa tshang sogs la gzugs bzhis ma pher stabs dgongs khrol zhu dgos byung ba sogs byas par/ 'o na yod kyi thag mi chod/ sgres gsum
la zhu dgos zhes re zhig log song / 'on kyang deng sang gi dus thabs g.yo 'phrul sna tshogs pa'i sgo nas bla ma la bka' shog zhus nas 'ong pa'i 'di tshor bsams na dar kha
gang yang phul nas mi dgos par 'bad med du nyis rim sum rim 'byung ba 'di'ang sngon bsags kyi 'phen shugs 'dra ni los yin/ nged kyi rjes su bla ma mdzad pa 'ga' zhig gis
ni bla ma sngon ma dang gang sa nas mi 'dra zhes rang nyid sngar ma grags pa'i khyad 'dod nas g.yo sgyu ngan gros byed pa'ang mthong thos byung kyang / 'jam mgon sa skya
paNDi tas/ ha cang g.yo sgyu ches drag na/ /re zhig 'grub kyang tha mar brlag /gzigs lpags bkab pa'i bong bu yang / /lo thog zos mthar gzhan gyis gsad/ /ces pa'i lung bstan
thog tu babs song / de nas mi 'gyang bar lho brag shing mang dgon du rang gi slob bu dpon slob kun dga' rdo rje gshegs pa'i zhal chems ltar grwa pa gnyis spyi so'i yi
ge bcas 'byor ba nan che gshis dam tshig dang lar rgyar bsam/ khag sbyong la ma bltas par khas len byas/ zla ba dgu

pa'i nang du rmor nas bteg sta ra ba smad du bsdad/ gzhung shag nas phal cher dang grwa pa phal cher gyi ja stir dang mjal dar bcas 'phrad par pheb/ tshogs la mang ja dang
spong 'thag gi 'gyed bcas phul/ de nas zhag bdun thog shing mang dgon du sleb/ kye rdor gyi sgo nas lam ston me mchod sogs rgyas par byas shing / grangs bcad kyis grwa pa
rnams la kye rdor rgyu dbang / mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs dang khrid/ kun rig gi dbang sogs bgyis shing / 'brum pas lnga lam du song ba mang ba'i stabs bsngo byang bag
med du byed dgos byung / grwa pa dang sbyin bdag che phra thams cad kyis mgrin gcig tu sa mtshams kyi dgon par song ba dang bcas sa skya pa'i bstan lar bsams pa'i khur len
byed dgos zhes lho brag pa'i u tshugs gtso bor gyur pa nan che gshis re zhig khas len mi byed kha med lta bu byung zhing / rang gi rogs gnyis kyis kyang re zhig khas len
byed dgos 'ong 'dra zer ba bcas zla ba bcu pa'i tshes bcu gnyis kyi nyin gza' tshes bzang po yod stabs bla brang gi rtsis len dang / de nyin sde pa mdo mkhar ba/ 'gag chos
sde ba/ sbyin bdag so so/ grwa dmangs bcas pa'i 'bul tshan bsnyen bkur dpag med dang bcas bka' gdams pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen rigs chen pos byin gyis brlabs pa'i khri
thog tu khri 'don rgyas pa/ sang nyin skya ser gyi khrom che bar grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe dbang bskur/ khyon zhag bco lnga skor bsdad/ thon dbang gi dus 'ong ba'i khas
len byas/ spyir sger thams cad nas lho zog gtsor gyur gyi zang zing gi 'bul nod dpag med dang / khyad

par bka' drin bskyangs lags dang sku mkhyen gyi tshig gi gtang rag 'ar ma 'ur ma byung / de nas rang gnas su slebs/ chos sde nas rdo rje slob dpon chos grags lags dpon g.yog
gnyis pheb/ sngar gyi u tshugs kyi 'phro mthud da lam cis kyang 'ong rogs ma byas na tshar chen rin po che'i bstan pa zhes smra ba'ang kha tsam yin 'dug pas bcu bzhi mchod
par pheb thub pa zhig cis kyang dgos 'dug cing / de'i ring yang sku tshab do chod cig pheb pa'i bla brang gi sa cha bkod chab dgos gnang bar/ thog mar kha zhe med par
mi lcogs tshul nan bskyed byas kyang khong u tshugs kyi spyan chab mdzad 'dug par bsam mno btang bas khong sgres po 'dis kyang 'di tsam mdzad pa tsam du ma zad/ sngar rang
lo bcu dgu pa'i dus chos sde mjal bar phyin skabs kyang rtags 'dra byung ba dang / bla ma dam pa rdo rje 'chang dang zhal mi gnyis pa gnyis kyi lung bstan 'dra gnang yod
cing / rang nyid kyang tshar pa chos rje'i ring lugs 'di la kha tsam min pa'i mos pa gting nas yod pa sogs rgyu du mas bskul zhing / rang gi rogs gnyis la rgyu mtshan
byas par yang da cha sku na dang bcas 'di khar sku mtshams 'dra gnang nas bzhugs na dga' ba 'dug kyang / cis kyang gnang na de kha las 'os med pas/ de ltar na bla brang gi
sa cha'i kha 'dzin mi dgos par phog blang chog par byung na de kha mi gnang kha med yin pas de kha'i dan 'khyol byung na zla ba bcu gcig pa tsam la 'ong / de 'dra'i spyi
tham ma byung phyin da lam khas blangs kyang mi 'ong zhes tshig dan byas log /de nas dge slong blo shes dpon g.yog gnyis byon/ sngar ltar klad pa nyes pa mthar

phog la dan kha 'khyol ba'i nges byung nas tshes bcu dgu tshun la 'ong ba'i dan kha byas/ de 'phral spyi tham bang phyen bcas byung stabs phyi ma lo nag tu song gshis nyi ldog
gi gong nas 'khod pa dgos tshul ltar tshes bcu gnyis la'ang gnas nas thon pas rmor pa/ spyi pa/ dbu chos/ sde pa/ star gdong pa'i sku tshab/ nged rang gi nu bo sogs kyis
rta skyel ba bcas ra ba smad du chos skyong chen po spyan 'dren zhus 'phral phugs kyi lung bstan mang du stsal/ de nub dol lce sde zhol du bsdad/ chos sde'i snga 'gros
pa rta pa gnyis kyang 'byor/ sang nyin snga bar bteg /bcur du gung tshigs byas/ de nub gra phyi tshor 'dus kun rar bsdad/ mkhan po 'jam dpal grags par kun rig gi dbang
dang / gur lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang byas/ grwa pa phal cher nas ja stir rgyug /mjal dar sogs byung / sang zhogs mkhan po'i sku tshab sog po ngag dbang bstan 'dzin yang bsko
'ja' gtong ba dang chibs skyel sbrags yod/ gling khar gung tshigs byas thon/ byar gyi mdar nang so dam chos rin chen yang ja bcas byung / chos sde nas dge slong blo shes
dang / gnyer pa nang so kun dga' bsod nams dpon g.yog gsum bya mdar gsol ja bcas bsu bar 'byor/ de nub bya sa lha khang du bsdad/ thab bsu dkar spro rgyas par 'dug /sger
pa bla brang nas rje drung rin po che'ang pheb/ gsung gleng bag pheb par byung / de'i sang nyin chos sder nyi dros la 'byor dgos khyad nam ma langs gong du chibs bsu
zhabs drung o sgron lags/ khe gsum chos mdzad lung rig /

ge re chos mdzad kun dga' chos kyi nyi ma/ dge slong blo shes sogs sum cu skor pheb/ rnam snang sku mdun du mjal/ de nas nam gseng la thon par byas/ grwa pa rnams rtser zhwa
mtshal mdog zhe gcig pa/ zhabs drung o sgron lags sogs sgar sbugs kha shas bcas spro sag ge phyin/ mkhar thog tu bkra shis mthong smon chos mdzad dpon g.yog gsum kyang
pheb/ ras chung phug gi mda' lha lud zhing gi steng du g.yab dkar phub pas chos sde'i thab bsu 'dug /der rta babs/ cung zhig bzhugs/ ras chung phug gi gnyer pas kyang ja
chang dkar spro tshan grangs rgyas par 'dug /bre kha ba rnams kyang zho sogs dang bcas mjal bar byung / de nas bkra shis dge mtshan du ma ldan pa'i chos grwa chen po'i 'dabs
nye bar slebs dus gzims chung mgon khang steng nas dung chen/ rgya gling / grwa dmangs rnams 'phan gdugs/ tshogs dung sogs phyag mtshan gzab sprod kyi ser sbrengs byin
chags pa shas g.yul gyi thad du slebs/ rdo rje slob dpon dge slong chos grags lags spos chags dang bcas bsu ba'i bkod pa phun sum tshogs pas bsus/ bla g.yel mthil dbang
stegs la hor 'dug byas/ skya ser thams cad la phyag dbang phul/ sman lung nas gzims chung du ma slebs par blo gsal mang thos ma stong phrag gcig song / rdo stegs la 'gro
ba'i dus snang ba ban ma bun 'di yin med pa'i phyod de ba'ang byung / thog mar gzims chung 'khor phibs su sgres pa rnams dang bcas bzhugs gral du zho dang gsol ja rgyas
par 'dug cing / de nas nyi dros thog gnyan ston mchog gi sprul pa'i zlos gar rgyal dbang

rdo rje 'chang gzhon nu blo gros yab sras kyi seng ge'i khri ga la ba der mgrin bzang gzigs lpags can gyi rnam par thar ba bzung nas the tshom med par 'dzegs/ 'dus pa'i tshogs
kyis bla ma gong ma'i gsol 'debs sngon du 'gro ba'i zhal 'don byin chags pa snang ba 'gyur nges gnang / ja mchod phun tshogs 'dod dgu ma gyer/ spyi so nas ston mo gzab
rgyas phog zhal dkar gyi dbul ba/ de thog grwa pa so so'i mjal dar btang / dge slong blo shes kyis thub pa'i dgongs pa rab tu gsal ba'i steng nas bshad pa rgyas par gnang
/ zhag 'ga' zhig gi bar du thog mar rdo rje brag nas pha rig 'dzin chen po'i chab shog /bsko 'ja'/ mang ja/ sne gzhag bcas/ lcags zam nas bsko 'ja'/ gnang skyes byams
mgon gyi gser sku/ sa chen gyi bka' 'bum sogs phon che ba/ grwa spyi tshogs mkhan rin po che/ sde pa star gdong pa/ shing mangs spyi so/ rmor spyi so sogs so so'i mang ja
tshan grangs 'ur deng nge ba byung / khri ston mang ja gnyis bkras btags re'i 'gyed bcas phul/ gtor zlog gi rdo rje slob dpon la 'ong dgos tshul ltar bsnyen pa sogs thems
gshis lag len phra rags thams cad 'phral 'phral dge slong blo shes kyis khrid nas o zob ma byas par phyin/ nyer dgu'i nyin chas zhugs byas/ gtor rtags kyang legs par byung
/ dgon pa gsar pa nas bka' 'gyur ba ngag dbang rab brtan lags kyis mang ja'i thog mthong gos tshan grangs gnang / gtor zlog grol nas yar log /slar zla ba gsum pa'i nang
du bsam yas

brgyud sger pa grub khar rje dbon rin po che dang / sde pa rgyal phrug rab 'byams pa/ rab 'byams pa ngag dbang bstan 'phel/ chos sde nas ge re che chos mdzad lags sogs bdun
gru khar pheb/ yar lam sger pa bla brang du shog gnang bar gung tshigs rgyas par stsal/ de nas chos sder 'byor pas dung rgya gling dang / grwa dmangs 'obs steng du bsu bar
pheb 'dug /'di lo bka' 'gyur ba ngag dbang rab brtan lags/ shing mang dpon slob sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje slob dpon chos grags lags/ blo shes lags sogs la mgon
pod me 'bar ma/ mkha' spyod ma'i be'u bum sogs kyi lung / bla ma lha khang du gong steng du dge slong ye shes sogs bgres pa rnams la gur gyi dbang grangs bcad dang / srung
'khor brag rdzong ma'i khrid shin tu smin pa phul/ mchog mang grol nas bsnyen gnas ma rnams kyis dbang gzhi stegs pas bla g.yel mthil du khrom shin tu che bar grub rgyal
lugs kyi tshe dbang zhis byas/ de dus nam mkha' la 'ja' gur ya mtshan pa chos sde rang gi thog tu 'dug ces gleng / rang nyid tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen po la mos pa
dpag med yod pa'i steng du/ de snga 'ong dus nas grwa pa sgres pa thams cad zhal ras lha khang du tshar chen bla ma'i rtogs brjod cig byung na zhes yang yang gsungs par
yod pa de sems la bzhag nas/ 'di lo dge slong kun dga' rgya mtsho/ nang so kun dga' bsod nams/ dge slong tshul khrims rgya mtsho/ phrin las rgya mtsho/ ngag dbang blo mchog
bcas chos sde nang gi bris pa lnga/ zhol nas nang so blo bzang yar

skyes bcas drug la za yon tshon sogs kyi rtsis zhib par chos mdzad lung rigs sogs kyis brgyabs nas khyon nas khal phyed sum brgya thob 'dug gsung bar/ des na phyag bris kyang
rung bar mdzad rogs mdzod zhus nas khal sum brgya rang sprod/ zla ba dgu pa tshun la grub par byas/ sngar rgyan drug /mchog gnyis/ mkhan slob chos gsum sogs hal tshon
yod par ar chog phul/ nub ngos kyi skya la ston pa bde bar gshegs pa la rgyan drug /mchog gnyis/ mkhan slob chos gsum/ rje btsun gong ma lnga/ rnam sras snyan grags sgrub
sogs tshon tshogs gzabs bris/ thub pa'i dbang po'i sku sha grang gser bcas 'di lo grub/ pra rtsi'ang bla brang nas phul/ de nas sger par mar lam zhag nyi shu skor bsdad/
sgrub thabs brgya rtsa/ rgya mtsho/ tshe dpag med lha dgu/ mi 'khrugs pa lha dgu/ kun rig sogs dbang lung rjes gnang mang bar phul/ de nas grwa phyi smin gling du chos rgyal
gter bdag gling pa mjal bar phyin/ shin tu dgyes pa'i bdag rkyen che bar gnang / grwa pa mngon shes kyi gter ma'i dzam dmar gyi rjes gnang / de skor gyi lung bcas bka'
drin bskyangs/ slar bde mchog mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho dang / bong zhal can sogs chos bka' mang tsam cis kyang zhu dgos 'dug pas thugs la gzhug dgos zhes bka' gnang / gnang
sbyin kyang dpe med 'dug /de nub mgar rtsar bskad/ de nas rang gnas su 'byor/ re zhig khams bsos/ de nas ra ba smad du sku rten pas gnas bcu gsar bzhengs gnang bar gzungs
'bul la phyin/ zhag gsum 'gor/ chos skyong thog 'bebs su pheb/ dgyes pa'i lung bstan mang po gnas/ rdo stegs mgor skyel bar pheb/ 'di lo shing mang dgon pa'i tshogs dung
la sprul sku zangs

bzo ba bos/ dung gshog dngul srang nyi shu rtsa gnyis las grub pa'i 'bul sogs legs pa cha/ dung g.yog gnyis la zhor du rag gshog bskyon/ shing mang grwa pa rnams kyis tshogs
dung 'di gshog pa bzhes kyin med zer 'dug kyang / bzhes drag song / dung gos kyang gos bzang bsgrigs/ dung mjug tu gos chen gyi rgyal mtshan cha bcas grub/ zla ba drug
pa'i nang lho brag tu bteg /lam zhag bdun 'gor/ 'di lo khrom shin tu che bar thon/ dbang / gtor bzlog sngar rgyun ltar byas/ gdan sa nas snyan brgyud kha skong pusti g.yar
po zhus pa'i bka' bcu kun dga' bsam 'grub kyis 'di lo snyan brgyud pusti shog grangs bdun brgya lhag pa spus dag pa glegs shing na bza' cha tshang bcas bzhengs/ zla ba
phyed gsum tsam bsdad/ tshogs dung zhal bsror bla brang nas mang ja/ gsol gro/ bkras btags kyi 'gyed/ dung dar legs pa/ spos ldong gser shog ma cha/ rag shan ma cha/ rag
gi rkang dung gzugs cha bcas phul/ dkar rgya nas legs so rigs gsum mgon po'i sku/ go khrab sogs dang / blo gsal blo ldan gnyis dpa' dar bcas gnang / rigs gsum mgon po'i sku
phar phul/ spyi so grwa dmangs sogs nas drin gsor mar srang rgya'i khal brgyar nye ba sogs dpe med byung / tshur lam khal ma nyi shu rtsa 'dren gyi skyel ma bcas zhag
dgu song / ra ba smad du mang ja rgyas par zhus/ de nas rang gnas su 'byor/ zla ba dgu pa'i nang du bsam yas rab byung pa dpon slob rnams kyis 'ong dgos tshul gnang ba ltar
khas len zhus nas gza' tshes dge bar bteg /rdo rje brag tu rig 'dzin

chen po mjal/ de nub sgrags mdar bsdad/ sang snga bar bteg /zur mkhar du dge slong kun dga' yar 'phel/ drung tsho kun dga' rgyal mtshan lags/ bka' bcu kun bzang don grub sogs
gsol ja dang bcas rta bsur pheb/ dbu rtser drung 'tsho kun rgyal lags kyi shag tu sdod sa byas/ zhag gnyis kyi bar nyer bsdogs grub pas nyer drug gi gza' tshes dge ba'i
snga dro dbu brtse'i bya 'dabs lho bla brang gi dkar phibs su shing mang dpon slob sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan sogs gnyug mar gnas pa drug cu rtsa 'dren gyi steng du rnam
ser slob dpon dpal 'byor rgyal mtshan sogs nam mdzod sgrub sde ba gsum/ rgya ma sku skye mkhyen rab kun dga' phrin las rgya mtsho sogs rgya ma ba bzhi/ dge slong blo gsal
phun tshogs sogs bye rdzing tshogs pa brgyad/ shing mang bla ma dam chos kun bzang sogs ra ba smad pa bzhi/ rin po che byams pa tshul khrims sogs rgyal gling tshogs pa bcas
khyon brgya zin tsam la 'jigs bral dpal ldan chos skyong birWa pa'i srol sa skya'i rje btsun rnams kyi nying khu gsung ngag rin po che slob bshad kyi khrid shin tu smin
pa thad so'i dbang byin rlabs rjes gnang lung sogs cha tshang zla ba gsum la bcar ba'i bar du rgyas par byas/ gong gsal slob bu rnams kyi steng du grwa byams pa gling
pa lnga/ rdo dga' ldan rnam rgyal ba gsum/ rgyal gling tshogs pa brgyad sogs la gdugs dkar lha bcu bdun ma'i dbang rdul tshon la brten pa grangs bcad du bskur/ gzhan yang
rnam sras kyi rjes gnang bco lnga/ 'jigs byed kyi dug dbang sogs so so'i bzhed pa bskangs/ be har lcog tu phrin las kyi mgon po puu tra dmar po mjal

bar phyin/ lkog gyur gyi lung bstan yid ches pa mang po stsal/ bar bar du bsrang mdo ba/ mchod rten dkar po sogs su tshe dbang byed par phyin/ gsung ngag grol nas sgra bsgyur
rgya gar du gling du skya ser gyi 'dus pa shin tu che bar dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed kyi sdom pa phab/ 'on kyang jo bo chen pos sems bskyed gnang ba'i gtam rgyud dang
'dra ba ni mi 'ong las che/ grol dbang du bar khang g.yu zhal steng du skya ser shin tu mang bar grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe dbang rgyas par byas shing / snga phyi thams cad
du dpal ldan sa skya pa'i bstan pa la bya ba byas snyam du dga' spro che bar byung / zang zing gi rnyed pa ni shin tu che/ 'di lam 'bras 'chad thengs drug pa yin/ lha khang
thams cad rgyas par mjal zhing bstan pa rgyas pa'i smon lam nan tan du btab/ de nas rab byung ba'i sgres pa mang ba'i chibs skyel dang bcas thon 'ong / khong dpon slob
zur mkhar nas phyir pheb/ de nub sgrags mdar slebs nas gnas tshang lding dpon gyi der tshe dbang dang zhi ba'i sbyin sreg sogs kyis zhag gnyis 'gor/ de nas rdo rje brag
tu pha rig 'dzin chen por mjal phyag zhus/ thugs dgyes pa'i bka' slob mang du stsal/ rim gyis rang gnas su 'byor/ re zhig ngal bsos/ de nas zla ba gnyis pa'i nang du yar
klungs su phyin/ zhag bco lnga skor bsdad/ 'di lo chos sde ba zhabs brtan 'bul ba'i khyad nas chog mang yang 'gyang gshis yar 'ong / kha skong pusti shog grangs bdun brgya
lhag pa bka' bcu kun dga' bsam grub kyis phyag bris spus gtsang ba/ glegs shing na bza' phyi nang sogs dngos gtsang ba grub/ zla ba

bzhi pa'i tshes gcig la blo ldan khrid nas lha sar thon/ shing bya 'du khang zhig ral shin tu ches pa'i mgon khang sogs grul thub med gshis e pa sprul sku lnga bos rgya bod
kyi gnas chen du ma'i sa sna/ rdo sna/ khyad par dpal ldan sa skya'i lha khang thams cad kyi sa sna/ rten 'dam dpe bral sogs dang / gzhan yang rin po che sna lnga/ sman
lnga/ 'bru lnga/ dri lnga/ dar zab sogs bsres pa'i 'jim pa byin brlabs bgyis par dpal rdo rje nag po chen po'i sku brnyan mi tshad lhag pa/ stobs 'phrog bram ze'i gzugs can
dang / dpal ldan lha mo 'dod khams dbang phyug ma'i sku brnyan mi tshad tsam bzhengs par/ thog mar 'jim pa/ bzo bo/ lag cha rnams byin gyis brlabs/ bzo bo rnams la kye
rdor gyi dbang dang / gur lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang bgyis/ ru shing mi bsad pa'i ro bsregs pa'i sdong dum las bzos/ zhabs rkang gnyis la drag shing la phur pa'i gzugs la
bod rbad gsad gsum man ngag ltar bris pa/ mi gsad kyi gri khungs ma las brdungs pa'i lcags mda' dang / thugs kar gri snying 'khor lo bcas pa/ lcags kyi rdo rje sogs tshad
ldan man ngag ltar rung bar bgyis/ mgon chen gyi thugs kar mgon pod me 'bar ma'i pusti/ mgon po'i dkyil thang gcig rnams bzhugs/ /zhabs 'og tu lingga sngags can man ngag
ltar bris pa la bstan pa'i spyi dgra mnan pa'i spel tshig sogs che phra thams cad sla bcos su ma song bar ruu nga ba lha sar ma 'gro gong du bgyis nas/ blo gsal gyis do
dam byas pas

zhag nyi shu rtsa bdun skor la sngar gyi sku gsum gyi steng du gzims chung mgon khang du gur mgon mda' tshad tsam dang / pu tra dang beg tse khru gang lhag tsam bcas legs par
grub/ nged kyis thog mar gzhung sa'i zhabs brtan/ de nas sde pa zur khang sogs so so'i thugs bzhed dang bstun pa'i dbang / rjes gnang / gdon dgrol gang la ci 'tshams bar
med du bgyis nas rang gnas su 'byor/ stong 'khor zhabs drung gi grwa sa se ra rab 'byams pa blo gros la dgyes rdor gyi dbang / mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs dang khrid/
gur zhal gyi rjes gnang sogs mang bar bgyis/ gza' tshes dge bar mgon khang la kye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dang 'brel ba'i rab gnas gnyug mar gnas pa rnams dang lhan
cig tu ngor pa'i phyag len sor bzhag rgyas pa dang / nged rang kha'u brag rdzong pa'i brgyud 'dzin 'dra yin gshis dam pa'i shog dril dang / rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug
rab brtan gyis mdzad pa'i sngags 'chang mgul rgyan/ khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba'i gsal ba'i me long steng nas slob bshad pa'i phyag len ltar thun mong ma yin pa'i zhag bdun
ma rgyas par byas/ 'di dag la gtso bor snyan brgyud 'ba' zhig la ltos dgos yod pas snyan brgyud pusti dang kha skong pusti la zhib tu dpyad/ zhal bsro'i ston mo'ang rgyas
par byung song / po Ta la nas rin chen zla ba/ mkhyen rab lags/ blo mkhar nas rnams pheb par nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs khrid sogs rgyas par phul/ zla ba bcu par
yar klungs su phyin/ gtor bzlog dang / sku mchod chen mo'i kye rdor sgrub mchod sogs

kyi rdo rje slob dpon du chag med du phyin/ chos sde'i grwa sgres rags rim la nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs dang / khrid rgyas pa dang / gzims chung mgon khang du gnas
gsar dbon rin po che sogs la brag rdzong ma'i khrid shin tu smin par phul zhing / dge slong tshul khrims rgya mtsho lags kyang yod/ zangs gri skor gsum gyi rjes gnang kyang
phul/ rang lo nga dgu pa chu 'brug lor sngar gyi 'phros zhal ras lha khang gi skya lho'i steng ltar la dbus su rigs bdag rdo ring pa chen po nas g.yas g.yon du gyes pa'i
g.yas ngos su rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pa/ g.yon ngos su rdo rje gdan pa stha bi ra sogs sku'i skyes rabs bcu gnyis rnams zhal sprod/ gtso bo rdo rje 'chang tshar
pa chos rje rigs lnga'i rnam 'gyur can che ba lnga la thugs sras re re sku mdun du yod pa sku tshe 'di'i 'khrungs rabs rgyas pa sor bzhag dang bcas pa mthong ba tsam gyis
yid 'phrog nus pa gzabs tshon/ mgon tshar pa chen po mi 'khrul ba shes phyir sku sha rnams gser/ 'khrungs rabs 'di gzur gnas kyis bltas na ya mtshan par yod/ lho nub ngos
kyi 'og tu nged rang 'khor bcas sbyin bdag gi tshul du yod pa/ lam zab lha khang ngos shar gyi skya la rdo rje 'chang gzhon nu blo gros kyi rtogs brjod/ mkhan rabs rnams
kyang zhib tu bkod pa tshon tshogs gzabs bris dang bcas pa legs par grub/ lo 'di nang du rje dbon kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sger pa rje dbon rin po che blo gsal 'jam
dbyangs phun tshogs/ khe gsum sde pa bstan 'dzin don grub sku mched/ dge slong tshul khrims rgya mtsho lags/ ge re sde

pa yab sras/ ri bo bde chen pa brgyad/ dar rgyas gling pa bzhi bcu/ jo bstan tshogs pa bcu gnyis/ ri bo chos gling pa nyi shu/ ban tshang pa gnyis/ rtses dong lnga mchod pa
lnga/ 'bras bu gling pa kha shas/ chos lam rim pa gnyis/ rdo dag rnam rgyal ba drug /bye rdzing tshogs pa bzhi/ rgya ma sku skye mkhyen rab/ phrin las rgya mtsho dang /
bka' kun rab gnyis/ gnyug mar gnas pa yongs rdzogs/ yas mas kyi skyes pho mo'i tshogs shin tu mang ba khyon lnga brgya brgal bar grub pa'i slob dpon chen po a bhA ya ka ra'i
bzhed srol dpal rdo rje phreng ba'i dkyil 'khor zhe gnyis/ slob dpon darpan a tsArya'i bzhed pa kr-i ya sa munytsa'i dge legs su byed pa'i dkyil 'khor gsum ste zhe lnga'i
ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i dkyil chog rdor phreng / mdzes rgyan gyi steng nas phyag len phra mo tshun sla chos su ma song
bar sta gon zhag gcig the ba zhag nyer lnga'i bar grub par phul zhing / bar bar du mkha' spyod ma'i khrid dang / rjes gnang mang bar phul/ gong gsal chos gsan pa rnams
la rgyal sras thogs med pa'i yi ge'i steng nas klu sgrub lugs kyi dbu ma sems bskyed du grags pa mchod pa shin tu bzang zhing gya nom pa'i sgo nas cho ga brda don 'phrod
nges zhus khul yin/ de nas mi ring bar gzims chung 'khor phebs su dbon rin po che dang / bka' 'gyur ba ngag rab lags/ dge slong tshul khrims rgya mtsho/ chos sde'i bgres
pa kha shas bcas nyi shu skor la rgyal sras rin po che'i yig cha'i steng nas byams mgon lugs sems tsam sems bskyed kyi sdom pa dngos gtsang ba phul te blo kha khengs par
byung song /

brtan mkhas kyi yon tan phun sum tshogs pa ma mchis kyang bsnyen par rdzogs nas lo bcu song zhing / phra rags kyi bcas pa rnams kyang ngo lkog med par rang zhe mi khrel tsam
yod pa nas/ nged rang gis mkhan po/ bka' 'gyur ba ngag dbang rab brtan lags kyis las slob/ ri bo chos gling pa dge slong bkra shis lags kyis gsang ston/ dge slong chos
grags lags kyis dus bsgo ba/ dge slong rin chen rgyal mtshan dang / dge slong tshul khrims rgya mtsho lags kyis kha skong gnang nas/ da lta'i dwags po grwa tshang gi bla
ma zur pa/ grwa phyi tshogs dbu mdzad kun ldan sogs sgrub khag gnyis la dge bsnyen nas bzung bsnyen rdzogs kyi bar sla chos su ma song bar pha rig 'dzin chen pos thub bstan
chos 'khor rnam par rgyal ba'i gling du gnang ba'i phyag len ltar bgyis/ chog mang nas yar lam smin grol gling du chos rgyal gter bdag gling par dpyal phag skor gsum gyi
byin rlabs lung bcas dang / lha mo rdo rje rab brtan ma'i rjes gnang rgyas par phul/ gnang skyes rgyas par stsal nas rang gnas su 'byor/ gsang phu dbyar chos dus tshogs
chen la mang ja nyis sbrel/ khri stod smad kyis dbus bla ma rnams la bsngo rten sne gzhag gzabs pa/ ra ba smad grwa tshang du grwa ja zhu bar blo ldan gyis phyin/ 'di lo
nas bzung lo bstar skabs rer mang ja bzhi nas re ma'i bar chag med zhus yod/ de nas lho brag tu bteg thon/ dbang sogs sngar 'khyud ltar byas/ mgon po gri gug dang 'dod
khams ma'i sku bris pa'i rgya zam sngon po'i phyar dar gong sa sgrog gdan gos chen gyis byas pa che legs su phul/ mdo

mkhar rdzong du sde pa g.yag rong bas shog gnang ba ltar phyin/ bkur bzos dang zhabs tog phun sum tshogs pa gnang zhing sde pa rin po che gzhan dang ma 'dra bas mkhyen pa rgyas
la byin chags par 'dug /tshe dbang sogs dgos tshul gnang ba ltar thog mar 'chi med dpal ster gyi dbang brgya tshar/ rta mgrin gsang sgrub kyi rjes gnang / sme brtsegs
dud ka'i byab khrus rjes gnang dang bcas pa/ stag lung pa'i yab chos bur sgom lugs kyi tshe dbang phul/ zhag gnyis bsdad/ mar la rta sogs kyi gnang sbyin dpag med gnang
/ dgon par spyan drangs/ mgo 'dren bka' drin bskyang dgos pa'i gnyer gtam zhus par dgyes bzhin du zhal gyis bzhes/ tha gdong gi chu tshan du 'phrod bsten la phyin/ zhag
lnga bsdad cing mdo mkhar nas sha rtsam mar sogs zur gsos gtos che ba gnang bar sngags 'chang gsang sngags bstan 'dzin pheb/ dgon par slebs nas zhag kha shas song thog mdo
mkhar sde pa zhabs drung rin po che dang / zhabs drung blo bkras lags bcas pheb par zhabs tog rgyas par zhus/ phyag rdor urtsa'i rjes gnang dgongs bzhed ltar phul/ gsung
'phros thugs nang dag pa mdo phug med pa gnang nas pheb/ zla gnyis lhag tsam 'gor zhing / bka' kun dga' bsam 'grub kyis dud sol pusti dang beg pod sogs phyag bris mdzad/
de nas nged rang rogs gnyis bcas gros mthun du da cha sa thag ring ba dang na so'i stabs bcas kha 'dzin 'jog par gros 'chams pas grwa dmangs la rgyu mtshan btang bas thog
mar grwa pa thams cad 'dod pa chig dril gyis u tshugs nyag bskyangs byung kyang /

da res phar u tshugs che bar byas pas/ ci nas zhal bzhes ma gnang phyin phyi'i lar rgya ma bor ba dang / da lam 'dir 'phral phugs la phan pa zhig dgongs dpyad kyis bsko dgos
gsungs kyang / 'di rigs legs sam/ legs na bza' smad rgu yang skyid/ nyes sam/ nyes na gri bo rang la 'bab/ ces pa'i dpe ltar lhus thengs pa rang gal che bas/ babs 'di dang
'di 'dra yod ces gleng bar/ de ltar na bsam yas rang 'phrod ngo che ba yod pas/ rab 'byams pa sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan rang la yi ge byed dgos 'dod pa mthun stabs/ nged
rang nas yi ge /spyi so nas rab 'byams pa dang rab byung spyi sor zhu yig 'bul bar mi gnyis btang / grwa pa so so nas dang nged kyi theg bka' sbyin dbang gis gong ma lnga'i
sku bzhengs pas rkyen byas grwa pa so sos 'byor pa dang bstun pas sku 'dra gnyis gsum re sogs sbyin bdag byas/ 'bur bzo ba gnyis kyis bzhengs pa'i slob bshad lugs kyi
gsung ngag nye brgyud sku 'dra nyi shu rtsa lnga/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen rigs chen po/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bkra shis/ chos rje tshul khrims byang chub/ jo mo bkra shis
tshe ring ma bcas mda' tshad lhag pa/ bla ma so so'i zhal khyim nged rang gis 'jim par bzos nas dpe bstan pas legs par byung / tshon/ pra rtsi/ gser bcas bla brang nas bgyis/
gzungs kyang khungs btsun khyad bkra shis chos sder grwa pa gnyis kyis phyin/ srog shing gzungs byin rten thams cad 'dzom par byung zhing / de bzhin gshegs pa'i ring
bsrel yang

gsum tsam bzhugs/ gzungs thams cad nged rang gi lag bdar du phul/ gnon sbyin 'khor lo'ang sgrub pa tshul bzhin bgyis pas zhabs bsdoms kyi mtha' brten pa sbyor dngos rjes gtsang
byas/ gza' tshes dge bar 'du khang gi sbugs lha khang du spyan drangs/ grwa dmangs kyis kye rdo rje mi mkhyen stabs nged rang rogs gnyis bcas pas bcom ldan 'das kye
rdo rje'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor la brten pa'i rab gnas rgyas pa phyag len dngos gtsang ba grub cing / rab ston yang rgyas par byung / gong gsal sku 'dra rnams so so'i
bzhengs tshul sogs rgyas par dkar chag zur du yod/ na bza' yang nged rang gi ras ber la gos chen gyi gong ba bcas dang / sku drin che ba rnams la gos chen gyi na bza' yang
'ong ba yod/ rgyun gyi mchod pa bla brang nas zhing dang lug sogs yod cing / grwa pa'i khrod nas kyang 'bul mi byung ba bcas dga' rab yod pas sa skya pa'i bstan pa la bya
ba phran bu byas bsam snying dga' ba'ang byung / sngar nas tshes bcur dkon mchog spyi 'dus gtong srol 'dug cing / gnas bdag tshe ring ma yin gshis bskang gso byed pas
phan snyam dkon mchog spyi 'dus kyi dbang / tshe ring ma'i rjes gnang grwa dmangs mi skya 'ga' zhig bcas par byas/ bsam yas nas bang phyin 'khor bas rab 'byams pas zhal len
dus 'khyol bcas 'dug pas rtsis sprod sogs kyang lar rgyar mi gnod khyad re zhig grwa dmangs rang la chad med du phul sngo thog nas rtsis sprad chog par byas/ 'ong khar
grwa pa rnams la tsha ra 'gyed bcas dang / gos bzang bsgrigs kyi rten khebs/ snyan dar sogs spyi gzhag kyang byas/

tshogs ha cang tshan ches na bag med du song dogs ma chad tsam las gzhan mang ngar bsgyur/ sgrig rnams skor gan 'doms tshogs gtam nan chags pa sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i lar rgyar
khur bsam byed dgos tshul dang / lhag tu gsang phu'i mar 'gyed/ rnam ser gyi grwa rgyun sogs chad med 'ong bas khur blang dgos tshul nan bskyed zhus/ 'on kyang phug
ron gsham nas a long 'byung ba'i dpe rang ni mi 'ong las che/ bka' rgya grwa dmangs bcas pas kyang mar gtso bor gyur pa'i 'bul dpangs mtho bar byung zhing / grwa btsun sbyin
bdag thams cad zhen gzhan las che ba yod stabs thugs 'phreng bar mdzad 'dug /'ong khar grwa pa so sos ja stir bcas dgon gsham du skyel bar pheb/ bgres gzhon med pa thams
cad spyan chab mi mdzad mkhan mi 'dug pas yid skyo bar byung kyang thams cad la gsung gleng zhib pa slog cha zab par phul/ rta kha bsgyur 'ong bar kha btags ras sogs
kyis g.yab mo mdzad byung ba slar 'ong ba'i rten 'brel gyis rta kha bsgyur ba gsum gyi bar du byas/ grwa pa thams cad ri sgang der dmar phung nge bzhugs 'dug /ri babs mtshams
gnyer pa bstan chos pas chibs shol dang rdzong ba ltar byung / de nub tha dkar rgyal po'i spang gshongs zhig tu bsdad/ lam zhag bcu song nas rang gnas su slebs/ zla
ba bcu gcig par yar klungs su chibs bsu dang ser sgreng rgyas pa bcas chos sder slebs/ gtor zlog gi rdo rje slob dpon du phyin/ zla ba bcu gcig pa'i nang du dbon rin po chen
kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ gsang phu gling stod zhabs drung / bzhi pa dpon slob phun tshogs skal bzang bla grwa drug /dge

slong tshul rgya ma/ rgya ma sku skye phrin las rgya mtsho/ bsam yas rab byung pa kun dga' tshul khrims/ rnam ser rab 'byams pa tshul khrims/ shing mang bla rnying dam chos
kun bzang / tsha ba dbon po sogs phyogs 'dus dang / gnyug mar gnas pa sgres grwa phal cher bcas brgyar nye ba la rnal 'byor dbang phyug 'jigs bral dpal ldan chos skyong
birWa pa'i bzhed gzhung gsung ngag rin po che slob bshad du grags pa shin tu smin pa/ snang gsum gyi skabs bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar gyi bshad pa rgyas pa ngag thog dang
/ lung yang cha tshang ba sngags lam nas brtsams dbang byin rlabs zin thun rnams kyang thad so thad sor sbyar ba'i phyag len 'khrul med pod ser/ pod dmar bcas lung cha
tshang zla ba gsum la nye bar song / 'di lam 'bras 'chad thengs bdun pa yin/ lam 'bras grol nas gling stod zhabs drung sogs mang dag la bka' gdams lha bzhi'i rjes gnang
/ so so'i khrid/ zur bka'i rigs mang bar phul/ 'di thams cad la dbon rin po che pheb yod/ nged rang gis mkhan po/ gling stod zhabs drung rin po ches las slob/ rdo rje slob
dpon chos grags lags kyis gsang ston/ blo shes kyis dus bsgo/ dge slong rin chen rgyal mtshan gyis kha skong byas nas rgya ma sku skye/ bka' byams pa bstan 'dzin/ shing
mang bla ma dam chos kun bzang / rang grwa dam chos dpal 'bar/ bshes gnyen phun tshogs bcas bsnyen rdzogs bsgrubs/ bla ma lha khang du lam 'bras brgyud pa'i kha skong du
drin chen rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub kyi sku brnyan lam 'bras brgyud pa dang sku tshad

mnyam pa/ rogs gnyis nas nged rang gi 'dra 'bags lam 'bras brgyud pa dang mnyam pa bcas par bzhugs khri/ mdun lcog /gos chen gyi 'gan sbyar/ drin chen bla ma'i sku 'drar sa
lo 'jam dpal rdo rje'i dbu zhwa 'khrul med nged rang gi 'dra 'bags la gos phrug gi sa zhu/ so sor spyi blugs/ zhal dkar chag med/ rag gi zhal stegs/ 'dzed zhal bcas cha
'grigs/ rdo rje dril bu cha 'grigs re bcas dang / mgon khang du gtor mgron las gshin dang gnod sbyin gyi sku brnyan med gshis de gnyis mi tshad ma so sor snyan dar/ brgyud
pa'i bka' bsgo rgyas pa dang / khyad par gnod sbyin gyi phyag mtshan mdung dar la bstan pa spyi sger bsrung zhing bstan dgra sgrol ba'i phrin bcol rgyas par bkod pa bcas
legs par bzhengs/ bla sku gnyis zhal ras lha khang du gdan drangs/ mchod pa'i bkod pa phun sum tshogs pa dang bcas nged rang dang sgres pa nyi shu skor gyis dpal kye rdor
la brten pa'i rab gnas rgyas pa sngon du rtogs brjod las bsdus pa ma gtogs maid pas da lam lhan du legs par byung zhing / de mthun tshogs su tshe dpag med kyi ras bris
kyi dkyil 'khor zhal phye nas/ cho ga tshar gsum/ de dang rjes 'brel gyi 'chi bslu dang brtan bzhugs rgyas par gnang / grwa dmangs la mang ja 'gyed bzang nges/ rab gnas
pa rnams dang ri mo pa drug la so sor tshan grangs bzang ba bcas lha mchod klu mchod du gyur/ sang nyin nged rang gi mchod g.yog dge slong bsod nams rin chen gyis byas/ mgon
khang du kye rdo rje'i sgo nas mgon khang rten brten pa gsar rnying thams cad la thun mong ma yin pa'i snyan brgyud zhal shes kyis kha

brgyan pas kha'u brag rdzong pa'i lugs kyi phyag len 'khrul med ltar bgyis pas sems la dga' spro thob cing phrin las sgrub snyam pa yod/ 'di lo chog mang la dus 'khor gyi sbyin
sreg bgyis pa'i bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i phyag len 'khrul med phur gdab kyi stangs stabs sogs blo gros shes rab kyis khrid nas o zob tu ma song bar byas/ dpon slob
sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan chab ma 'phrod/ shing mang bla ma brtag dril phul bar gung thang pa dam chos kun bzang thon pa bsko bzhag byas/ sngar sor lha sar zhabs brtan
skabs 'chad kha zur khang pa'i sde pa sogs mi gsod skor gyi 'khrun gcod zhu don la 'dug par nged kyi 'khris su byon pa'i 'chad ka ba nyam dma' ba yod pa 'di lo gzhungs nas
bka' stsal bcas sngar lugs ltar byas chog pheb pas des na sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i lar rgyar bsam pa'i khur len la cis kyang 'ong dgos tshul byung bar/ khyed rang rnams
snying rus bskyed pa'i bsam khur de bzhin shin tu legs shing / da dung yang sngar mus ltar mus mthud pa'i zhe rus bskyed dgos/ nged kyi phan thogs pa byung na los kyang
byed/ da cha na so mtho zhing sa thag ring ba dang dgon pa gnyis tsam gyi kha 'dzin dgos shing de 'dra'i re ba med ces smras par/ da dung 'ong chog par dgos zhes gsungs 'dug
kyang / don rang la slebs mi 'ong bsam par 'di lo lo tsA ba byed mi bka' bcu sangs rgyas bzang po can gnyis 'byor pa'i sngar mus ltar u tshugs kha zhe med par zer ba'i
ram chos sde'i grwa sgres 'ga' dang / rgya ma sku skye sogs kyis bteg u tshugs ches par brten de ltar na zla ba bzhi par lan

len du byon byas phyir slog pas/ nged chos sde nas ma 'khor gong nas rmor du slebs grub 'dug pas/ do gal dang bstan pa la zhe rus che bar 'dug snyam khas blangs/ zla ba lnga
par yang tig 'bod mi byung ba bcas tshes lnga la rang gnas nas bteg /yar lam snon la phyin/ tshe dbang sogs phul nas rim gyis phyin pas grib 'phrang thug nau'ang skyel
bar yod/ tshes dgu'i nyin dgon pa'i chu lho/ sribs ri'i mdun spang ljongs zhig tu tshogs gur phub pa'i thab bsu rgyas par 'dug /sang nyin sde pa bstan 'dzin/ dbu chos/ tsho
gsum gyi chibs bsu bcas rab brgal nyi dros la 'byor par byas pa'i ser sbreng sogs kyi srol ni mi 'dug /zla mchod 'du khang gi bad steng du grwa pa rnams rtse zhwa dang
bcas tshogs gral bsgrigs pa lta bur bzhugs/ rnga cho la sogs rol mo khrol bar 'dug /spyi sger thams cad nas khri ston 'bul ba sogs 'brog lugs kyis gzabs par byung / spang
pa spyan snga ngag dbang phrin las kyang ja 'dren par byung / rgya ma sku skye sogs dang gnyug mar gnas pa sum cu skor la grangs bcad kyis kye rdo rje'i dbang ras bris
la bsten pa sgrub mchod khang du bskur/ de rjes mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs sngon du btang ba'i nyams khrid smin pa zhag bco lnga skor byas/ grol gdong mkha' 'gro ma 'gro
ba bzang mo'i lugs dar lam gcod pa sogs kyi brtan bzhugs sha mar thud gsum sogs tshogs 'khor rgyas par phul/ zhag nyi shu skor bsdad nas dgun 'ong bar khas blangs/ chu shin
tu rgyas gshis rin chen gling gi mdun zam skor mar lam gung

thang du zur sprul rin po che mjal/ gzhis kha sne'u nang lhor tshe dbang byas/ rnam ser drung chen rin po che sogs grwa pa mang ba 'phrad par pheb/ bsnon gzhis kar zhal ngo
rnams la tshe dbang phul/ rang gnas su 'byor/ 'chad kha dgon du sman bla rgyun 'don dar so shin tu che ba 'dug kyang dmigs rten gyi pho brang sogs tshul ldan mi 'dug gshis
bstan par phan che bar bsams shing bzo bo kun gsal gyis byas pa'i pho brang gi sgrom bang rim bzhi brtsegs byas pa'i 'khrul ma/ sprel zhing sprul skus tshon rtsi bzang
ba/ rgyal srid sna bdun mchod pa'i lha mo sogs tsa ka li las zor yang khyad pho brang gi bang rim rnams su bris/ gser shog sogs rgyas par byas pa/ steng du dgram rgyu'i
dkyil thang pra rtsis mnan pa sogs gsham bcas dang / lha nga gnyis sman 'dam las grub pa/ dbus su sman mdo brgyad brgya pa'i glegs bam/ glegs shing / sku chings/ na bza'
mintra bcas/ gos dar gyi 'phan lag gsum pa phyogs rer bcu gsum re/ zur bzhir rgyal mtshan/ dbus su gdugs bcas/ gser tog lnga bcas/ phan yu lcags rkang ma rgyun du rdul dang
nyi lhags bsrung ba'i la ta sngon po'i yol ba a lung kha bshur bcas cha 'grigs bzos/ pheb mi mang ba bcas 'di lo mgron khang dang blo gsal gyi spyil bu gsar rgyag byas/
tshong 'dus tshogs mkhan po 'jam dpal grags pa pheb par sgrub thabs brgya rtsa'i rjes gnang sogs chos mang bar phul/ sbrul lo zla ba dgu pa'i nang du grwa tshang gi sde
pa don yod lags steng grib kyi snyun babs lci bar brten nged rang tshad snar

dbang zhig byed par yod skabs dge slong ngag dbang bde chen mtshan rang du pheb pa'i 'phral du 'ong dgos tshul gnang ba ltar sde pa gzhan dang mi 'dra zhing dge slong yang
rang gi slob bur song ba bcas phan thogs min ji ltar yang ma phyin pas ga la 'ong zhus/ zhogs pa nam gseng la nged blo ldan gnyis kyis yar phyin/ rnam chos pa blo gsal rtsar
gnas tshul gyi yi ge bcas slog /nor bu dge 'phel du gung tshigs byas/ shar mar zil gnon lcog tu phyin/ sku ltem babs lci ba re lta bu 'dug par 'phral du rnam 'joms kyi
byabs bkrus phul/ e ma phyi rin rgyam gyi shag tu nub mo sdod sa byas/ nyin bstar sme brtsegs kyi byabs khrus/ khyung khra/ seng ge sgra sogs kyi byab khrus nan tan zhus
pas mchog gsum gyi thugs rjes sku khams rim bder byung / zur chen yang pheb/ zhag gsum bzhugs stan 'jags/ bka' gleng smar bar byung / 'di skabs grwa tshang dngos gzhi 'bras
spungs su bzhugs kyang / rtse'i spyi bskang pa dge slong bkras sgang nas sogs dang / sad srung blo bzang dpal 'bar sogs la rnam rgyal 'joms/ khyug khra nag /sme brtsegs
dud ka dang ljang nag /khro mo sme brtsegs dang seng ge sgra sogs kyi rjes gnang / rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs dang khrid/ bkras sgang dge slong mthu stobs sogs la gsar
ma'i sgrol dkar gyi 'chi bslu/ ba ri gtor chen gyi phyag len sogs phul/ nyin rgyug la lha sar sde pa lum pa nas la tshe dbang sogs dang / ram pa khang sar du mkhyen rab
lags kyi rje btsun rdo rje chos kyi sku bzhengs par rab gnas dang / po ta lar mkha'

spyod ma'i byin rlabs dang khrid spungs kyang byas/ rtser zhag nyi shu rtsa lnga bsdad/ de nas sde pa dwangs bskyed che nges byung bas nged 'bras spungs su ma spos bar sdod
dgos tshul gnang ba ltar tshes bcu dgu'i tho rengs snga bar nas thon pa gnang / bkra shis khang gsar du nam ma langs gong du pheb/ sku khams kyang shin tu bde mus byung
bar sang nyin bsdad/ de skabs nged rang ya ma shin tu na ba byung bas mi 'ong kha med nas dgongs pa nan gyis zhus/ hu ja 'khor drug /gos dar/ gser dngul sogs gnang sbyin
dpag med stsal/ dan 'bags nas ko gzhung la 'ong / 'dzom 'phrang du gung tshigs byas/ lum pa'i rgyab tu srod 'khor la chod tsam byung / mnyan pa'ang rgyus med pa bcas lcang
gseb kyi rgyab 'dam khrod du sngo phung zhig gi steng du stan dmar bting nas bsdad par zhogs pa bltas pas tsher ma'i phung po yin 'dug /mtshan yal char pa babs/ kha ton
ma chags tsam las bza' btung gi spro bsdu ni ci'ang ma byung / mnyan pa ni chas dang mnyam du ko ba kha sbub pa'i 'og dang / sde pas mar lam bsil grib la gnang ba'i shog
gdugs che ba zhig yod pa phul/ blo ldan nged rang gi 'khris su nyal song ba char pas ma sbangs tsam byung / song zhogs rab brtan nas nu bo dang blo gsal bcas byung bas mdangs
sku bsnyel po byung yod ces shin tu blo ma bde bar byed/ de nas rang gnas su slebs/ 'phrod bsten mu mthud byas/ lhag par nu bos mgo bshal zhig byas bas 'phrod ngo che
bar byung / 'di lo bla brang rang nas spyi pa'i khur len byed dgos byung zhing chu shin tu che ba'i

ston thog bsdu thebs dang bral ba byung kyang blo gsal gyis khur blangs pa'i sgrub mchod thams cad chag med btang song kyang / stag lung cha la'i bong bu'i dpe ltar byung song
/ de nas 'phrod bsten gyis mjug mthud long med par snon nas sde pa star gdong nas dang / grwa tshang gi sde pa gnyis nas 'phral du 'ong dgos pa'i bslab don sha 'then
pags 'then byung bas gnyis ka sku yul gnyan zhing zhal ngo khu mtshan du song bas thog mar snon la phyin/ zhag gnyis las ma 'gor bar slebs 'ong tshul gyi zhu yig phul phyin
pa yin rung / sde pa chen mo thugs tsha gshis snon du bang chen gnang / lam srang nas 'ong dgos pa'i bang chen gnang bar brten shar mar phyin/ de nub nor bu sgang du bsdad/
sang nyin snga b.raphyin pas 'bras spungs su gung tshigs zin par slebs/ sde pa rin po cher bkru byabs dang / dbang / rjes gnang / lung rnams rim par nyin bstar gyis
phul/ grwa tshang gi rdo rje slob dpon pad 'dus lags dang / klu sgrub lags kyis sde par dgongs pa zhus gnang ltar gung seng la 'og gi gzims chung zur 'phyong du grwa pa
bzhi bcu skor la jo bo lugs sgrol ma nyi shu rtsa gcig gi rjes gnang lung bcas phul bas steng du sde pa'i sku zhabs su'ang tshar gcig 'bul dgos byung / de nas grwa tshang
gi grwa pa sgres pa rnams bka' bgros gnang grub pa'i rjes gnang lung sogs mang bar dgos tshul pheb par brten 'bras spungs chu ngan gshis khams bde rgyu ma byung kyang bstan
rgyun la bsam pa'i

gung tshigs grol nas kyang bkra shis kha dar gyi tshom chen du dge slong padma dbang 'dus lags/ dge slong klu sgrub lags/ dbu chos sgres pa brgya skor la/ slob dpon a bhA ya
ka ra'i bzhed srol sgrub thabs rgya mtsho rjes gnang brgya dang bzhi bcu zhe gnyis/ tho yig rin chen sgron me'i lung bcas dang / sgrub thabs brgya rtsa rjes gnang bdun
cu don dgu pod gzhung gi lung bcas/ bka' gdams lha bzhi'i rjes gnang lung bcas/ phyag rdor/ 'byung 'dul/ rnam rgyal 'joms/ gser chos seng ge sgra/ seng gdong nag po/ 'jam
dpal nag po sogs kyi rjes gnang lung bcas/ dza bhir gyi khrid lung bcas/ rgyal sras thogs med pa'i yi ge'i steng nas dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed sogs zhag lnga skor la phul/
nub mo dang gung sang sogs su dge slong o lo sogs la rgyal sras bka' 'bum gyi lung / em phyi rin rgyan sogs la zhang blon gyi rjes gnang lung bcas phul zhing / khyon
'bras spungs su zhag nyi shu rtsa bdun 'gor/ sde pa'i sku zhabs nas bla gos/ mthong gos/ stod 'gag /rngul gzan sogs rung mthun gyi gos cha tshang / gser dngul/ ja gos/ dar
sogs dpag med/ grwa pa spyi sger thams cad nas dngul sogs phon che ba/ gser/ ja/ gos chen/ stod 'gag /kha btags spus legs sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung / chibs ra steng
du klu dbang lags/ dge slong 'jam dbyangs lags/ padma rgya mtsho sogs la rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs dang shar khrid/ 'jam dkar gyi rjes gnang bcas

phul/ ja/ gos dar/ rgya'i nya lcibs kyi me tog cha sogs byung / sde pa sku khams sangs dwangs lta bur song bas dgongs khrol zhus nas log 'ong / snon gzhis dkar zhag gsum bsdad/
zhal ngo rnams la tshe rta brgya rtsa sogs phul/ blo gsal yang bsu bar 'byor/ snye thang du lcang skya pa'i bu 'das pa'i dbang bskur lam ston bsreg sbyang bgyis nas
rang gnas su slebs/ snye thang 'phags sde grwa tshang du mkhan po 'jam dbyangs grags pas kye rdor sgrub mchod gsar zhus gnang ba'i mkhan pos dbus grwa pa thams cad la ras
bris kyi dkyil 'khor du kye rdo rje'i dbang grangs bcad du phul/ kun dga' dam chos sogs grwa pa brgyad phyag len 'khrid par 'di gar pheb par ngor lugs kyi phyag len phra
rags thams cad khrid/ de nas mi 'gyang bar mkhan po gshegs pa'i dbang bskur zhugs 'bul la dgon par phyin/ kun rig gi sgo nas dbang bskur/ bsreg sbyang / lam ston zhu ba
rgyas par zhag gcig las ma 'gor/ 'di kha'i mgon khang du sngar gyi 'phros su gnod sbyin yab yum/ pu tra/ bha Ta/ srin mo rnams mi tshad tsam ru shing nas zhal bsro rab gnas
kyi bar sngar ltar spus legs grub pa mgon khang du gsar du bsgrigs/ 'di 'brug lo rang lo nga dgu pa yin/ de dag gi sngar phyir 'di gar sbyor 'jags su mgon khang du lha
brgyad kyi 'bur sku so sor na bza' kha btags che legs re/ gser rnga legs pa bzhi/ bal sbubs skyon med legs pa cha/ gos chen gyi rgyal mtshan cha re/ ras yol kha gsar

a long kha bshur cha 'grigs/ khro skyon med/ zo lag lcags shan ma skyogs/ rgya thur bcas phul bas blo gzur gnas rnams ni dgyes los yod/ de nas 'chad kar sman bla'i pho brang
gdan drangs/ spyi sger thams cad nas zhal bsro rgyas pa dang bcas zla mchod 'du khang du bsgrigs/ bskang gso ba rnams la gur lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang / trakshad kyi rjes
gnang byas/ tshe rta sogs skya ser thams cad kyi blo'i re ba bskangs/ zla ba gcig lhag par bsdad/ mar lam gung thang gzims khang shar du grwa pa rnams la gur lha brgyad
dang / zhal gyi gtor dbang byas/ zhag gcig bsdad/ de nas lha sar zhag lnga 'gor ring sde pa lum pa nas la tshe rta/ nang pa rag pa'i nang du klu dbang lags sogs thams cad
la tshe dbang dang / mgon po bar chad kun sel gyi rjes gnang / rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs/ ram pa khang gsar du'ang de mtshungs/ rab mthil par yang tshe rta dang bar chad
kun sel/ rnyed pa'ang dpag med byung / mar lam snon gzhis kar sde pa rab brtan phun tshogs gshegs pa'i bsngo rten byang bzhu bcas 'chad kar byung kyang / 'dir yang chibs
sga sogs rgyas par byung bas dge ba rdzogs byang du bsngos/ zhal ngo rnams la tshe rta sogs phul/ rang gnas su 'byor/ mdo khams sde dge ba sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ chos
grags/ skyo mda' ba bsod nams dbang phyug bcas par bde mchog sbyangs pa'i yon tan gyi dbang ras bris la brten pa/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs dang nyams

khrid/ chos nyid dngos ston gyi byin rlabs/ rtsa dbu ma'i nyams khrid smin pa/ gur lha brgyad dang gri gug lha lha'i dbang ras bris la brten pa/ rdo rje brag rdzong ma'i phyi
nang gsang ba'i khrid smin rgyas/ gong steng du rgyud smad pa'i grwa pa brgyad/ chos 'khor gnas pa bcu bcas par bde mchog lU dril gnyis ras bris la brten pa'i dbang /
bde mchog sngags btu'i byin rlabs/ chos 'khor gnas pa rab 'byams kun dga' bsam gtan sogs la dril bu rim lnga'i dbang byin rlabs khrid dang bcas pa/ sde dge ba gnyis la mi
'khrugs pa lha dgu/ tshe dpag med lha dgu /kun rigs sogs kyang byas/ lcags zam du mchog gi sprul pa'i sku cung zad sku ltem par rkyen sel 'dra 'bul ba sogs la phyin/ zhag
lnga nas 'khor/ nged rang nu bo gso rig phul phyin shes pa de'ang nad gcong dam pos zin/ dbang byin rlabs bka' bsgo sogs gang drag bgyis mod kyang cis kyang ma phan par
dus kyi chos nyid du gyur/ sreg chog ma gtogs thams cad nged rang gis bgyis/ ston gsang phu mchod khang pa blo bzang lags pheb par brag rdzong ma'i khrid/ khro bcu'i rjes
gnang smin pa rgyab rten lung bcas phul zhing / de kha'i mjug thog tu tshul khang bla ma tshul khrims phun tshogs la'ang brag rdzong ma'i khrid rgyas par byas/ kha'u bra
rdzong pa'i phyag bzhes 'khrul med/ ru mtshon rnams gsar bzos cho ga rgyas par bstar/ 'phrod bsten du sga 'dra chu tshan la phyin/ de nas zla ba

bcu par yar klungs su bteg /ra ba smad du gung tshigs byas/ lha rtser nyal/ de nas bya sar zhag gcig byas thog chos sder 'byor/ rdo rje brag nas spang leb kham pa gnyis la
bsnyen rdzogs bgyid gnang ba'i/ bka' shog phyag bris stsal ba ltar bsnyen rdzogs 'phral du bsgrubs/ tshes bco lngar chu bo ri ra mchog gi sprul pa'i sku ngag dbang blo gsal
nyi zla 'od 'bar zhing khams 'pho tshul bstan pa'i tha ma'i gsung bdag la sku'i rjes kyi bya ba sgrubs shig pa'i bka' byung tshul bzhin gzims phyag nas phyag bris zhib
'khod pheb par thugs nang dag par ma zad/ thugs 'jog che ba bcas de ka'i gnang nyin 'phral du phyin pa'i de nub tshong 'dus su bsdad/ de nas sang snga bar 'ong / ra ba smad
du slebs/ gnyan shar nang so byung ba'i sang nyin nam srod la slebs pa dgos zhes gsang ba'i khul mdzad/ sang nyi dros la thon/ gru khar blo gsal yang 'byor byung bas
slar 'phros byung bstun shog byas/ nged blo ldan gnyis bcas pas yab la'i sgang du nyi nub la slebs/ dgon chung der ja zhig bkol nas sa sribs par bsdad/ de nas tshe ring mchod
rten gyi rtsar kha ton rnams byed kyin bsdad/ de nas ngag dbang don grub sngon la btang nas nam phyed ma zin tsam la slebs par byas/ shar mar gzims chung du phyin/ de
nub gzims phyag gnyis kyis gzhan don gshegs kha'i bslab don bsnyel tho bcas zhib par gnang / sang zhogs gdung rin po cher snyan shal phyag mchod sogs phul/ re zhig gsang
sgo gnang rtsis 'dug

kyang nged rang nas de 'dra gtan nas mi 'gab tshul zhus pas/ blo ldan gyis ram bteg nas zhus song bar de gar gsan mi gnang bar thag chod/ de ga'i sang nyin nas thog mar gong
zhabs yas phyin ljags bsngo rten dpangs mtho ba sogs bsgrigs/ gsang brtol/ nyer bzhir gdung rin po che zhugs la zhen pa dang / ra ba smad grwa tshang stong rtsar 'phral
du pheb pa dang / gdung chog pa brgyad snyan gsan phul bar nyer gsum la pheb/ blo gsal yang de nyin 'byor pas 'di ga nas grwa tshang la mang ja/ gdung 'bul/ snyan dar gya
nom pa phul/ zhag gsum par gzhan phan bdud rtsi'i dgongs pa ltar kye rdo rje'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du bdun tshigs kyi cho ga rgyas par phul/ de nas nyer bzhi'i srod
la nged rang zla bo gnyis bcas pas gdung yid bzhin nor bu dgyes mdzad rdo rje dang tha mi dad par zhi ba'i bsreg blugs rgyas par phul/ zhag gsum gyi bar gdung khang la
rgyas 'debs la sogs phyag len ltar bgyis/ zhag gsum thog zhal phye nas rus bu sgrub pa sogs kyi bar sbyor dngos rjes gtsang zhus/ na bza' cha tshang / chibs pa legs pa/ stag
sgam cha/ stag 'bog gsar pa cha sogs phun sum tshogs pa gnang / de nas rmor du zhag bzhi bsdad/ slar yar klungs su phyin/ dbon rin po che/ dge slong tshul khrims rgya
mtsho/ ri bde'i grwa pa kha shas/ li thang pa ngag dbang legs bshad/ chos sde rang gi grwa bgres phal cher/ chos mdzad kun dga' chos nyid sogs don gnyer rnams la gsang ba
'dus pa'i dmar khrid/ gshed dmar lha lnga'i

dbang / rta mgrin yang gsang gi dbang / rta pod sogs yongs rdzogs kyi lung bcas phul/ 'di lo bka' ngag rab lags kyang pheb/ tshur jo bo'i chos 'byung brgya rtsa'i lung zhus/
bka' 'gyur ba lags sogs la ma Ni bka' 'bum gyi lung phul/ dbon drung / dge slong lags bcas par khrid brgya'i lung khrid/ zhen pa bzhi bral gyi nyams khrid dang / gzhan
rnams la bshad pa phul/ 'jigs byed kyi rwa khrid kyang bskyed rim yan chad song / ngag dbang legs bshad sogs la ma gcig gi gcod khrid kyang smin par byas/ 'di lo rang lo'i
skeg gi sku rim du tshogs su tshe chog rgyas pa/ de dang rjes 'brel 'chi bslu/ grwa dmangs rnams nas sgrol dkar la brten pa'i brtan bzhugs/ tshan grangs zab pa bcas ster
bar mdzad/ spong 'thag tu rung mthun gyi gos cha tshang / rta na gzhon sga bcas cha 'grigs/ tshan grangs rgyas pa/ snyan dar/ bsngo rten bzang ba bcas phul/ brgya bzhi
dang bskang gso brgya tshar/ brgya mchod sogs gang 'bungs zhus/ chog mang sbyin sreg sogs sngar 'khyud ltar byas/ chog mang grol nas rang gnas su 'byor pas sangs rgyas rgya
mtsho can la dpal mgon gyi gsang khrid smin pa dang / zhal pod phyi nang yongs rdzogs/ kha skong pu sti'i lung sogs mang bar byas/ sa ga'i tshes bco lnga la rdo rje brag
tu gnam gling sprul sku bsnyen rdzogs bzhes pa'i las slob tu phyin/ rje bla mar lam dbang phul/ rje nyid kyi yig cha'i steng nas gur lha brgyad kyi dbang zhus/ 'phreng

po zhi ba e ma phyi gsal byed dang / shel grong gsang gling e ma phyi kun bstan sogs la rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs dang khrid smin par byas/ snon gzhis khar tshe rta sogs 'bul
ba phyin/ ston sga 'dra chu tshan phyin par 'khor 'phral mal gror bteg /lkog nas chos mdzad don grub pheb pa dang / gnyug mar gnas pa'i grwa pa nyi shu skor la/ rang
gi dbang bskur ba sha stag yin gshis mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs sngon du 'gro ba'i nyams khrid zhal shes kyis brgyan pa zhag bco lnga skor la smin par phul bas phal cher
la go ba'ang dga' mo byung song / gur lha brgyad/ seng ldeng nags sgrol sogs kyi rjes gnang dang / chos khri thang du nyi ma gnyis brgyud mar khrom che bar grub rgyal lugs
kyi tshe dbang bskur/ zla ba gnyis la nye bar bsdad/ mar lam rgya ma rin chen sgang du phyin/ zhag gnyis bsdad pa'i sgrub rnying bla brang du grwa pa rnams la gnod sbyin
beg tse 'khor mang gi rjes gnang / rgya ma sku skye lags sogs grangs gcad la mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs byas/ sgrub gsar ba dang grwa tshang ba sogs kyang mang bar 'phrad
par pheb/ bka' bcu kun dga' rab brtan gyi shag tu tshe dbang grub rgyal lugs skya ser mang bar byas/ de nas gung thang gzims shar du gnod sbyin beg tse'i rjes gnang
byas/ zhag gcig bsdad/ lha sar zhag lnga 'gor zhing / nang rag klu dbang lags/ ra mthil/ lags 'or stod pa sogs kyi nang du tshe rta/ mgon po bar chad kun sel rnams dang /
mkhyen rab lags can la de steng rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs kyang byed

dgos byung / rgyal rtse lcang lo can pa'i nang tshe dbang dang lha mo rdo rje rab brtan ma'i rjes gnang rgyas par byas/ rang gnas su 'byor/ chu bo ri nas gzims mal sku 'dra
rin po che tsan 'dam las grub pa gnyis dang / dngul gdung rin po che grub pa'i gzungs 'bul rab gnas la 'ong dgos tshul pheb pa dang / gzungs 'bul rung ba dang / khyad par
dngul gdung rin po che la dri med rnam gnyis kyi srog shing 'dzugs pa'i cho ga sogs sla chos su ma song bar byas pa'i phyag len gtsang bar bgyis/ kye rdor kyi cho gar brten
pa'i rab gnas nyin gnyis ma rgyas par/ sprul sku myur du pheb pa dang bstan pa rgyas pa'i smon lam dmigs su phug pa zhus/ gtsug tor 'bar ba dang / 'jam dpal nag po'i
rjes gnang / tshe dbang sogs phul zhing / yul chos pa'i chos drung sku ltem pa'i lcags zam rtser phyin/ zhag gcig bsdad/ tshe rta'i dbang dang bka' bsgo rgyas par phul/
rtse shod thams cad nas bsnyen bkur zab rgyas gnang / mar lam ko gzhung byas rang gnas su 'byor/ sde pa lum pa nas lum par pheb par 'ong dgos tshul gnang ba ltar phyin/ zhal
ngo thams cad la tshe dbang brgya rtsa/ sde pa khrus phu nas yab sras la zhal bsnyen dus kyi rjes gnang dgos pa lhan du phul/ de nas dgun yar klungs su bteg /ngor pa'i
grwa pa mang mkhar du sdod mi dpon slob/ gro mo lung pa'i rten gsum thams cad la mchod pa dang / mang ja bcas 'byor par mgon pod kha skong pusti'i lung / gur lha bcu gnyis
ma'i rjes gnang / dmar po skor gsum gyi rjes gnang sogs bgyis/

'di lo drin can bla ma dam pa rnasas la zab pa dang rgya che'i dam chos kyi bka' drin nos pa'i thob yig 'bri ba'i mgo rmor nas tshugs pa kun dga' bsam 'grub kyis yar klungs
su rdzogs par grub/ gtor zlog dang sku mchod chen po'i rdo rje slob dpon du phyin/ rang lo re gnyis pa shing lugs zla ba dang po'i tshes nas rgyal dwags po grwa tshang gi
dpon slob ngag dbang don grub dpon slob gsum/ 'phyong rgyas ri bo bde chen pa da lta mdo mkhar chos sde'i bla ma klong yangs sogs lnga bcu skor/ len mkhar bla ma sogs dar
rgyas gling pa bcu gsum/ jo bstan tshogs kyi bla ma dbu mdzad rab 'byams pa mkhas btsun sogs bco lnga/ ri bo chos gling pa lnga bcu skor/ chos lam rim pa gsum/ rta wang
dpon slob sogs rtses thang lnga mchod pa bdun/ rgyal sar sgang ba lnga/ g.ya' bzang pa gsum/ sku zhabs grwa tshang nas dge slong klu sgrub lags/ rin chen zla ba/ dge slong
tshul khrims rgya mtsho sogs dang / sne gdong ban tshang pa gsum/ bsam yas rab byung ba bsam gtan dpal bzang sogs gsum/ lcags zam pa bstan 'dzin bzang po/ /shing mang
ba bka' bcu kun dga' bsam 'grub/ rje dpon rin po che sogs gnyug mar gnas pa yongs rdzogs/ pho brang rdzongs bzhugs sde pa rtar mdo pa dpon g.yog /ge re sde pa rnam rgyal
sogs skya ser lnga brgya nyer bar paN grub chen po a bhA ya ka ra'i bzhed srol rdo rje phreng ba dang / darpan a tsArya'i bzhed srol kr-i la sa munytsa brgyud pa'i chu bo
gcig 'dres kyi ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor chen por dbang

bskur ba sta gon the ba'i zhag bco brgyad kyi bar du dkyil 'khor zhe lnga'i dbang yongs su rdzogs pa phyag len phra rags tshun sla chos su ma song ba'i bshad pa rgyas par phul/
'di yan la phreng ba tshar bzhi song zhing / 'di khrod nas dwags po dpon slob ngag dbang don grub kyis 'dus pa mang rab la tshar gnyis gnang thub song pas bstan rgyun
la phan par byung / de dag gi snga phyi thams cad du rnam sras kyi rjes gnang bco lnga/ sgrol ma dkar sngon sogs rjes gnang zur bka' rigs kyang shin tu mang bar bgyis/
'di dag gi snga phyi thams cad dge slong tshul khrims rgya mtsho lags dang / dbon rin po che sogs la bka' gdams gzhung drug /dpag bsam 'khri shing / jo bo'i lam yig lha khang
ma sogs gsum/ rgyud bzhi dge slong lags sger du dpe chos dang / gtam brgyud rin spungs gnyis/ spyod bsdus sgron me/ thams cad la lhan du 'khrungs rabs brgya nyer lnga
pa/ mdzad pa 'khrul med me tog phreng brgyud/ mdo rtsa so thar mdo sum brgya pa ka ri ka lnga bcu pa/ chos 'byung brgya rtsa/ man ngag brgya rtsa sogs lung mang du phul/
gzims chung du grwa tshang gi grwa pa gnyis la mkha' spyod ma'i khrid kha thig tshang bar phul/ rdor phreng grol nas jo bo lugs sgrol ma nyer gcig gi rjes gnang dang /
grol dbang du bla g.yel mthil du khrom shin tu che bar grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe dbang byas nas ris su ma chad pa'i skya ser rnams so sor gyes/ de mjug jo bstan tshogs pa
bdun/ dar gling pa gcig /len mkhar dpon

slob gnyis/ rta ra mdo'i a mchod pa/ bka' kun bsam/ lcags zam pa bstan 'dzin bzang po bcas par nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i khrid smin par phul/ nged rang gis mkhan slob sbrags/
bka' ngag rab lags kyis gsang ston/ dge slong tshul khrims rgya mtsho lags/ dge slong snang byed/ dge slong blo shes rnams kyis grogs dan kha skong / dus bsgo mdzad pa'i
dge slong bsod nams rin chen sogs bsgrub khag gcig la bsnyen rdzogs byas/ sde pa o rong pa'i bla ma a mchod spyan g.yas dge slong gcig la rig byed ma/ 'dod rgyal/ 'jam dpal
nag po/ seng ge sgra rnams kyi rjes gnang / dar gling pa lnga la mgon po phyag bzhi pa lha mang gi rjes gnang / g.ya' bzang pa gsum la 'chi med dpal ster gyi tshe dbang
rnams bskur/ dge slong blo shes/ chos ldan bzang po/ nang so kun dga' bsod nams sogs rang grwa bzhi bcu skor la gzims chung 'khor phibs su rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i byin
rlabs sngon du 'gro ba'i khrid shin tu rgyas pa/ zhal shes gsum dang bcas pa zhag nyi shu skor la tshang bar phul/ de dag gi snga phyir jo bstan tshogs pa nyi shu/ dar gling
pa 'ga' zhig bcas par bla ma lha khang du sgrol ma nyer gcig jo bo lugs kyi rjes gnang dang / kha che paN chen lugs kyi sgrol ma nor sbyin ma gtso 'khor gyi rjes gnang
/ skyid sdug lam khyer gyi khrid paN chen lugs/ yang gang steng du rin bo chos gling pa sum cu tsam dang / dar gling pa/ len mkhar dpon slob/ rang grwa phyed nyis brgya
skor bcas la bla ma lha khang du phyag drug pa bka' bcu

gsum gyi rjes gnang / dmag zor ma'i rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa/ chos rgyal lha bcu gsum ma'i rjes gnang bcas phul bas thams cad dgyes pa rab kyi rtser son/ snga phyi thams
cad du dbon rin po che yod/ 'di lo pha bla ma tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i sku mchod zla ba byung ngo cog gi tshes bco lnga la dus ja chag med thebs dang / brgya
mchod kyi thebs bcas par nas spungs 'phyar ma lcags 'bo chen mo'i khal brgya tham pa phul/ chog mang gi sbyin sreg sgrub mchod sogs brel ba grub nas tshes brgyad la chos
sde nas thon/ yar lam grwa nang byams gling nam mdzod sgrub sde ba rnams kyis 'ong dgos tshul nan che bar brten sgrub sder zhag bzhi bsdad/ de bar du kye rdo rje'i rgyu
lam gnyis/ kun rig /tshe dpag med lha dgu rnams kyi dbang / nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs bcas sgrub sde pa rnams kyi steng du bye rdzing tshogs pa bco brgyad/ grwa
thang pa lnga bcas la grangs bcad du bskur/ rnam 'joms/ sme brtsegs dud ka /seng ldeng nags sgrol/ gur lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang / mjug tu 'chi med dpal ster gyi tshe dbang
rnams byas/ mar lam grwa thang gi thad du rgyal po dang / bla brang nas ja 'dren byung / de nub lha rtser bsdad/ sang nyin rdor brag gi bang phyin gnang ba ltar phyin/
sang nyin sger pa rje drung rin po che blo gsal 'jam dbyangs phun tshogs/ sha gzugs sku 'bring / grub pa dgon sku skye sogs sgrub grwa drug la dus chen sum 'dzom thog bsnyen
rdzogs gnang ba'i las slob zhus/ tshes bcu drug la rang gnas su 'byor/ blo

ldan gyis gsang phu'i lo dus kyi mang ja zhu bar phyin/ de nas snon du tshe rta sogs 'bul bar phyin nas 'khor 'phral lcags zam rtser mchod rten zhig gsos gsar bzhengs gnang
bar rab gnas dang / phyag gzims grwa pa bcas par tshe dbang phul/ gzhan yang rnam rgyal lha dgu /seng ge sgra/ seng ldeng nags sgrol/ gtsug tor 'bar ba'i rjes gnang rnams
su zhag drug 'gor/ chu bo ri'i rtser mchod rten la kye rdor la brten pa'i rab gnas nyin gang ma rgyas par byas/ de zhor grub thob chen po'i gzims spyil sgor mo'i zhig gsos
gnang bar me tog 'thor/ gzims spyil nang du 'chi med dpal ster gyi mngon rtogs tshar gcig bzlas pa dang bcas pa bgyis pas rten 'brel gyi ltas legs par byung / de nas
rang gnas su 'khor bas da lta'i spu brag bla ma se ra sde pa legs pa don grub pheb par 'khor lo bde mchog nag po pa'i dbang sngon du 'gro bas nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i khrid
dang / rje btsun rig byed ma'i chos skor bcas chos bka' mang bar phul/ ston mjug mal grol phyin/ 'di lo rjes gnang phran bu dang / chos khri thang du tshe dbang nyi ma gnyis
kyi bar du byas/ mar lam lha sar 'ong / sde pa lum pa nas sde pa bka' blon bu chung lags bcas par tshe rta brgya tshar dang / mthong gsal dang nang rag pa'i klu dbang
lags gshegs pa'i phyi rten rnal 'byor ma'i brgya thang la rab gnas sogs bgyis nas bsnol du mar zhor zhal ngo tshor tshe rta brgya rtsa sogs phul nas rang gnas su slebs/
de nas yar klungs su phyin pa'i bcu bzhi mchod pa/ gtor zlog /sku

mchod chen mo rnams kyi rdor slob la sngar rgyun ltar phyin/ chog mang sbyin sreg sngar rgyun ltar bgyis/ zhal ras lha khang du nyin bstar mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i mngon rtogs
dkyil chog sogs kyi lung bklags/ nyer bdun gyi nyin gung yol la gtsug lag khang gi steng du byad ka'i rnam par thog babs pas/ de nub nas grwa khag gcig bla ma lha khang
du gdugs dkar gyi mdos/ rdo rje slob dpon sogs nyi shu skor gyis 'du khang du khro bcu'i gtor zlog /nged rang gis mkhan chen gyi gzims chung mgon khang du zlog 'khor sgrub
pa rnams bdun gcig gi bar bgyis nas grol mnyam gyis mdos gtor 'phen pa dang zlog 'khor 'dzugs pa dus gcig tu bgyis pas bar chad zhi ba'i rtags kyang legs par byung /
de nas yar 'khor/ 'di lo dbyar mal gror phyin/ 'chad ka spun snga/ ra ba smad dpon slob blo gsal bstan 'dzin/ tshur khang bla ma tshul khrims phun tshogs/ rgya ba bzhi/ rnam
ser rab 'byams tshul khrims can bzhi/ 'chad ka rang gi grwa pa phal cher bcas brgya skor la nye bar/ lam 'bras slob bshad shin du smin pa/ smin byed kyang rdul tshon
gyi dkyil 'khor bgyis shing slob bshad pa'i phyag len 'khrul med zla ba gsum la nye ba'i bar lung dang bcas cha tshang dang / sman bla mtho brtsegs/ gnas bcu'i rjes gnang
sogs nyin re bzhin snga chos la rjes gnang re ma chag par bgyis/ gzhan kun rig gi dbang sogs kyang so so'i 'dod pa ltar chag med bgyis/ 'brog lugs kyi tshogs 'khor ston
mo yang yang zab par byung zhing / rnyed pa'ang phun sum tshogs par byung / chos khri thang du skya ser gyi khrom shin tu che

bar grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe dbang rgyas par byas/ 'di lo bkra shis chos sder/ 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi tas/ mi gang drin du mi bzo ba/ /de ni skyes bu tha shal yin/ /zhes gsungs
pa ltar grwa pa rnams la jus khag gang yang med kyang / khrel dang dam tshig la ci'ang mi sems pa'i grwa rgan 'jungs med re gnyis kyis zhabs drung o sgron sogs bslad
pas nged de gar bsdad na rang la cang mi 'ong bsams nas/ dA byin la mgo btags pa'i rme ru a mchod bos nas dpe med med kyi khas drag byed rtsis kyi gzhi bting kyang / 'jam
mgon bla mas/ lcags kyi tho bas lcags rnams 'joms shing brdung / ra las byas pa'i 'ur rdo rang la gnod/ /ces gsungs pa ltar/ dbon rin po che'ang chab gsang la dgongs pa
zhu dgos pa dang / grwa pa rnams kyang byi ba rdza mar tshud pa lta bur gyur pa'i skad cha skyel bar mkhyen brtse nyi ma can gnyis byung bar/ nged rang ni jo bo chen pos/
gang la gnod pa yod pa'i sa phyogs las/ /dpag tshad brgya yi pha rol 'gro bar dga'/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar shin tu legs pas kho pa gang 'dod byed chug ces smras shing /
blo gsal la'ang de kha'i yi ge bskur ba yin kyang / lam 'bras grol bstun du chu tshan la slebs thog rdor brag nas chab nag ri bo dga' ldan pa'i mkhan po rgyal skor dpon slob
bsnyen rdzogs la pheb pas las slob tu 'phral rang du 'ong dgos tshul pheb lam shad nas 'ong / rdor brag tu'ang las grwar gyi slob dpon zhus skabs rgyu mtshan gsol bar
bla ma'i gdan sa nyams 'gro ba 'dug

gshis cis kyang zhu dgos bslab don nan ches pa dang / sde pa bka' blon bu chung lags dang / gzhan yang khe dar sogs kyis kyang zhu dgos u tshugs gnang bar lha sar phyin/ zhu
rten gong smos sde pa rnams dang / sde pa lum pa nas/ lhag par sde pa zur khang pa sku mched nas thugs khur che bzhes kyi bsdu ba gnang nas dar kha gang dang dngul zho
gang gi zhu rten yang ma dgos/ sgrub mchod dang phyag len dgongs che tshul gyi zhu tshig them pa 'bul ba gnang zhing / mgron gnyer skyid sbugs nas kyis gnang / tshar chen
yab sras kyi thugs bskyed smon lam gyi mthu las rgyal po'ang thugs yid ches shing bka' 'dri gnang ba'ang lan phul bas thugs la 'thad pa byung / lan bzhi'i bar 'bod pa gnang
bas thugs mnyes par gyur nas/ dA byin la'ang de kha'i bsed bkrol gnang / bka' shog kyang sa bon 'bul ma dgos par gtsang rgyag gnang nas sne gdong rdzong nas 'phral rang
du sprod dgos pa'i rgya ma gnang zhing / de mthun/ dA byin rang nas kyang sne gdong rdzong dpon la do khur dgos tshul gyi phyag tham gnang / lha sar 'dod yon ni bsam mi
khyab pa byung / 'di skabs dga' rab dbang phyug gi rjes 'brang kha cig nas/ deng sang gi dus rgyal bu'i drung dang dA byin gnyis dbyer med yin pas g.yul ngo mi ldog ces
gnang mi byung 'dug kyang 'phral du ldog 'phral/ blo gsal blo ldan gnyis kyis bka' shog sgrogs sar phyin/ sne gdong rdzong dpon rta ra mdo nas kyis tshogs su sgrogs pa gnang
bas gnyan yod mchod pa'i ston pa drug ltar gyur/ de nas nged rang gi rtsis len sar phyin pas yul mi rnams kyang dga' spro thob cing thams

cad blo mal du tshud par gyur/ chos sde nas ser sbreng mdzad/ der chog mang bar bsdad/ de dus rje drung lo tsA ba rmor du 'byor bas dge slong chos 'byor bang phyin la 'byor
ba ltar 'ong / chos 'khor gnas pa rab 'byams pa kun dga' bsam gtan sogs gcig gnyis dang / dge slong tshul khrims rgya mtsho lags kyang yod/ rje drung la gsang ba 'dus pa
'jam dpal rdo rje'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du/ smin byed sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas/ zhal sgrub dus/ bsnyen dus/ las spor sogs dang / khyad par gsang sgrub kyi rjes gnang
sngon du 'gro bas/ dpal mgon chen po'i tshe khrid gur khang ma dang / gsang khrid shin tu smin pa sogs mang bar byas/ gos chen/ rgya sbugs/ ting bdun tshar sogs chos
yon mang bar byung / 'di lo sa ga zla ba'i nyer gnyis rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi rtogs pa brnyes pa'i dus nas 'chi med bdud rtsi ril bu'i sgrub pa rje bla ma'i phyag len 'khrul
med ltar rung bar bgyis/ 'di'i sman gyi sbyin bdag sde pa zur khang pa/ blo mkhar nas/ ram pa khang gsar ba/ 'or stod pa/ a lag dpal sgron/ lkog nas chos mdzad don
grub rnams kyis mdzad pa'i gegs med du bsgrubs/ sbyin bdag so sor sku skal kyang rgyas par phul/ shel grong gsang sngags gling dgon par em chi kun dga' bstan 'phel gyi lam
'bras gtso bsdus kyi sku brnyan bzhengs par gzungs 'bul rab gnas la phyin/ gzungs rung bar phul zhing / kye rdor la brten pa'i rab gnas nyin gang ma/ zhi ba'i sbyin sreg
dang bcas rgyas

par bsgrubs/ de 'khor 'phral grwa phyi tshong 'dus tshogs su gtsang khang gi thog tu dbu mdzad kun ldan dang / ma chen rgyal mtshan bzang po can gyis khur 'khur ba'i gser zangs
kyi ganydzi ra che bar bzhengs pa'i gzungs rab gnas la 'ong dgos tshul ltar phyin/ gzungs sogs rung bar phul zhing / mkhan po bkra shis dpal ldan tshogs pa dang bcas
nged rang gis rdo rje slob dpon bgyis pa'i kye rdor la brten pa'i rab gnas rgyas pa gtsug lag khang gi steng du gur phub nas bgyis/ rab ston dang bsnyen bkur phun sum tshogs
pa byung / yar lam grwa thang du drung lags gshegs pa'i gsal 'debs dbang bskur la phyin/ mkhan rin po che grwa pa brgya tsam dang bcas lhan du kun rig gi cho ga lho
sgo dang 'brel ba dang gsal 'debs dbang bskur gang rgyas byas nas gra'i lce bde'i phu'i kre ba'i nang du tshe rta'i dbang byas/ zhag gcig bsdad nas mar zhor rgyal gling tshogs
su rin po che byams pa tshul khrims kyi shag tu bos nas gung tshigs byas/ grwa pa ja rgyug byed mi mang bar byung / de nub lha rtser bsdad nas rang gnas su 'byor/ zla
ba lnga pa nas gling smad zhabs drung kun dga' 'byung gnas/ rnam ser drung chen ngag dbang dngos grub/ ra ba smad pa dpon slob blo gsal bstan 'dzin/ dge slong tshul khrims
rgya mtsho lags/ chos 'khor gnas rab 'byams pa kun dga' bsam gtan can gsum/ rgya ma sku skye lags sogs gsum/ shing mang ba bka' bcu kun dga' bsam 'grub/ bsam yas rab
byung pa mthu stobs rgya mtsho lags sogs drug /rnam ser rab 'byams pa tshul khrims dang / dbu mdzad

ngag dbang dar rgyas/ bye rdzing tshogs pa kun bzang rdo rje dang / dge slong bstan pa/ zhi ba dge slong rnam rgyal/ ngag dbang phun tshogs sogs lnga/ gnyug mar gnas pa yongs
rdzogs/ snye thang brag sna ba kha shas/ sgrub sde pa bdun/ ra ba smad pa gsum bcas khyon bdun cu rtsa 'dren skor la gsung ngag slob bshad shin tu smin pa so so'i byin
rlabs smin byed thad sor sbyar ba rnal 'byor ma'i shar khrid byin rlabs bcas phul/ dge slong tshul rgya ma lags kyis sil snyan legs pa sogs so so nas chos yon rgyas par
byung / de ka'i zla ba drug pa'i mjug nas mi bde ba'i mgo tshugs dpung 'degs kyi brda 'grims sogs zing long shin tu che ba'i ngang nas sbyong mkhar ba zla ba bcu pa'i nang
du lha sar 'byor/ bcu gcig pa'i tshes gcig la po Ta la dang / gnyis la lha sa rtsis blangs/ rgyal po bkrongs/ kho pa tshos khrom gzigs khang bzung / de nas so so'i lha
sde mi sde thams cad 'phral du mjal khar 'ong dgos pa'i brda 'grims byung ba ltar re zhig mjal khar blo gsal dge slong lags bcas pheb par gang yin med pa'i rgya mtshor rdo
bskyur lta bu 'dug zer bas re zhig ma phyin/ bcu gcig pa'i nyi shu gsum la nged rang dge slong blo ldan bcas kyi dpon khag lnga so sor mjal/ snga sor rgyal po'i dus grwa
tshang khag rnying grwa bcas la las sbyor tsha drag dgos pa'i bka' shog bkram/ bsde bas su bkra shis chos sder yang tsha nan gyi bka' shog byung bar rang rer de 'dra'i
lag len med par ma zad/ shes kyang mi 'gab pas bka'

'gyur dang bskang gso sogs byas pa 'gab ces rmor nas yi ge bskur ba bka' shog rnams rtsad gcod dam par 'dug gshis sngon rgyu mtshan btang na dga' bsam so sor rgyu mtshan byas
par gang yang mi 'ong / da nas de 'dra'i rigs ma byed tsam las legs nyes ma byung / bka' shog tu chos 'phel dmigs bsal yod stabs chos 'phel nas bka' shog ngo bo dang mi
do chod 'ong dgos tshul byung bar 'phral du btang ba'i ge re chos mdzad lags gnyer par song gshis pheb byung / skor yang mang du byas mthar tshes bcu'i zhogs pa nged rang
sog por rtsis sprad pa'i 'dzin 'chags byas shing gnyer pa'ang mnyam du zin par chu chags yang yang brgyabs song kyang tshig kha ma thal gshis re zhig sog po rer rtsis
sprad pa'i dam rtsi che bar byung / blo gsal rmor du yod pa'ang 'phral du lha sar slebs/ thams cad nas sku rim smar ba dang / mkhyen rab/ blo mkhar nas/ lags 'or stod/ chos
mdzad don grub sogs kyis kyang bsdu cha mdzad pa'i sku rim smar ba byung 'dug /blo gsal grul thub grags pa'i sde srid sku zhabs su sde pa mdo mkhar nas kyis zhu ba gnang
zhing / sog por dge slong nam mkha' rgyal mtshan gyis thabs 'khrul sna tshogs byas pa dang / pha bla ma tshar pa chen po'i chos srung rnams kyi thugs rjes dgon pa rnams
su'ang sog po'i bsun gtser med pa'i steng zla gcig zhag bzhi thog nas stag rtse sku tshab/ dge slong nam mkha' rgyal mtshan blo gsal bcas pas phying gur nang nas thon nas
slebs 'phral legs so byed mi'ang shin tu mang bar byung

zhing / sde pa lum pa nas la tshe rta brgya rtsa phul/ snga sor lha sar slebs gdong bco brgyad rje dbon rin po che dang mjal/ gsung gleng bag pheb pa byung zhing sang nyin
nas nyin re bzhin mjal dgos 'dug gnang byung kyang nged sog pos gtses pas mjal ma thub/ de nas rang gnas rmor du 'byor/ yas mas thams cad nas 'phrad mi shin tu mang bar byung
/ de nas yar klungs su bteg /ra ba smad du ja stir dang kha bcas grwa pa bgres gzhon phal cher gyis byung / sang nub chos 'khor gnas su bsdad/ legs so gnang mi shin
tu mang ba dang / tshong 'dus su nang so mjal dpal gyi nang du bsdad/ grwa pa phal cher pheb/ bgres pa rnams spyan chab kyang gnang / bka' phun tshogs grags pa sogs sgrub
sde ba'ang mang bar pheb/ shin tu dgyes pa'i legs so gnang mi mang po byung / de nas bya sar zhag gcig bsdad nas chos sder sleb/ ser sbreng chibs bsu sogs mi 'gab zhus te
re zhig par stir ja sogs gnang / 'du khang du spyi tshogs nas sgrol dkar la brten pa'i brtan bzhugs ston mo gos ber sogs 'bul ba zab rgyas dang / shing mang dpon slob dam
chos kun bzang grwa pa gnyis bcas legs so rgyas pa/ spyi so nas dge slong nam mkha' rgyal mtshan la drin gzor ston mo'i thog gos chen gyi snam sbyar gcig phul song / da
cha thog mar rme ru ba'i lag nas dgon pa blangs/ 'di lo srog dang bdos pas dgon pa nyen dang bral bar byas pas/ bstan par bya ba'ang de tsam yin/ dgongs khrol zhus par
re zhig 'khur len

dgos tshul byung kyang / zla bo gnyis nas da cha de tsam rang dga' bas dgongs pa zhu dgos tshul ltar gzhung sar zhu yig phul bas/ sde pa lum pa nas kyis kyang re zhig 'khur
len dgos tshul phyag bris nan chags gnang byung kyang / yang bskyar 'u thug gi zhu yig phul bas dgongs pa khrol/ grwa dmangs rnams la'ang de ka'i rgyu mtshan phul bas thugs
