gzur gnas rnams ni shin tu gnang 'dug /tshogs su'ang spyi dang khyad par tshar chen yab sras kyi bstan pa la thugs khur che bzhes dgos pa'i tshogs gtam rgyas par phul/
blo'ang shin tu 'khol bar byung / blo gsal yang slebs pas rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub kyi sku drin bsab phyir zla ba byung ngo cog gi gnam gang
la mang ja chad med dang / brgya mchod kyi thebs nas spungs 'phyar ma lcags 'bo chen mo'i brgya dang brgyad/ bla ma lha khang du bla mchod kyi thebs bcas sbyar/ rim gro
ja thug brgyad tsam zhus/ spyi so nas drin gzor ston pa/ 'jam dbyangs/ rdor sems bcas kyi gser sku che legs gsum/ rgya sbugs che legs skyon med/ karma gan dril skyon med
cha 'grigs shub bcas/ khrab rmog cha tshang / bye ltang / snam ras sogs byung / mang ja'i thog ltang rtse ma gtogs cha tshang tshogs gsham du phul/ de'i steng du dril
ras gtos che ba/ bsngo rten gyi gri/ ga'u/ dkar yol/ sku 'dra sogs mang ba 'gyed du phul/ de nas thon gdong grwa dmangs thams cad thugs 'phreng ba'i spyan chab g.yo ba dang
bcas skyel bar pheb/ dbon rin po che bla g.yel mthil na byis pa chung ngu

ltar bshum gyin skyel bar pheb byung / nged rang kyang 'dzin bdag bgyis pa'i dgon pa thams cad kyi nang nas 'di rang la yid 'gro ba yod pas 'ong gdong sems shin tu 'phreng
bar byung / gnyer pa sogs chibs skyel ba yang mang bar yod/ bkra shis zam pa'i thad du pheb pa'i gra pa rnams kyi kha btags kyi g.yab mo gnang bar rta kha bsgyur thengs gsum
byas/ tshur lam bkra shis mthong smon du dkar spro zhabs tog rgyas par 'dug /dbon drung sogs de nas phyir pheb/ bkra shis mthong smon gyi chos mdzad dpon g.yog de nub
sger par pheb/ zhal ngo rnams la 'chi med dpal ster gyi tshe dbang phul/ de nas rim gyis rang gnas su 'byor/ 'di lo dus stabs nas sems ma bde ba ma gtogs kha ton 'phel ba
byung / ston zur khang sde pa rdo rje rnam rgyal la mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs sngon du 'gro ba'i nyams khrid zhal shes gsum gyis brgyan pa/ chos nyid dngos ston gyi byin
rlabs/ rtsa dbu ma che ba'i khrid bcas phul/ de nas sde pa kun dga' dpal 'byor la'ang byin rlabs shar khrid rgyas par phul/ 'di lo ston mjug nged rang rogs bcas gros
byas pas tshogs gsog sgrib sbyong bcas ra ba smad pa/ gzhi ba/ gsang sngags gling pa/ rab brtan gyi btsun ma/ rmor pa bcas khyon nyis brgyar nye bar dgongs rdzogs byas pa'i
sang nyin 'khyongs/ pheb gdong mang ja bzhes thug gnyis bcas dang / dngos gzhi'i nyin tshar dus gnyis sku yon zab rgyas bcas zhus pa 'di nas lo bstar ma chad par zhus/
lo sngon ma ra ba smad/ chos

'khor gnas/ grwa phyi tshogs/ byams gling sgrub sde rnams su'ang sa bstan gyi rim gror mang ja gnyis re/ bsngo rten bcas zhus/ 'di lo snga rting tshor rtsa tshig dge lugs ma
gtogs grub mtha' gzhan thams cad la mang 'gyed lta ci/ zhabs tog gi rigs che phra gang yang byed pa med pa dang / rnying ma ming bsgrags sa med pa sogs yid shin tu pham
par byung / nged rang khri mon nas gegs med du thon pas sa lugs gzhan ma la'ang cung zhig phan par byung ste/ sdig can tsho'i lag tu tshud phyin thar pa bla ma bdag tsam
du zad do/ /smras pa/ yongs gdug pa 'dab chags shwa na'i lo/ /kho dga' rab dbang phyug stobs rgyas pas/ /rten khyad 'phags rnams la bzang btson bcol/ /skyabs gu ru'i tshogs
la g.yul las byas/ /mi che che thams cad til bzhin 'tshir/ /dgon mang po ming gi lhag mar btang / /khong dud 'gro'ang yid 'byung mchi ma dku/ /sems med kyi bems po rnams
kyang 'gul/ /kho log smon gyi las shugs btsan pa dang / /bstan spyi sger gyi byur chag langs pa'i stabs/ /lar bde ba'i gnas skabs ma mchis kyang / /rang skal gyi bsod
nams mi dman pa/ /dgra 'chi bdag kha nas de'u thar/ /lar de 'dra'i gnas skabs bsam tsa na/ /sdang dgra bo yang mig nas mchi ma 'chor/ /skyabs dkon mchog gsum gyi bka' drin
las/ /dus da lta skyid pa'i nyi ma shar/ /pha gcig chog rgyal po tshar pa rje/ /khyed bsam zhing snying nas gsol 'debs kyi/ /dus byang chub snying po ma thob bar/ /thugs
brtse ba'i lcags kyus gzung du gsol/ /de dag gi snga phyi thams cad du gzhung gi che gnyan

thams cad nged rang la dad mos gnang ba'i stabs kyis sa dgon thams cad la phan gang thogs byed khul byas/ chos 'khor gnas rab 'byams pa yar 'phel sogs mi bcu gcig la bde mchog
gi dbang dang / nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs dang khrid/ gzhan yang 'dod chos mang du phul/ phran sgo dga' ldan gling gzhis kar sde pa zur khang pa'i bka' 'gyur
la tshoms chen du gzhi ba'i grwa pa bzhi bcu skor dang lhan du kun rig la brten pa'i rab gnas nyin gang ma rgyas pa/ zhi ba'i sbyin bsreg dang bcas pa byas/ gzhi pa grwa
tshang nas 'du khang du 'bod pa mdzad/ sgrol ma maNDal bzhi dang 'brel ba'i brtan bzhugs rgyas par byung zhing / spyi sger thams cad nas zab zab dpe med gnang / sde pa zur
khang nas kyang rab ston 'bul ba rgya nag gi dgang blug sogs dpag med stsal/ rdo rje shugs ldan rtsal la phrin bcol dang dmod nas phul bas dgyes bzhin du srung mar zhal
gyis bzhes/ kha reg nas theg mchog gling dbon slob sku mched pheb/ padma dbang drag lags kyis gnas bcu'i rtogs brjod kyi sku thang grwa mtshungs bcu gcig kha gsar ri mo
dang gong gsham sogs spus legs dang / chos rje gcung gis yab kyi byang chog rten sogs dpang sa mtho ba gnang / sa phag lo gsar pa rang lo re drug pa'i nang du rin chen spungs
pa'i dpon slob/ 'jam dbyangs byang pa/ bslab btus/ chos 'byung brgya rtsa sogs lung dkon pa mang po dang rjes gnang rigs kyang mang bar phul/ gsang phur mang ja sngar
rgyun ltar lo sngon ma'i nang du shing mang nas

chos ldan can gnyis gnang ba'i gzims chung gsar rgyag sogs la rab gnas dang bcas cis kyang 'ong dgos tshul byung kyang stabs ma 'grigs pas 'gro ma thub pa nas/ 'di lo bka'
bcu kun dga' sangs rgyas dang / bstan 'dzin yar 'phel gnyis ched gtad du gtang byung bas tshag gur la tshe dbang zhig la phyin pa/ lha sa nas sde pa bka' blon lum pa nas
kyis rib tsam 'ong dgos tshul gnang ba ltar phyin/ zhag gsum bsdad/ sde pa bka' blon/ sde pa khrus phu nas yab/ sde pa byings nas sogs la tshe dbang 'chi med dpal ster/ rta
mgrin gyi byin rlabs sogs phul/ mar lam snon gzhis kar yang tshe rta'i dbang sogs grub/ 'khor 'phral lho brag la 'gro ba'i grabs bgyis nas nyi shu gsum la bteg /'di lo
dus stabs dang bcas blo gsal 'di gar khag che ba'i sdod dgos byung stabs nged rang gi rogs blo ldan/ chos ldan rnams 'chos pa/ skya bo gnyis bcas dang / lho brag gnyis bcas
su lum gru grangs pa'i de nub ra ba smad bla brang du zhabs tog rgyas par byung zhing / rim gyis dol brgyud zhag lnga thog tu slebs/ dpon slob dam chos kun bzang grwa
pa gsum bcas rong pa bar chibs bsur 'byor/ gling chen gzhis kar thab bsu rgyas par bcas 'dug /der gung tshigs grub/ de nas dgon par phyin/ ser sbreng bcas bla brang du 'byor/
snga sor khur len gyi skabs gzims chung zhig med na sde pa gdan 'dren sogs med thabs mi 'dug pas cis kyang bzo dgos bla brang nas shing sogs kyi thebs sprad pa yin
kyang dpon slob bsam yas pa'i skabs gnang ma

thub pas dam chos kun bzang gi skabs legs par grub pa bkod pa shin tu legs pa'i sdod nyams spro bar 'dug /de'i sang nyin thon dbang yin 'dug pas snga sor phul ba'i phyar dar
gnyis la thug lcags rtse gsum shin tu legs pa me ri bkrol bcas che nges gnyis gsar bzos byas pa bskyon song bas bag dro ba shin tu legs pa byung ngo / /thon dbang gi 'tshams
sogs grwa 'grigs par byung bas dbang kyang nged rang gis byas shing / khrom shin tu che zhing nam mkha' 'jam pa/ lha mi thams cad spro sag ge bar gyur/ bka' bcu kun
dga' bsam 'grub kyis thams cad mkhyen pa klu sgrub rgya mtsho'i gsung ngag slob bshad kyi khrid yig tshang bar bris pa dngos gtsang bar byung / de nas bka' bcu kun dga'
shes rab kyis dkar steng du bos/ zhag gnyis bsdad/ sgo mtha'i khrom shin tu che bar grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe dbang rgyas par byas/ lho brag pa dad zhen che ba'i stabs gang
phyin sar char pa shin tu che ba babs pas char dkon pa'i stabs dad pa lhag par 'phel/ mar lam bka' bcu sbyin pa dbang pos sa bzang du bos/ zhag gnyis bsdad/ der yang rjen
lha gral ba'i khrom shin tu che bar grub rgyal tshe dbang byas/ 'dir yang char chen po babs/ 'bul ba'ang shin tu tshan che bar byung / shing mang rang du'ang khrom dbang
rgyas par byas/ rgyun du stod smad bar gsum thams cad nas nyin bstar 'phrad mi bar ma chad par rang la gang yod kyi thog nas sprug sprug gsig gsig byung bas rnyed pa'ang
shin tu che bar byung / shing mang spyi so nas kyang khro che ba bcas 'bul ba bsam

gyis mi khyab pa dang / grwa pa rnams kyis kyang mar gtso bor gyur pa'i 'bul ba bsam gyis mi khyab par phul/ sbyong gar gyi stabs nas btsun ma rnams bskul ma thub pas g.yag
khal grwa bsgrigs par 'bul mi mang du byung zhing 'ga' re nyos pa bcas mdzo g.yag bcu bzhi tsam dang / bong khal brgyad dgu bcas par mar rkyang khal brgya skor byung zhing
/ gzhan yang ras tshos sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa bcas 'ong / tshur lam gnam rdo sogs su'ang 'brog pa rnams kyis sha mar dpag med 'bul mi 'dug /gri gur zhag gsum bsdad
dgos byung zhing / sde pa mdo mkhar nas dang / lha khang dang sde pa gri mdzod nas bcas kyis sku 'dra gsar bzhengs la gzungs gzhug rab gnas/ tshe rta sogs so so'i dgongs
bzhed dang mthun par phul/ ri bo bde chen pa'i brgyad grwa pa rnams la'ang sgrol ma dang sme brtsegs kyi rjes gnang sogs byas/ rdzong dpon so so dang gri mdzod nas bcas
kyis mar gtso bor gyur pa'i 'bul ba gtos che ba dang / gri gu ba rnams kyis kyang sha mar sogs dpag med byung / de nas dkar mo gling du zhag gnyis bsdad dgos byung ba'i chibs
dpon tshor tshe rta sogs kyi dbang bskur nas rim gyis rang gnas su 'byor/ 'phreng po dga' ldan gling du gling smad zhabs drung kun dga' 'byung gnas gshegs par 'ong dgos
tshul bzhin phyin/ gzhi pa'i dpon slob grwa bgres dang bcas pa dang lhan du kun rig gi sgo nas dbang bskur lam ston zhus/ sger du kye rdor gyi sgo nas bdun tshigs kyi
cho ga dang / zhi ba las thams cad pa'i sbyin sreg gi sgo nas bsreg blugs

rgyas par phul/ tshogs dbur phyin nas byang chog rgyas par phul/ na bza' cha tshang sogs nyer spyad thams cad rang gnas su 'byor/ yang 'brog mig pa'i sde pa dpon g.yog la nA
ro mkha' spyod ma'i khrid sogs byas/ lo bstar gyi ser tshogs sngar rgyun ltar rgyas par zhus/ de nas lcags byi rang lo re bdun pa'i zla ba brgyad par ra ba smad nas rab
'byams pa ngag dbang tshe brtan/ rab 'byams pa kun gsal rnam rgyal/ bka' dpal ldan phrin las/ lcags zam pa blo gsal phrin las dang kun gsal/ sde pa zur khang pa'i chos mdzad
ma gnyis sogs la nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs khrid bcas rgyas par byas/ zla ba gsum par bka' bcu byams pa bstan 'dzin dang / bka' bcu kun dga' rab brtan gnyis
'byor pas de gong nas sems la bsams kyang bar skabs su dus kyi stabs ma grub par 'di lo bka' bcu kun dga' rab brtan gyis phyag bris gnang ba'i rje btsun gong ma lnga/ tshar
chen rdo rje 'chang / drin can bco brgyad pa chen po rnams kyi gtsor byas pa'i thang sku bdun la gsung ngag nye brgyud/ nA ro mkha' spyod/ gur zhal thams cad kyi brgyud
pa tshang ba/ gser chos kyi yi dam thams cad dang / gur/ bram gzugs/ rdo rje rab brtan ma/ beg tse/ rnam sras sogs lha mgron la tshang ba'i gzabs bris gnang / bka' bcu
byams pa bstan 'dzin gyis brgyad stong pa brgya rtsa dang / 'bum sogs sgrogs pa gnang / sde pa khrus phu nas kyis bka' 'gyur dang / gnas bcu'i zhal thang gi rab gnas la 'ong
dgos tshul pheb pa ltar phyin/ yar lam lcags zam du

phyin nas khro phur zhag gsum bsdad/ nged blo gsal/ chos grags/ chos mdzad bcas kyis kye rdor la brten pa'i rab gnas nyin gang ma rgyas par byas/ sde pa yab sras steng zhal
thams cad la tshe dbang brgya tshar/ skyed tshal 'og gi dpon slob bcas la gur lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang byas/ mar lam lcags zam la 'ong / zhag gcig bsdad nas ko gzhung bcas
rang gnas su 'byor/ 'phrod bsten la sga 'dra chu tshan la phyin/ tshur lam chos 'khor gnas dpon slob bstan 'dzin dpal bzang dang / rab 'byams pa kun dga' smon lam bcas
dpal sgang du pheb nas/ sang nyin dgon par cis kyang 'ong dgos gnang ba ltar khas len zhus/ sang nyin phyin/ grwa slob thams cad rgya sgo 'gag tu bsu bar pheb/ shar mar
bla brang du phyin/ gsol 'dren zhabs tog phun sum tshogs par 'dug /rab 'byams pa yar 'phel sogs slob bu rnams kyis bsnyen bkur dpag med bsgrigs pa gnang / grwa pa'ang phal
cher gyis mjal dar ja stir bsnams nas pheb/ lce zhol ba'ang 'phrad mi mang bar byung / phyi dro chos grar tshogs gur gyi thog phub pa'i skya ser shin tu mang bar grub
rgyal lugs kyi tshe dbang byas/ sang zhogs tshogs su mang ja bsngo rten sne gzhag zhus nas ra ba smad pa'i grwa tshang gsang phur dbyar chos la pheb gshis shar mar gru don
'ong pas dgon par chos rje blo bzang don grub kyang pheb 'dug /chos rje lags la gser btul dang dngul btul tshan shin tu che bar 'dug pas tshogs gsog gnang bzhed la gang
'gab bka' 'dri gnang 'dug pa/ de ltar na gnas chen rnams dang khyad par zhabs tog

cher med pa rnams la gnang rgyu byung na gzhan las phan yon che bar 'ong / thugs khyad med phyin bkra shis chos sde'i bla ma lha khang gi lam 'bras brgyud pa rnams la snga
sor mi sha mdog ma gtogs med pas cis kyang gnang dgos rgyu zhus ltar bka' bcu kun dga' rab brtan gyis sku zlar pheb pa'i zhal gser thams cad la phun sum tshogs pa dang /
khyad par lam 'bras brgyud pa gsar bzhengs lta bur byung 'dug pas bsam pa tshim par byung / de nas yar pheb pa'i bka' bcu lags kyis phyag bris btsugs/ rgyal dwags po grwa
tshang gi dpon slob ngag dbang don grub dpon slob gsum pheb cing / bkra shis chos sde nas dbon rin po che'ang 'di khar bzhugs bzhin bcas par sgrub thabs rgya mtsho lung
bcas/ sgrol ma dkar sngon sogs dang / gur lha brgyad/ zhal bsnyen dus/ phyag bzhi pa lha mang / phyag drug pa shangs lugs gtsang ma/ dmag zor ma thun mong ma yin pa/ dur
khrod bdag po'i rjes gnang dang / lung gi rigs shin tu mang ba 'di lo rgyal dbyar chos la byed rgyu yin pheb par bstan rgyun la bsams nas rgyas par phul/ mar lam dbon drung
dang lhan du pheb/ de nas dpon slob sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan pheb par sngar ma gsan pa'i kha skong pu sti/ dud sol pusti/ gyi ljang pusti/ beg pod/ rjes gnang kyang gur
lha brgyad dang lha bcu gnyis/ lcam dral lha gsum thun mong ma yin pa/ zangs gri skor gsum/ pu tra'i zur bka' sogs bstan don la bsam pa'i sba bsri med par phul zhing /
mjug tu gling stod

zhabs drung rin po che'ang pheb par phal cher la 'ong ba yod/ nged rang gi thob yig pusti'i lung sogs kyang phul/ khong dpon slob gnyis nas 'chad nyan kyang gnang thub pa yong
gshis sems spro bar byung / zla ba lnga pa nas mgo brtsams dpung 'jug gi mgo tshugs/ mi rnams g.yeng ba che ba'i ngang du gyur/ thog mar sbyong gar pa rnams kyis dmag
do dam par bskul ba'i zir long che bar byung kyang 'di lo byas pa don ldan gyi skyabs mgon rgyal dbang mchog chen po chibs kha bsgyur ba'i sgo dod pas mi rnams khag spyod
la ji mi snyam par gyur/ de nas rim gyis je gsal je gsal du gyur/ kong po sde pa sga chags pa gshegs pa'i bsngo byang rten dngul srang nyi shu rtsa drug /hu ja 'khor drug
/mar ltang shin tu che ba/ gos rgyan bzhi'i sku stod sogs stobs che ba 'byor bar byang chog bsngo smon sogs rgyas par zhus/ de nas zla ba brgyad pa'i mjug nas kong dmag
gi byar dwags lhum rtse sogs rim gyis blangs/ byang 'dam du sbyong gar pa sbrang ma me 'od la ma chags pa ltar rgyang ring du bros/ dgu pa'i nang du rgya nag gi dmag dpon
gtsang jun dang / tA lo ye sogs mal gro brgyud lha sa'i lcags grong du 'byor zhing / rtse'i gzims chung phyag mdzod thams cad du rgya yig gis mnan/ mi srun pa'i gtso bo
bdun pha rol gyi gzigs mor btang / zla ba de ka'i tshes bco lnga la srid zhi'i gtsug rgyan lhar bcas 'gro ba yongs kyi skyabs mgon rgyal dbang phyag na pad dkar 'dzin pa
skal bzang rgya mtsho'i sde chen po gru 'dzin pho brang chen po'i seng ge'i khri la zhabs sen padmo rnam par bkod pa'i rten 'brel zhal dkar thog ma gzhol/ mngar 'og gnang
ba'i grwa bsgrig la blo gsal gyis phyin pa'i rten 'brel gyi sgo 'phar dang po 'grigs/ bod khams skyid pa'i nyi ma shar ba'i

skabs so/ /smras pa/ kha ba ri ba'i bsod nams phung po'i rdul/ /gcig tu spungs pa'i legs byas skya rengs kyis/ /skal bzang dpyid kyi nor 'dzin kun khyab pa/ /rgya mtsho'i mthar
thug 'gro rnams rtse dgar rol/ /a ho 'di 'dra'i dga' ba thob pa 'di/ /yang na mes pos ched du byas pa'am/ /'on te sgyu ma rmi lam lta zhig snyam/ /tha mal blo 'di 'khyog
la 'phyang mo nyug /de lta na yang gru 'dzin bdag po yis/ /rang zhing bskyang phyir sna tshogs sgyu thabs kyis/ /ma rungs skrod pa'i mdzad bzang 'phrul mo cher/ /tshangs
pa'i 'jig rten man chad gzigs mor g.yeng / /de nas zla ba bcu par zhal mjal phyag dbang la phyin/ thog mar mchod dpon 'jam dbyangs lha dbang sku mched rang slob tu song
gshis blo gsal sku zhabs la btang bas sang nyin mjal kha zhu ba'i rogs ram gnang dgos pa'i zhu sam 'bul bar btang bas shin tu dgyes pas thog mar mchod dpon shag rang
du shog gnang ltar phyin/ sku mched gnyis char nas mjal dar gtong ba gnang / gdan bzos dpag med dang / mjal kha shin tu 'gol ba zhig byed dgos gnang bar gong chos pa'i zhabs
brtan dang 'grigs/ rnam thar rgya chen gyi phyag dpe gser pod 'gongs che ba sogs phyag mjal gya nom pa dang bcas mjal bas shin tu dgyes pa'i zhal 'dzum lhag par stsal/
mchod dpon sku mched nas da dung thengs cig mjal na 'ong pheb ltar/ slar 'di khar 'ong dgos rgyu mtshan phul/ de nub pu trag dpon slob sde pa drung yig nas se rar shog
gnang ltar phyin/ dgongs ja buu ram sogs rgyas pa dang / sang nyin

rig byed ma'i rjes gnang byas/ gung tshigs thon nas mar 'ong / gser dmar gyi dril bu rtse gdong gi phyag dril yin zhes gnang / lha sar bkra shis bde legs su sde pa khrus bu
nas sku zhud kyis ltem par glud rdzong zhus pas phan ngo shin tu che ba byung zhing / sde pa bka' blon dang lhan du tshe dbang 'chi med dpal ster brgya tshar phul/ slar
rgyal sras rin po che'ang pheb pas tshe dbang 'chi med rdo rje'i srog shing rgyal sras rin po che dpon slob/ sde pa bka' blon/ khrus phu nas yab sras sogs lhan du phul/ rgyal
sras rin po ches snam sbyar legs pa zhig phyag bdar nas bskon pa gnang / kha btags sogs dpe med gnang / snga sor zla ba dgu pa'i mjug char can kyi sku rim ser tshogs
skabs bstan 'dzin dbang gi bka' shog dang / dga' ldan khri rin po che'i thugs dam bcas rgyal por bstan skyong gi bla ma sngags rams pa stobs ldan la zhal gyi chos skor sogs
mang ba dgos zer 'byor par zhag bcu'i bar du gsang 'dus 'jam rdor gyi dbang / zhal gyis rjes gnang rigs bdun tsam dang / gzhan yang rjes gnang gi rigs mang ba/ zhal pod
kyi lung bcas byed dgos byung zhing / 'di skabs kyang ched gnyer gyi dpal 'dzin pod chung gi lung / klu dbang rgyal po dang / sme brtsegs lugs gnyis/ khro mo sme brtsegs
sogs kyi rjes gnang dang / no mo khang phyag mdzod sde par rnam sras mdung dmar phyag mtshan bzhi pa'i rjes gnang dge slong 'jam dbyangs lags dang sngags rams pa stobs
ldan sogs dang mnyam du byas/ dngul phon che ba/

gos yug sogs rnyed pa bla med byung / slar yang gong zhabs rin po che'i zhal mjal phyag dbang la phyin par sems dpa' chen po dang / nged dpon slob gnyis ma gtogs gzhan su yang
med/ sku mdun de gar 'jog pa gnang / sems dpa' chen po ni smyon pa ltar bzhengs nas thogs song / nged rang la bka' 'dri'ang lhod par pheb pas skal pa bzang pa'i yang
rtser son/ mar lam mchod dpon shag tu gung tshigs rgyas pa/ kha btags/ chab rog /bla gos/ gos chen gyi pang khebs sogs bla med stsal/ lha ldan du zhag nyi shu 'gor nas rang
gnas su 'byor/ snga sor sprel lo rgyal po'i skabs lha ldan du yun ring 'gor dus/ ngor e wa~M chos ldan gyi khri thog pa mkhan chen dpal gling pa pheb par dmar po skor
gsum gyi rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa/ zhal sgrub dus las sbyor gyi mgon po/ dkar po tshe 'phel thun mong ma yin pa/ nyi ma sbas pa'i lugs kyi sgrol ma nyer gcig gi rjes
gnang / gser chos dzaM dmar srog sgrub kyi rjes gnang / yi ge gsar rnying gi lung sogs bstan rgyun la phan pa'i 'gro gang che byas/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i khri
thog pa yin pas ngor bstod sde snod ma'i ljags lung thugs thog nas zhus/ gser srang gang sogs gnang skyes dpag med stsal/ yar 'brog zhabs drung rin po cher mkha' spyod
ma'i byin rlabs zhal gso phul/ gangs can mkhan zur ngag dbang rab brtan/ sngags rams pa stobs ldan dang lhan du thams cad 'tshems med yod/ yang de nas mi

'gyang bar e ti ni sbo shog thu'i phyag bris bcas 'ong dgos tshul gnang ba ltar blo gsal bcas phyin/ blo ldan mal grol song / de nub mgar tshad du bsdad/ gzhis ka nas gsol
ja dgong ja/ bu ram bcas gnang / mar lam 'ong dgos tshul 'dug /de nas smon grod du shar mar phyin/ zhag bco lnga bskor bsdad/ grub rgyal tshe dbang / gzungs grwa lnga'i dbang
zur bka'/ gzungs grwa lnga/ phyag rdor u tsArya/ rta mgrin dbyug tog can/ sgrol ma dkar sngon/ mgon po phyag drug pa sogs rjes gnang mang bar byas/ lo tsA ba rje drung
gi lo tsA ba mdzad pas shin tu mgu bar byung song zhing / srid 'ong ba'i bsrung ba'ang gang zab bzos/ blo bzang dpal 'bar gtor ma bzo bar mgo mjug thams cad la yod/ de
dus zur khang sde pa dbang ldan rdo rje sku zhud kyis shin tu ltem par tshe dbang brgya rtsa sogs byed par 'phral 'phral 'ongs pas sku khams seng dwangs la song / gdan sa
gong nas gong ma rin po che mjal khar pheb pa g.yu thog tu bzhugs stan 'jags 'dug pa/ ma gzhi ra ba smad du mjal dgos kyang / da lam phyag dbang dang slar zhabs brtan sogs
snyan gsan 'bul ba bcas phyin par/ mjal mi mang bas mgron gnyer gyi kha la ma nyan par blo gsal gyis lan yang med par slog song / sang nyin de mjal khar yang mi 'gro
zer 'dug nyer lnga'i nyin chibs kha bsgyur song bas 'di res mjal ma thub/ rtse nas drung yig rab 'byams pa ngag dbang 'jam dpal pheb par jo lugs kyi sgrol ma nyer gcig gi
rjes gnang byas/ blo bzang lung rigs dang ngag dbang 'jigs med sogs grwa tshang gi grwa pa bcu skor dang phyed phan la sde pa rta mgrin kyang yod/ blo bzang dngos grub dang
/ bstan dar/ chos mdzad don grub kyang yod cing / nyin bstar gyi grwa pa gnyis re gsum re sogs so so'i thugs bzhed

dang mthun pa'i rjes gnang rigs dang lung yang mang bar phul/ gangs can mkhan zur la rnal 'byor ma'i be'u bum nas lung mang ba dang rjes gnang kha shas sogs song / 'ong gdong
sha zab par zhus shing / dngul lnga bcu pa/ gos yug /gser srang do sogs phul/ lo tsA ba des longs nas gtam bshad mang du btang/ sbo shog thu steng zhal la rgyun du zhal
'don mdzad rgyu nged rang gi ming sgra yod pa dgos gsung pa ltar phul/ dad mos che bar mdzad/ gru khar thug /sog po zhig btang / snga ma log 'ong dus no mo khang sde pa
dpon g.yog gru khar thug pheb/ kha btags 'dom do yod pa zhig nged rang gi mdun rgyab tu skor/ slar mjal ba'i rten 'brel yin gsung / spyan chab mang po mdzad 'dug /de nas
mar lam snon du 'ong / zhal ngo tshor tshe rta brgya rtsa byab khrus sogs phul nas rang gnas su slebs/ sde pa rta ra mdo nas sku mched pheb par rnal 'byor ma'i khrid skyor
byas/ bsam yas rab byung pa kun dga' tshul khrims dang kun dga' shes rab gnyis byung bar ra ba smad dpon slob kyis las slob dang gsang ston sbrags/ bye rdzing tshogs pa
dge slong ngag dbang tshul khrims/ bka' bcu kun dga' bstan 'phel gyis kha skong dang grogs ldan byas te bsnyen rdzogs byas/ lcags glang zla ba dang po rang lo re brgyad
pa'i steng gdan sa chen po nas sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams rin chen gang gi mjal phyag grub nas bsam yas brgyud lho kha phyogs su chibs kha bsgyur ba ra
ba smad du tshes drug la pheb pa'i sgo dod/ de nyin lcags zam

du'ang sprul sku rin po che skyabs sdom bzhes pa dang / mgon po bdun tshogs sngags thang grwa tshar bzhengs pa'i rab gnas sbrags pa/ zhal dkar khri 'bul bcas da lam dus tshes
phul thebs med gshis ma 'ongs pa'i bka' thebs mi 'dug gnang bar brten/ nged rang blo ldan bcas pas tshes bzhi la lcags zam du thon/ blo gsal dang grwa pa rnams yo byad
dang bcas tshes lnga la thon nas zhabs brtan gyi snyan gsan sogs 'bul ba'i grwa sgrigs bcas 'gro bar byas/ lcags zam du tshes lnga'i nyin tshe dbang / gur mgon lha brgyad
kyi rjes gnang sogs phul/ tshes drug gi nam phyed nas grwa pa rnams kyis lha bsang mdzad/ nged rang gis kyang snga nyin nas grabs shoms grub stabs kha ton sogs grub 'phral
tshoms chen du kye rdo rje'i bdag bskyed sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas rab gnas rgyas pa dngos gzhi thams cad nam langs gong du grub par byas/ gzims chung du sprul sku rin
po cher skyabs sdom phul/ de nas grwa pa rnams kyis rol mo'i bsu ba dang bcas tshoms chen du pheb pa rten 'brel khyad nas thog mar nged rang nas sku gsung thugs rten/
na bza' cha tshang sogs zhal dkar phul/ de nas sde pa bka' blon/ gnyan mkhar shar sogs kyis legs 'bul dpangs mtho ba dngos gtsang bar 'dug /de nas ston mo bzang ba 'dug thog
phyag mdzod la sbyin bdag bsko ba nas mjug chog gi bar du bgyis/ de nas nyin gung yol mtshams grub pas nged rang 'gro dgos stabs dgongs pa zhus par/ da lam zhag lnga
drug nyin bstar rten 'brel khyad nas sdod dgos 'dug rung / don gzhan dang ma 'dra gshis

de ga gnang dgos yod pas sang zhog 'di kha nas nam skyag chog gnang gsungs 'dug kyang sems khol ba'i de nub rang nas thon par 'ong / zhabs tog bsnyen bkur ni tshad las 'das
par 'dug /phyag mdzod grwa dmangs bcas nas mchod rten rtsa bar skyel bar pheb/ de nub gong dkar du nyi nub la slebs/ gong dkar du drung yig rgya mtsho'i nang du bsdad/ mkhyen
rab lags dang dkon gnyer ba'i grwa pa 'ga' zhig /gnas chung ba'i sku mag sogs pheb mi mang bar byung / sang zhog nam phyed yol kha ton grub 'phral thon song / rgyal
grub gling thub nam gyis 'khyol/ de nas mgyogs par 'ongs pas ra ba smad du nyi ma kha 'bol la 'byor/ tshes drug gi nyin blo gsal kyang pheb bsur phyin pa'i mgron gnyer la
tshes bdun la grwa tshang gi zhabs brtan yin gshis brgyad la phul chog pa snyan gsan phul 'dug don ltar/ de nyin grwa tshang gi zhabs brtan gyi dung brda gtong ba dang
sleb pa dus mnyam du byung / mjal phyag kyang shar mar tshogs rang du zhus par gong ma rin po che khri thog nas bzhengs pa'i dgyes tshor che bar zhal 'dzum bcas gnang / dpon
slob nas tshe dpag med rong ston brgyud par sbyar chog pa'i chog khrigs nged rang nas bgyis pa de 'dzugs pa gnang ba gsung chog kyang shin tu 'grigs par/ sku gsung thugs
rten bdag gis bshad pa bgyis nas dpon slob kyis rim gyis bteg nas phyag tu 'bul ba gnang / zhal bzhes nged kyis zhus par/ tshogs pas maNDal 'bul ba sogs dang / spyi sger
thams cad nas 'bul dpangs shin tu mtho bar 'dug /de'i sang nyin yang snga ma ji lta

ba bzhin gsung chog grwa tshang nas mang ja gnyis thog nas gnang bar/ nged rang nas sku rten bdag nyin chen po bzang po dpal gyi zhal gzigs gyi sgrol ma'i sku mtho gang ba/
gsung rten bdag nyid chen po'i phyag dpe rgya nag ma padma rA ga dang ma rgad sogs kyi phra ldan/ ba so'i glegs shing 'gongs che ba/ thugs rten gdung rten lcags rtse ma/
mdzod btags 'dom 'khor ma bcas phyag tu phul/ mdzod btags/ bsod btags/ rtags brgyad bcas legs pa nyi shu rtsa dgu'i phon gyis mgo byas pa'i bcu gsum tshan/ rdo rje gsang
lam dmar po legs pas mgo byas pa/ sangs rgyas so lnga'i sku thang grwa tshar spus legs bco lngas mgo byas pa/ sbugs chol rnyid ma shub bcas kyi mgo byas pa/ 'di thams cad
la dril gtan nas med/ mjug tu nya lcibs kyi me tog chas mgo byas pa sogs gang yod thog nas dngos gtsang bar phul/ rmor pa'i spyi so grwa pa so so'i 'bul ba 'ong nad khyag
yod/ de mjug tu rab brtan gyi btsun ma rnams kyis spyi 'bul dang sger 'bul/ byang kha brgyud kyi sbyin bdag rnams kyang mthud pas bag dro bar byung / steng du sger mjal
la'ang mdzod btags phon che ba dang / yum drung dang phyag mdzod la'ang phyag mjal ja nom pa phul/ yar klungs sogs nas nged kyi lag tu gnam lcags kyi rdo rje yongs grags
de yod pa snyan du 'bul mi byung stabs/ phyag mdzod nas de 'dra yod 'dug pa spus bsgyur dgos nan gyis gnang byung bar thog mar de 'dri'i regs med ces sku rtsed zhus par
nan bskyed gnang byung bar/ de 'dra yod pa snga sor nas 'bul rtsis

yin rung bdag rkyen ma gnang na chud zos dogs byung kyang thugs la gtad na cis kyang 'bul spro zhes mthing khra dang kha btags kyi na bza' bcas bdag chen rin po che rang gi
phyag tu phul bas shin tu dgyes pa'i rtser son/ bdag ni nor bdag po'i phyag tu 'phrod snyam dga' ba thob/ da dung de rigs lag tu 'khor byung na cis kyang dgos zhes bka'
gnang zhing / yum nas kyang nan bcag che bar byung / sku zhabs rin po ches dam rdzas stong rdo brgya rdo gnyis/ sil ma phon che ba phyag mdud bcas dang / dngul sogs tshan
grangs gnang ba ma zhus kyang / de nub phyag mdzod nas rdo rje'i legs so yin gnang ba'i dngul srang sum cu kha btags bcas gnang bar/ de la bltas nas phul ba min pas dam
rdzas byung na gong byung zhu dgos zhus par tha ma'ang phyed bzhes gnang kyang ma zhus/ da lam 'di khar dam rdzas 'dzangs pas tshan che ba med/ slar 'bul gnang bas zhogs
pa dam rdzas brgya rdo sil ma bcas mang bar byung / de nas grwa tshang dpon slob dang nged gsum/ dbu chos/ zhol gyi drung 'khor bcas chibs skyel tshan che ba bcas sgang sib
bar chibs skyel zhus/ nged de nub ra ba smad du bsdad/ sang nyin rang gnas su log /de skabs skyid gshongs su yum drung nas sa skyar rgya can med gshis snga phan rtsol
ba byas kyang ma byung bas/ da lam de kha gzhan dang ma 'dra ba'i thugs 'dris che stabs phyag na yod na dang / de min thugs rtsol dgos tshul gnang byung bar/ nged rang la
khyad par 'phags pa zhig yod pa sku zhabs su phul tshar bas gong chos tshun la 'bul thub pa 'ong zhus nas 'di kha

nas rgya can rtsa ba dang / bla ma mal gyi thugs dam rten 'khor lo bde mchog nag po lugs kyi sku brnyan rdo nag las grub pa sa chen gyi phyag tu byung ba/ phyis dpon ag glen
la gnang ba'i sna dkar rtse'i nang rten du bzhugs/ phyis rdor brag gi phyag tu 'byor par stor dus 'khyar ba nged rang gi lag tu 'byor ba'i khyad can de dang bcas 'bul bar
blo gsal btang / gong dkar chos sder zhu yig bcas phul bas shin tu dgyes/ bka' lan rgyas pa dam rdzas mang ba bcas gnang zhing / da dung de rigs byung na dgos tshul bka'
nan che ba bcas sku zhabs/ yum/ phyag mdzod thams cad nas rgyas par gnang / skyid gshongs su chos ldan bzang po 'das pa'i gong zhabs su ljags bsngo rten dang / 'di gar
kyang bsngo byang gi rten skyel bar 'byor/ bla brang nas kyang dbon rin po ches zhabs brtan 'bul bar mgyogs par thon rgyun yin pas zhal bzhes zhu lugs rgyas bsdus gnyis
tsam dgos gnang ltar lugs mang bar yod pa'i rgyas pa dang / cung zad bsdus tsam bcas phul/ mi 'gyang bar rgod dkar la brgyud grwa pa lnga bcu skor zhabs brtan 'bul bar pheb
par grwa 'grigs par byung 'dug /tshur lam dpon slob thams cad 'di gar pheb/ rje btsun yid bzhin 'khor lo'i gsung chog dang 'brel ba'i brtan bzhugs rgyas par gnang / spyi
so nas rgyal srid sna bdun dngul gyi 'bur ma/ rdzas brgyad tsakli/ rten khebs/ ther ma sbugs sogs dang / dbon rin po che grwa dmangs bcas pas che 'byor chung 'byor 'bul
ba gnang / dbon rin po ches snga sor phul ba'i zhal bzhes sgra dag cing brjod bya gtsang bar 'dug pas dga' bar byung /

zhag gnyis kyi bar bzhugs/ bskang gso rgyas par gnang bas sku rim smar bar byung / dge slong tshul rgyam lags kyang pheb pa phyag rdor thugs dam ma spus gtsang ba ster ba gnang
/ 'di lo bsam yas su mchod 'bul dang gnas gzigs la cis kyang 'ong dgos gnang byung bas de ga byed dgos 'dug zhus kyang / zla ba bzhi par sger pa nas bang phyin gnang
ba'i rgyal sras rin po che'ang pheb stabs chos bka' mang tsam zhu dgos bcas tshes ga tsam la gdan 'dren btang chog gi gsal dgos pheb par/ tshes bcu gsum la gnang na 'ong
zhus pa dus thog de gar pheb byung / blo gsal ni 'gro ma thub/ nged blo ldan gnyis/ dge slong tshul rgyam/ chos ldan bcas dang / sras po rta g.yog bcas tshes bcu gsum la
'di nas bteg /de nub lha rtser bsdad/ de nas tshong 'dus tshogs su zhag gcig /bco lnga'i nyin rtses dong brag gdong gzims spyil du thog mar phyin/ de'i sang nyin sger pa
rje dbon rin po che pheb nas/ rgyal sras rin po che ma phebs bar kha skong pusti/ zhal pod sogs lung mang du phul/ de nas rgyal sras rin po che'ang pheb pa'i thog mar gsang
'dus 'jam rdor gyi dbang ras bris la brten pa/ zhal bsnyen dus/ sgrub dus/ las sbyor/ gsang sgrub kyi rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa/ sgrub dus thun mong ma yin pa/ las
bzhi so so'i mgon po dang / srung 'khor tshe khrid thun mong ma yin pa/ gsang khrid shin tu smin pa/ gur gyi yang skong pusti'i lung / beg pod kyi lung / rta mgrin yang
gsang gi dbang / ging lnga gza' gdong gi

bka' gtad/ beg tse gtso rkyang gi bka' gtad/ rdzong chung tshe dbang / rta mgrin gsang sgrub kyi byin rlabs sogs mang bar phul/ rtses dong lnga mchod pa gling smad bka' bcu
pa dang / dbu mdzad nam mkha' sogs la rnam 'joms sogs dang / sme brtsegs kyi rjes gnang / gling smad bka' bcu par rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs dang / shar khrid/ 'bras gling
dpon slob dang / bka' ngag brtan sogs la rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs dang shar khrid/ mar bla ma la'ang yod/ sde pa rgya phrug pa sogs dang / lnga mchod 'bras gling sogs
nas pheb mi shin tu mang bar byung / 'di lo char pa dkon stabs char 'bebs dgos tshul gzhis bzhugs nas gsung ba ltar char rdzas sbas kyang rgyal po'i bkag bya che ba'i rlung
gis gtor ba 'ba' zhig byung bar/ do sngon gyi rtser dar lcog dmar po legs pa dang / gsol mchod/ gser skyems bcas 'bul bcug /de mthun gzims spyil thog nas dge slong lags
kyis gser skyems 'bul ba gnang / nged rang nas kyang dmigs phug gi gtor ma phul bas de nub sa sribs nas nam ma langs bar mtshan yal char pa shin tu che bar babs/ mi thams
cad bde la bkod/ khe gsum rtswa rar dpal li'i sog po rta gso ba 'ga' re na ba chibs dpon dbang grags kyis khrid nas byung bas bka' bsgo tshe dbang byas pas drag nas
dga' bar byed kyin 'dug /bkra shis chos sde nas dge slong kun mkhyen rin chen bya ma rtar byung bas cis kyang 'ong dgos tshul zer bar re zhig khas len mi bde byas kyang /
dpon rin po che rgyal sras

sku zhabs su pheb zhor du pheb pas 'ong dgos tshul dang / dge slong bsod nams rin chen gyis kyang u tshugs bcas na ning pheb gdong nas mkhas btsun gyi snyan gsan phab don ltar
da lam dam tshig thub byung bas ser tshogs kyi dbur cis kyang 'ong dgos/ grwa bsgrigs tshar zer bar zhag gcig 'ong bar khas blangs/ dbang drag sog po can la rta gsar
nas dus bsgrigs/ rgyal sras sku zhabs nas tshogs 'khor rgyas pa'i thog /phag mo'i sku rgyu legs pa/ kha btags che ba/ gser srang gang / dngul srang bdun/ gos chen dmar po
yug /dngul gyi bum pa 'bur ma/ rigs gsum dkyil thang / rtse zhwa legs pa sogs dpag med/ dge slong lags kyis ri bo chos gling nas len mi gnang ba'i gnas bcu'i sku/ thang
bris spus legs zhal khebs tog sogs bzang grub bcu gcig grwa tshar/ me tog bum pa brgyad gzhogs che legs tsha gser ma cha/ thang ka'i bzhugs sgam skyi btums ma sgo lcags lde
bcas cha/ bal zam khra bsgrigs kyi gnam rgyan gling gsum bcas gnang / de nas bkra shis chos sder phyin pa'i yar zhor khra 'brug na gar sog po rnams kyis zho dang ja sogs
zhus/ dngul dar sogs phul byung / de nas bkra shis zam pa thon mtshams su ser sbreng rgyas pa/ mgon khang thog nas dung rgya gling sogs rgyas pa/ dbon rin po che dang
gnyer pa sogs sne gdong gi thad du chibs bsur pheb/ de nyin rgyal sa sgang pa/ ras chung phug pa/ chos lung rab brtan pa/ shel brag pa sogs tshogs pa che bar 'dug /

thog mar sgo spe steng du bzhugs gral dang / de nas ser tshogs kyi tshogs dbur phyin/ bsngo ba rgyas par byas/ tshogs su ja mchod dus gsum rgyal ba ma gyer byung bas dga' spro
thob/ dbon rin po ches chos kyi dri ba brda chad chags pa 'dug cing / sang zhogs bla brang la dkar spro 'bul nod rgyas pa/ de nas 'du khang du bzhugs khri chen mo'i thog
tu bos/ spyi so'i ston mo 'bul ba dpag med byung / de nas u tshugs gnang byung kyang brel g.yeng stabs mchod mjal zhus nas thon 'ong / grwa dmangs shar gyi zhing steng
du skyel bar pheb/ dbon rin po che spyi sa bcas pas rta skyel du pheb/ bkra shis zam pa'i thad ka nas kha btags kyi g.yab mo gnang bar rta kha lan gsum bsgyur/ bkra shis
mthong smon du bos pas ster sbyin dang dkar spro rgyas par gnang / dbon rin po che dpon g.yog de nas phyir pheb/ de nub khe gsum du shog gnang phyin sde pa mchod dpon lags
kyang pheb 'dug /zangs par gling gi sbugs gzims chung shin tu spro bar 'dug pa der bsdad/ zhal ngo rnams dang / rgyal chen gyi sku rten pa bcas la tshe rta rgyas pa brgya
rtsa phul/ sang zhogs steng shod thams cad dang mgon khang bcas par khrus gsol dang me tog gtor/ spyi sger thams cad nas ther ma spus legs sogs gnang skyes dpag med
stsal/ de nub rtses dong du phyin/ rab 'byams pa ngag dbang bstan 'phel lags kyi sku 'khor thams cad la tshe dbang phul/ rab 'byams pa lags kyis ther ma sogs gnang byung
/ de nas sger par phyin/ rje btsun bgres pa rnal 'byor ma'i mtshams lo

gsum la bzhugs pa cung zhig ltem par tshe dbang bka' bsgo phul/ zhal ngo dmangs la gzims chung du 'chi med dpal ster gyi tshe dbang phul/ chos yon bla gos lu hang legs pa/
ja 'khor drug /gser sogs dpag med gnang / de nas tshogs 'dus su zhag tu bsdad/ lum gru gtong ma thub gshis rdor brag gi gru don de nub smad pa'i nang du bsdad/ sang nyin
snga bar 'ongs pas gung tshigs snga phyogs la 'byor/ 'phreng po dga' ldan gling du rgyal chen gyi gtsang khang la rab gnas zhu bar phyin/ gzhi pa grwa tshang du'ang 'bod
pa gnang / brtan bzhugs rgyas par byung / sde pa grwa tshang thams cad nas 'bul nod bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung / bsam yas pa drung 'tsho lags kyis yang bskyar dang / bka'
kun dga' don grub zhen che zhing ngar ba yod pa nas drung 'tsho lags dang mnyam du gsung 'phros byas pas/ da lam lam 'bras slob bshad cig ma byas pas dka' thebs med pas
'ong dgos shing dus kyang zla ba dgu pa rang la/ de min zla ba bcu pa tshun la ma tshugs pas dka' thebs med pa'i yi ge nan cher byung zhing / 'di lo mal gro ba rnams kyis
kyang 'ong dgos tshul byung bas de 'khor nas gsal len mi thong byas/ sbus sde nas sde pa khro phu nas kyis 'ong dgos tshul gnang ltar phyin/ yar lam lcags zam du zhag gcig
byas nas sbus sder yab sras gsum char bzhugs par phyag rdor 'byung 'dul/ gur khro bcu'i rjes gnang / brag rdzong ma'i shar khrid/ tshe rta sogs phul/ zhag gsum bsdad
nas mar

lam kyang lcags zam du tshe rta sogs chos spyod kyi lung dpon slob thams cad la lhan du phul/ de nas mal gror phyin pa'i yar lam snon gzhis kar zhal ngo rnams la tshe rta bya
bas khrus phul/ lha sa nas sde pa bka' blon lum pa nas kyis kyang 'ong dgos gnang ltar bkra shis bde legs su zhag gsum 'gor zhing tshe dbang brgya rtsa phul/ gang cis
bka' gleng gnang sbyar mang bar stsal/ de nas lha gdong brgyud mal gror slebs 'phral nas tshogs pa gdan 'dren gyi gral dbur 'gro nyag cig byas/ grwa pa rnams la mang ja bkras
btags re'i phyag 'gyed phul/ bar skabs su ma phyin pas skya ser thams cad nas gzhis len mi 'thob lta bur byung / rdzam chung bka' bcu pas sbyin bdag byas pa'i chos khri
thang du khrom dbang nyi ma gnyis byas/ zla ba gcig tsam 'gor zhing tshe dbang ma gtogs chos kyi rigs ma dgos pas skyid pa byung / sha mar thud gsum gyi gtsor gyur gyi
tshogs 'khor bcas brtan bzhugs byed mi mang bar byung / tshal pa khang gsar pa'i ma na ba'i ram pa khang gsar nas mar lam du 'ong dgos pa'i mi 'chad ka rang du byung /
tshar dgu nas kyang mar lam 'ong dgos pa dang / lhag tu sde pa bka' blon/ blo mkhar nas sogs snyan gsan 'bul mi shin tu mang bar byung / mal gro nas mar lam blo mkhar du
zhag gnyis bsdad/ de nas gzims khang shar pa rnams kyis bos pas gung tshigs byas/ mang ja sbugs chol sogs phul/ de nas blo mkhar tu'ang ram pa khang gsar rang du shar mar
'ong dgos pa'i bang phyin byung ba ltar shar mar phyin pas mthong gsal gnas tshang mi dga' bar dpe med byed 'dug /zhag lnga 'gor rin phan

tshun thams cad du nam langs sa rub lta bur 'gro dgos byung zhing / bka' blon nga phod pa'i der yang tshe dbang byas/ ja 'khor drug /mar ltang che ba/ 'bras ltang sogs dpe
med byung / dga' ldan khang gsar du grwa pa yongs rdzogs la 'chi med dpal ster dang / rta mgrin gsang sgrub kyi byin rlabs phul/ grwa pa thams cad thugs nang dag cing dam
tshig gtsang ba bcas 'bul spro bar byung / sde pa bka' lum ma bzhugs stabs bkra shis bde legs su 'gro ma dgos kyang / che gnyen mang por 'gro dgos byung bas sun par byung
/ 'bul nod ni tshad las 'das par byung / dge slong nam mkha' rgyal mtshan mtsho kha nas pheb pa'i ja mar ltos che ba/ gos yug rta sogs 'phyos ma che/ er ti ni sbo shog
thus kyang rta dang gos chen sogs byung / de nas tshag gur du zhag gnyis/ nang lhor zhag gcig /snon du zhag gnyis rnams 'gor bas rang gnas su 'byor/ bsam yas rab byung nas
yang bskyar byung bar zla ba dang po'i mjug tu 'ong bar khas blangs/ tshes bco brgyad la bteg pas de nub sbrags mdar bsdad/ sang nyin lding dpon gyis grwa rab mdar gro
bteg pa'i zur khang du drung 'tsho kun dga' rgyal mtshan lags/ bka' bcu kun bzang don grub bcas gsol ja dang rta bsur pheb/ shar mar dbu rtser drung 'tsho lags kyi shag tu
sdod sa byas/ nyi ma gnyis nye bsdogs byas nas chu stag hor zla dang por rang lo re dgu par slebs pa'i nyer gcig gi gza' tshes lo paN rgyal blon thams cad kyis byin gyis
brlabs shing stan chags pa dbu

rtse'i bar khang g.yu zhal du 'dus pa'i gtso bo gnas gsar dbon rin po che kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ shing mang dpon slob sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ chos 'khor gnas dpon
slob zur pa/ gzhi pa dpon slob phun tshogs legs ldan sogs bla ma'i tshogs dang / gzhi pa drug /ra ba smad rab 'byams pa ngag dbang tshe brtan/ tsha pa dbon po/ byams gling
sgrub sde ba bdun/ bye rdzing tshogs pa bcu gcig /bkra shis chos sde pa bzhi/ rmor pa gnyis/ se ra ba gnyis/ mdo gling pa bcu gcig /ri bo bde chen pa gnyis/ shing mang
rab 'byams pa bstan pa bkra shis/ btsun chung slob dpon sogs gnyug mar gnas pa brgyar nye ba bcas khyon phyed nyis brgya skor la/ gsung ngag rin po che slob bshad kyi khrid
shin tu smin pa tshogs bshad sogs kyi bsre lhad med pa snang gsum zhag bco lnga skor dang / byang chub chen po'i sku mdun du sngar gyi slob ma rnams kyi steng du zhal
ngo bgres pa lags sogs skya ser gyi 'dus pa shin tu che bar mchod pa'i rgya dpangs che ba bcas brgyud pa'i khyad par nyis ldan gyis sems bskyed/ de nub bar khang du slob
ma rjes 'dzin grub nas bum pa la brten pa'i bsnyen pa kha gso zhag bdun gyi bar du byas/ thun mtshams su dpon slob sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan la sngar ma gsan pa'i dmar po
skor gsum gyi rjes gnang gi rigs sogs phul/ de nas rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang cha bcad pa'i nyis brgya skor dgos byung zhing / dbang stegs kyi dkyil 'khor kyang
rdul tshon bzhengs par dbon rin po che bzhugs/ lam zab phyi nang / bir srung phyi nang / bla ma rin

'byung / tshar gsum khug pa sogs btang / lam dbang bskur ba'i phyi nang bskyed rim/ dbang bzhi so sor lam/ lta ba/ grub mtha'/ 'da' kha ma/ bar do/ sgyu lus/ rmi lam sogs chad
med dang / bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar gyi lung la snga chos la rjes gnang gi rigs kyang ma chags par bgyis/ bar skabs su'ang zhal ngo sku rten par rnal 'byor ma'i byin
rlabs shar khrid/ nyer mkho'i rjes gnang rigs mang bar phul/ sde pa khro phu nas dang / rab brtan rdo rje lags la'ang tshe rta phyag rdor sogs phul/ bar bar du srang
kha gnang / srang mdo ba/ bu tshal/ chu 'khor ba sogs mang por yang tshe dbang sogs la phyin/ slob ma rnams kyis tshe dpag med kyi cho ga dang 'brel pa'i brtan bzhugs jo
bo'i sku mdun rab byung ba'i tshogs khang du rgyas par 'bul ba gnang / snga phyi phyogs 'dus dang gtso bor rab byung pa thams cad kyis gser dngul/ gos dar/ sku 'dra/ rdor
dril sogs tshad 'das 'bul ba gnang byung / zhal ngo sku rten pa lags kyis lcog tu sku 'dra gsar bzhengs gnang bar rab gnas la 'bod pa gnang / rab byung dbu mdzad sogs nyi
shu skor gyis kye rdor la brten pa'i rab gnas nyin gang ma rgyas par byas/ rab ston 'bul ba ha las par byung / tshogs pa thams cad la byin rlabs sngon du 'gro ba'i rnal
'byor ma'i khrid rgyas pa bdun phrag gcig gi bar byas/ dge slong bsam 'phel sogs grwa tshang gi grwa pa bdun tsam yod/ nged rang gis mkhan po/ dpon slob sangs rgyas rgyal
mtshan gyis las slob/

chos 'khor dpon slob kyis gsang ston/ bzhi pa dpon slob kyis dus bsgo ba/ dge slong tshul khrims rgya mtsho lags dang drung 'tsho lags kyis kha skong gnang nas dbon rin po
che gtso bor gyur pa'i sgrub tsho bcu gnyis la bsnyen rdzogs byas/ dge tshul brgyad cu skor bsgrubs/ 'dzugs ston drung 'tsho lags kyis rgyas pa dang / grol ston bka' bcu
kun bzang don grub kyis zhus/ drung 'tsho lags kyis sman rgyal gyi sku rgya nag ma/ bla bre 'gangs che bas gtsos pa'i 'bul dpangs che ba/ bka' kun don gyis dngul dang ja
'khor drug sogs dpangs mtho ba/ bkra shis rab brtan gyis chos zhu ba thams cad la ston mo/ stod ja'i 'gyed 'bul dpangs mtho ba/ grwa pa so sos spyi mjal sger mjal sogs shin
tu zab par byung / rnam sras gling nas 'ong dgos tshul gnang ltar khas len zhus nas phyin/ sga mkhan gyis sga gsar bzos byas par zhal ngo sku rten pa lags kyis sga chas
cha 'grigs kha khebs dang bcas gnang nas gnam gling du bstod dgos gnang zhing bstad/ gnam gling du zhag gnyis bsdad/ zhal ngo rnams la tshe rta brgya tshar/ rnam 'joms
kyi byabs khrus/ phyag mdzod du dzam lha dang dbyu gu ma'i rten 'dzugs rgyas par zhus/ phyug po dgon pa ba grangs bcad la kun rig gi dbang cha gnyis bskur/ snga sor 'di ga'i
dpe cha 'khyar ba pusti gsum lag tu byung / dpon g.yog thams cad nas bsnyen bkur zab pa dang / lags dpal skyabs kyi nang du tshe rta bka' bsgo sogs byas nas bsam yas
rang du sleb/ sang nyin mchod rten dmar po shog gnang ltar phyin/ zhal ngo rnams la tshe rta

brgya rtsa/ dmangs la tshe dbang phul/ snga rting du gos chen gyi 'gan sbyar/ rgyan bzhi'i gos ber/ pang khebs spus gtsang ba/ spyan ras gzigs kyi ldem sku dzhai kShiM/ tshe
dpag med kyi gser sku sogs dpe med stsal/ sang nyin chos mjal zhus pa'i lha khang so sor mchod pa sna lnga/ dbu rtser brgya mchod/ snyan shal sogs phul zhing / lha khang
so sor smon lam rgyas par btab/ sde pa khrus phu nas dang rab brtan lags gnyis kyang mchod mjal la pheb yod/ rab byung par mang ja 'gyed zla ba byung ngo cog gi gnam gang
la drin can rdo rje 'chang gi sku mchod la dmigs nas dngul srang sum cu phul/ snga sor bka' blon shag nas gzhung sa'i dmar po skor gsum gyi sgrub pa la 'ong dgos tshul
gyi bka' rgya pheb don ltar 'gro rtsis la/ bkra shis bde legs nas sde pa gzims dpon lags sku ltem pa'i 'phral rang du 'ong dgos pa'i tsha nan bcas pheb gshis tshes dgu la
thon pas rab byung mkhan po/ mkhan tshang drung rams pa/ dbu chos gnyer pa/ dpon slob sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan sogs kyis chibs skyel dang / grwa dmangs yongs rdzogs/ spyi
sas thab bteg pas khams gsum na kha bsgral ba'i mtshams su pheb/ mkhan po sogs de nas phyir pheb/ drung 'tsho lags/ bka' kun bzang don grub/ bkras rab lags/ 'jam dbyangs
yar 'phel lags/ spyi sa drung 'tsho tshul bstan sogs zur mkhar bar skyel bar pheb/ de nas khong dpon slob phyir pheb/ nged rang gis yar 'ong / g.yab mo byung bar rta kha
lan gsum bsgyur/ de

nub sgrags mdar bsdad/ sang nyin rdor brag gnyer pa chu so khar ja dang bcas pa'i klu sdings su dkar spro rgyas par 'dug /de nas zhag gnyis ngal bsos/ lha sar phyin pa'i yar
lam snon du zhag gcig byas nas bkra shis bde legs su phyin/ sde pa bka' blon yab sras thams cad la tshe dbang / rta mgrin gyi rjes gnang phul/ sde gzims rgyal po'i gnod
pa yin 'dug pas gsol mchod dang bka' bsgo phul bas dwangs skyed che bar byung / zhag gsum thog bkra shis bde legs su rgyal phur 'grub sbyor 'dzoms thog gzhung gi dmar po
skor gsum gyi 'khor lo mkhyen rab lags mtshams 'og tu bzhag pa'i phyag bris rung bar gnang / rtags kyang shin tu legs par byung / bdun gcig gi bar sgrub pa tshul bzhin bgyis/
rab gnas kyang gzhan gyis rgyas bkab ma yin par so so'i lugs ltar bgyis nas dngul gyi mgul gwa bsngags bzos gnang bar bcug /gza' tshes legs par phul zhing / grol mkhar
sde pa/ gzims dpon/ bka' blon gnyis bcas par dmar po skor gsum gyi rjes gnang kyang phul/ de grol nas sde pa gzims dpon lags kyi sku rim du sgrol dkar dang rta mgrin
gnyis snga dro phyi red bgyis pa'i bdun gcig byas grol/ sde pa gzims dpon lags/ sde pa bka' blon gung / se pe bcas par sgrol dkar gyi tshe dbang dang / rta mgrin gyi byin
rlabs phul/ de nas sde pa rdo rje rgyal po lags kyi gzims khang du zhag lnga bsdad/ tshe dbang / 'jam dpal nag po/ khyung khra'i rjes gnang rnams phul/ rnam 'joms

dang sme brtsegs kyi byabs khrus rgyas pa nyin re bzhin re mos kyis phul/ tshur lam zur khang du 'ong / ir ti ni sbo shog thus bla brang rnying par bos/ sha ston dang dngul
srang bcu/ kha btags sogs byin byung / nga phod nor nor lags gshegs pa'i byang bzhu zhu dgos byung bar dngul srang bco lnga/ chung ja 'khor drug ma/ gos chen gyi rtsag pa
sogs dpangs che bar 'dug /ra mthil/ ram pa khang gsar sogs su'ang 'gro dgos dang / chu bzang nas tshangs dbyangs rta mgrin pheb par nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs khrid
shar/ rnam 'joms kyi byabs khrus rnams phul/ gser dngul gos yug sogs dpangs mtho bar 'dug /de nas bka' blon zhal ngo gnyis nas gser dngul/ ja/ mar ltang sogs dpag med
byung ba rnyed pa 'tshol mkhan gyi dpe thub par byung / rim gyis ta nang lho/ snon rnams su tshe rta byabs khrus phul/ 'phreng gong gsal sgang du gdugs dkar gyi rjes gnang
bgyis nas rang gnas su slebs/ 'di dag gi snga phyi thams cad du lho brag pa bka' bcu kun dga' bsam 'grub kyis lam 'bras slob bshad pusti che ba gnyis/ tshogs bshad pusti
che ba gcig /chos 'byung brgya rtsa pusti gcig rjes gnang pusti gnyis/ 'jigs byed kyi tshar pod pusti gcig /brtag gnyis gser gyi pod chung gcig /gser chos pusti gcig /rdo
rje phreng ba'i mdzes rgyan rnams bzhengs/ gung thang grags pa don grub dang / bstan 'dzin rig 'dzin bcas 'ong / ra ba smad dpon

slob zal phu nas pheb pa'i las slob dang gsang ston sbrags/ sangs rgyas rgya mtsho dang kun dga' bstan 'phel bcas kha skong byas nas gung thang pa gnyis la bsnyen rdzogs byas/
rgya mtsho mdo khams spo bo nas 'khor ba'i sngar ma thos pa'i tshar lugs kyi chos bka' gang thob dgos tshul byung / lha sa nas dpal li'i tshe sgrub bdun gsum dgos pa
'phral rang du tshugs dgos byung gshis ra ba smad dpon slob dang rgya mtsho mtshams 'og tu bzhag /mtshams bsdams/ de nas skyid gshongs nas dpon slob kyang pheb/ rnam ser
drung chen gshegs pa'i sreg chog sogs la 'ong dgos tshul byung yang mtshams dang thug pas 'gro ma thub/ dpon slob rgya mtsho bcas la mgon po'i snyan brgyud pusti/ kha skong
pusti/ me 'bar ma rnams kyi lung bklags/ chab nag ri bo dga' ldan gyi mkhan po zur pa/ ser dpon slob chos mdzad/ rab 'byams pa mgon po/ bdud 'joms gling pa blo bzang phun
tshogs bcas la 'khor lo bde mchog dril bu lha lnga'i dbang ras bris la brten pa/ rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs sngon du 'gro ba'i khrid smin par zhal shes kyis brgyan pa/
yab yum thun mong ma yin pa'i 'pho ba rnams/ gong steng du mgar rtse bsam gtan chos 'khor ba'i btsun ma brgyad/ bka' phun tshogs grags pa bcas la mi 'khrugs pa lha dgu'i
dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba/ spyan ras gzigs kyi rjes gnang / tshems bu lugs kyi dmar khrid rgyas pa/ grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe dbang / yang shel grong pa a'o bstan 'dzin
can la 'chi

med dpal ster gyi tshe dbang rnams/ gong gi chab nag mkhan po gsum/ dge slong tshul khrims rgya mtsho lags/ sde dge sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ bka' bcu kun dga' bsam 'grub/ ngag
dbang chos grags bcas la 'jigs byed bcu gsum ma'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du tshar lugs thun mong ma yin pa'i dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs pa/ se ra ba gsum/ chos dbang
/ ngag chos bcas la rwa khrid shin tu rgyas pa bskyed rdzogs tshang ba/ kye rdor gyi ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba bcas song / rnal 'byor ma'i khrid la lcags
zam pa bsod nams rin chen kyang yod/ yang skyor mo lung mkhan po ra tshar khu thug thu dga' ldan byang rtse'i rab 'byams pa blo bzang rgyal mtshan sogs dpon g.yog bzhi
pheb pa 'jigs byed kyi dbang la yod cing / khong dpon slob bzhi/ se ra ba gsum/ dge slong lags/ bka' drung yig /ngag chos rgya mtsho/ kun dga' dbang phyug /chos grags/ dpal
ldan lags bcas par nai gu'i khrid smin rgyas phul/ dmar po skor gsum gyi rjes gnang dkon mchog lhun grub pa'i yi ge'i steng dang / dzam dmar srog sgrub kyi rjes gnang
lung bcas/ rnam rgyal lha dgu /sme brtsegs ljang nag gi rjes gnang bcas song / de steng 'bras spungs pa'i grwa pa rab 'byams pa gsum la rnam 'joms kyi rjes gnang / dbyangs
can ma dkar dmar/ yang dag gi ras dbang / beng dmar nag gi rjes gnang bcas song / yang rgyal sras sprul

pa'i sku dang / sger pa rje dpon rin po che pheb par tshe dbang grub rgyal lugs/ rdo rje gdan pa'i chos drug gi nang tshan 'od zer can ma gtso rkyang gi rjes gnang lung bcas/
rta mgrin gsang sgrub kyi byin rlabs rnams phul zhing / rje btsun sgrol ma'i gser sku/ kha btags che legs/ dngul gyi maNDal/ gser/ ther srab/ gos yug ser po spus legs/
gos chen gyi pang khebs sogs dpag med bstar/ khu thug thus kyang kha btags dngul sogs rnyed pa mang du bstar ro/ /dge slong tshul khrims rgya mtsho lags bka' bcu kun dga'
bsam 'grub bcas la las gshin phyi nang / tshe dpag med 'chi bdag 'joms pa'i dbang lung bcas phul/ hor zla brgyad par rnam sras gling nas sprul sku mkhar khyim pa bos pas
dngul bum cha/ dngul gyi maNDal/ ka li nang shan/ khebs/ stegs/ mchod kong sogs gsar du bzos/ lha sar em phyi rag kha chu 'khor bas dus gsum sangs rgyas sogs sku bcu tsam
bzhengs par gzungs 'bul rab gnas sogs la phyin/ de zhor du nag tshang byang du bka' blon so so'i sku zhabs su'ang zhag shas bsdad/ tshe rta dang / mdo mkhar nas zhabs
drung tshe ring dbang rgyal pheb par bde mchog lU hi pa'i dbang dang rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs sngon du 'gro ba'i khrid smin rgyas phul/ sde dge ba lhun grub chos 'byor
ba'ang mnyam du yod/ sde pa mkhyen pa gzhan dang ma 'dra gshis dmigs pa rnams thugs la nges par byung song / thob yig sogs kyi mgo brjod la

bi brta'ang 'phral 'phral du gnang / bka' bcu kun dga' bsam 'grub kyis nged rang gi 'khrul gtam ring mo dang / sgrub thabs brgya rtsa sogs phyag bris gnang / rnam sras gling
lags pad skyabs bos pa'i tsakli brgya skor spus gtsang bar bzhengs/ bkra shis dpal ri'i chos mdzad sku gzhon pa ngag dbang 'jam dpal pheb par rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs
sngon du 'gro ba'i khrid zhal shes gsum gyis brgyan pa smin rgyas dang / rig byed ma/ tshogs bdag /'dod rgyal gsum gyi rjes gnang dang / mkha' spyod ma'i be'u bum nas lung
mang bar phul/ bka' blon gung sde gzims bcas pheb par tshe rta brgya rtsa dang / bka' bsgo rgyas pa bcas phul zhing gang ci'i gsung gleng bag pheb par byung / de mtshungs
zla dpon blo bzang dar rgyas kyang pheb par byad 'grol/ tshe rta brgya tshar sogs phul/ snon du chos drung lags rgyal gdon gyis sku ltem par tshe rta brgya tshar/ byabs
khrus sogs phul nas zla ba bcu pa 'di'i tshes nas lo bstar gyi sku rim ser tshogs byas/ 'di lo mda' phu bsam gtan chos gling pa'ang yod/ zla mjug tu gzhung sa'i sku rim
kye rdor gyi zhi ba'i sbyin sreg smin rgyas bgyis pa'i rdor slob tu phyin/ zhag bdun gyi bar bgyis/ zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i mgor sbus sder mo che ba'i pha 'das pa'i byang
chog bgyid par phyin zhing / mar lam lcags zam du sprul sku rin po cher tshe rta sogs phul/ 'phreng sgo zur khang du rgyal chen gyi sku brnyan bzhengs pa'i gzungs rab gnas
sogs la phyin/ rgyal chen sku brlabs pa'i rnam 'gyur mdzad/ yang

snon du chos drung lags zhal ma 'tsho ba'i zhugs 'bul la 'ong dgos tshul pheb par brten gshegs bzhugs thams cad kyi thugs 'dod bskang phyir 'gro dgos byung bar kun rig gi sgo
nas sbyor dngos mjug tshang gi me mchod rgyas par phul/ chibs legs pa sogs gnang skyes dmar bar byung / snga gong nas yang yang bang phyin gnang ba'i skyid gshongs ra
ba smad nas grwa dpon slob/ khams nas 'bul dpon lhun grub chos 'byor sogs thams cad kyis rten 'brel gyi khyad nas brtan bzhugs shig byed rtsis yin pas cis kyang 'ong dgos
pheb par brten hor zla bcu gcig pa'i tshes gsum la phyin/ gru khar spyi bla brang 'bul dpon sogs chibs bsur 'dug cing / tshes bzhi'i nyin 'du khang du mgon po tshe dpag
med kyi gsung chog nged rang gi gsar bsgrig steng nas rgyas par gnang / sku gsung thugs rten/ rgyal srid sna bdun/ bkra shis rdzas brgyad 'bul ba sogs dpon slob kyis gsung
bshad rgyas pa dang bcas stsal/ khyad par bla ma lhun grub chos 'byor gyis gser/ dngul/ ja/ dre'u sogs dang / byams pas tshogs la 'gyed/ sger 'bul rab 'byams pa ngag dbang
tshe brtan spun ston mo zab pa/ 'bul dpangs mtho ba bcas rten 'brel phun sum tshogs par byung / de grol nas rdo gcal du zhol gyi tshes bcu pa khag rnams kyi sbyin bdag
mdzad nas grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe dbang bgyis par mi tshogs shin tu che zhing / chos skyong chen po'ang sku chas gzab 'chor bcas pheb nas/ gongs pheb dus dang mtshungs
pa'i bkur

bzos/ phyag mtshan rgyal mtshan dang kha btags che ba bcas lag tu gtod pa gnang / ma grol bar du bzhugs/ de nub yas mas kyi skya ser 'phrad mi mang bar pheb/ 'bul dpon pa khag
sogs la lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang byas/ sang zhogs lcog tu sger nas spyan 'dren zhus par chos skyong chen po rdo stegs mgor bsu bar pheb/ gtsang khang du khri'u shing
gi khar stag lpags bting nas 'bod pa gnang / lkog 'gyur gyi bslab don bag pheb par gnang zhing phyag gi zhags pa dang / kha btags gnang / lus dang grib ma ltar mi 'bral
bar zhal gyis bzhes nas skas gsham thug skyel bar pheb/ sang nyin spyi bla brang sku rten pa lags bcas gru kha thug skyel bar pheb nas rang gnas su 'byor/ de nas hor zla
bcu gnyis pa'i nang du sde pa bka' blon thun mong nas phyag bris nan chen pheb pa'i 'phral rang du 'ong dgos tshul gnang ba ltar zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i tshes nyer gsum nyin
thon par/ de nub snye phu lhom pa'i ma 'das pa'i dbang bskur sogs la 'ong dgos tshul nan ches pa'i stabs de nub snye phur bsdad/ byang chog /dbang bskur/ lam ston sogs
smin rgyas bgyis/ sang nyin thon/ yar lam snon du zhag gnyis 'gor/ de nas shar mar lha ldan bkra shis bde legs su phyin/ thog mar sku zhabs rin po che'i zhabs brtan la dmigs
nas rgya can gyi tshe dpag med 'chi med bdud 'joms kyi sgo nas bdun phrag gcig gi bar sku tshe tshe sgrub zhus/ grol skabs sde pa gung dang yum sras lhan rgyas bcas la
tshe dbang rnams brgya tshar dang /

'chi med dpal ster gyi sgo nas kyang brgya tshar phul/ rgya can snying po lha gsum gyi dbang / de dang rjes 'brel gyi byad 'grol kyang phul/ sde pa mda' dpon o rang pa la'ang
gong gsal gyi tshe dbang rnams brgya tshar phul zhing / rnam gling zhabs drung rgyal bu'i drung kyang pheb yod/ khyon zhag dgu 'gor/ de nas dpal 'byor rab brtan du sde
pa so so'i sku zhabs su'ang zhag bcu tsam 'gor/ nyin bstar gyi tshe dbang rigs mi gcig pa brgya tshar re zhal ngo bgres gzhon dgu char la phul/ sku zhabs rin po che'i zhal
mjal/ phyag dbang la rtser phyin/ de nyin 'bras spungs kyi bla khag /se ra/ dge ldan bcas pa'i bla ma dge bskos dbu mdzad sogs dang mjal kha lhan du byung / sum ldan sogs
bdag rkyen che bar gnang / bka' 'dri yang bka' drin bskyangs/ tshes bcu bzhir sde pa so so'i zhabs brtan chen mo'i mgron du'ang 'bod pa gnang / gral mgo zhig tu gdan
bzos dang / ston mo dpangs mtho bar 'dug cing / gong zhabs nas gsol ras kyang rgyas par gnang byung / de dus yab rje sku zhabs nas kyang dpal 'byor rab brtan du pheb pa'i
tshe dbang gang zab zhig dgos pheb par rgya chen 'chi bdag 'joms kyi byabs khrus rgyas pa/ phyag g.yog la drung yig chos mdzad yod/ de'i sang nyin 'chi med dga' tshal/ rgyal
yum sku zhabs la byabs khrus dang sku tshe tshe dbang dgos pheb ltar rnam 'joms kyi byabs khrus rgyas pa/ 'chi med dpal ster gyi tshe dbang brgya tshar bcas/ skal bzang
lags yum sras lhan rgyas la phul/ sku cung zad ltem par zhag bdun gyi bar du chu bzang du tshe sgrub cig kyang

dgos tshul pheb pa ltar yo byad rnams chu bzang chos rje tshangs dbyangs rta mgrin lags la bslab ston gnang ba tshes bco brgyad nas chu bzang du phyin pa'i 'chi med dpal ster
dang 'chi bdag 'joms pa gnyis snga dro dang phyi red du bgyis pa rim 'gyangs su song ba'i bdun gnyis tsam dgos byung zhing / chos skyong chen pos kyang kha btags legs
pa dang / dbu bsdoms legs pa sogs gnang / mchod gtor ma chag par dgos tshul dang / blang dor gyi lung bstan gsal por gnang / thun mtshams kyi srub dbar la chos rje lags sku
'khor bcas par rgya can gro lod dang / 'jig rten dbang phyug /byang gter thang lha'i srog gtad/ 'chi bdag 'joms kyi tshe dbang sogs phul/ grol gdong chu bzang gi rab 'byams
pa ngag dbang grags par rta mgrin yang gsang gi cha lags/ rdzong chung tshe'i dbang bskur/ de dus se rar bka' 'gyur gyi lung tshugs par 'ga' zhig gi dbang ma thob par
rgyud 'bum gyi lung gsan ma thub gshis/ bde mchog gi dbang zhig cis kyang dgos gnang ba'i dge slong sgros pa 'ba' zhig 'dug gshis dka' tshegs la ma 'dzems par grwa pa
bco lnga skor la nub dang po sta gon dang / gnyis tho rengs nas bdag 'jug blangs pa'i bde mchog lU hi pa'i dbang ras bris la brten pa sla chos su ma song bar rgyas par phul/
chu bzang du sdod khang spro zhing chos rje lags nas zhabs tog sogs rgyas par gnang gshis so bsod pa skyid par byung / spro bde khang gsar pa'i a ce skyid 'dzom gdon
zhud kyis ltem par byung ba'i

rkyen sel du sgrol dkar gyi 'chi bslu'i sbyin sreg dgos tshul nan ches par thun mtshams su bgyis par ngo shin tu che ba byung 'dug /rgyal yum sku zhabs nas mar lam lha klu'i
dga' tshal du tshe dbang dang byad 'grol byed pa dang bcas zhag gnyis ma bsdad pas mi 'ong pheb/ 'ong gdong chos rje lags kyis sbugs chol rnying ma dang / sil snyan legs
pa/ gos dar la sogs pa dpag med stsal/ chos rje lags kyang pheb pas dga' tshal tu shar mar phyin/ zhag gnyis kyi bar tshe dbang brgya tshar dang / byad 'grol/ thang lha'i
srog gtad sogs phul bas sku dwangs bskyed kyang che bar byung zhing / hu ja 'khor drug /gos yug /ling yug sogs dpangs mtho bar gnang / shin tu dgyes par gyur/ de nas dpal
'byor rab brtan du phyin/ zhag gnyis kyi bar tshe rta brgya tshar phul ba'i mur/ lha klu dga' tshal du rgyal yum sku ltem du song bas da lam 'phral mar 'gro dgos pa'i
gong zhabs rin po che'i bslab ston bsgyur bar sde pa phug nas pheb par skur nyin pa rang med na tshes grangs dang gang sa'i rten 'brel bcas sang nyin yong dgos zhus pas
de ga legs tshul pheb/ sang nyi shar la phyin/ sku zhud kyis ltem babs lci bar 'dug par thog mar tshe rta brgya tshar phul/ re zhig sdod dgos pheb pas bka' ldog ma nus/ steng
gi gzims chung du bsdad/ nyin bstar gyi byabs khrus/ tshe dbang rigs mi gcig pa/ rjes gnang gi rigs sogs chag med du yum sras lhan du phul/ sku khams kyang rim bde byung
kyang zhag bco brgyad song nub rkyen gdon zhud lta bus

zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes nyer gcig gi nub sku tshes ma zin par sku la bsnyun zug sogs gang yang med par gshegs/ nyin snga ma rnams su chos bka' phul ba rnams kyang thugs la
'jags par byung song gshis thugs dam gsal 'debs/ gnas spar sogs zhus pa dang gzhan dang ma 'dra ba'i mnal du byung song / de nas yab rje sku zhabs dang / skal bzang lags
lhan rgyas thog nas sku tshigs bdun ma tshar bar du sdod dgos nan cher pheb gshis re zhig zhu len 'bul ma bde bas nyin bstar kun rig gi cho ga lho sgo dang 'brel ba sku gdung
ma pheb bar nyin bstar dbang bskur gsal 'debs zhus/ de nas bsam yas su rdor phreng gsan mi rnams 'dzom ches pas dgongs khrol zhus pas 'di gar yang rdor phreng tshar
gcig dgos pheb par bco brgyad nas dkyil thang dang phyag dpe g.yar zhus kyis nyin bstar rdor phreng gi dkyil 'khor gsum bzhi re zhal phye ba'i sku zhang lags/ sro me lags
gnyis/ gtso bor skal bzang lags/ chu bzang chos rje lags bcas dang / bde mchog gi skabs su sde pa gung gi sras mo chos lags kyang yod/ mjug tu dge legs su byed pa'i dkyil
'khor gsum la yab rje'ang pheb/ khyon sta gon the ba'i nyin bcu gcig la phreng ba'i dkyil 'khor zhe gnyis kyi steng du kr-i ya'i bde legs su byed pa'i dkyil 'khor gsum
bcas khyon dkyil 'khor zhe lnga'i dbang bskur ba gegs med du phul zhing cho ga tshar re la'ang sku rus la khrus chog sogs rgyas par zhus/ de nas zhag bdun drug gi thog tu
grol ba gnang rgyu nyer dgu'i nyin yin kyang / nyin drug la dgongs pa

khrol ba'i gser dngul/ ja/ gos dar/ chibs sga/ 'khor sogs rgya che ba bka' drin stsal/ bsam yas su rdor phreng gi ring sdod gnas bzan shing sogs mkho rgu'i yo byad gang dgos
'ong ba'i bka' drin stsal/ nyin drug gi nyin dpal 'byor rab brtan du phyin pa'i zhag gnyis 'gor ring sde pa so so'i zhal ngo rnams la tshe rta brgya tshar lan gsum phul/
rag em phyi/ spro sde khang gsar/ kun bzang rtse/ ram pa khang gsar rnams su'ang nyin 'khor gyi tshe rta sogs bgyis de nas bkra shis bde legs su'ang zhag gnyis 'gor ring
zhal ngo rnams la tshe rta/ byabs khrus sogs brgya tshar phul/ sde pa bka' blon gnyis char nas ja 'khor drug /gos yug sogs dpag med gnang / 'dod yon kho na don du gnyer
ba rnams la 'di rigs shin tu mkho'ang mkho ste byung yang byung ste/ sngo nas sbyin 'bras yin na ma gtogs sku khres re lji rang byung song / dus 'di dag gi gnas tshul la
bsams na 'di tsam thob ste/ e ma/ sngon bsags kyi las 'phro mthu btsan pas/ /las ma myongs bya ba'i dgu gcig myong / /dus re 'ga' skyid pa'i nyi ma shar/ /dus re 'ga' sna
tshogs kyi sdug bsngal myong / /de dag gi gnas tshul la legs bsams na/ /bde ba rnams dkon mchog gi thugs rjer nges/ /sdug bsngal rnams rang gi las 'bras yin/ /de shes na
'dun ma'i yang rtser son/ /de nas lha ldan nas thon nub sne'u nang lhor zhi ba'i sbyin sreg dang tshe rta sogs bgyis/ zhag gcig 'gor/ mar lam snon du zhag gnyis bsdad pas
zhal ngo tshor byabs khrus tshe rta brgya rtsa sogs phul/

'phreng gong gsal sgang du dbang byas/ gung tshigs thon nas bye la brgyud rang gnas su 'byor/ zhag dgu tsam gyi ring ngal bsos/ de nas bsam yas kyi yang bskyar bang phyin byung
ba'i tshes bcu gnyis la bteg /blo gsal yang skyel mar yod cing / rdor brag klu sdings su zur khang nas thab bsu gnang ba'i rgyas par 'dug cing / sde pa rdo rje rnam
rgyal yang pheb par gang ci'i gsung gleng 'phel bar byung / 'phreng po mdar rdor brag gnyer tshang dge slong rnams mkhyen ja 'drin du gnang bar cung zhig 'gor/ de nub sgrags
mdar phyin pas lding dpon dang / lags sogs ri gdong du pheb pa'i sgrags mda'i rdzing gsar par nas 'thor dgos tshul gsung ba ltar rdzing la ye dhar gyis byin gyis brlabs
pa'i me tog gtor/ de nub lding dpon gyi nang du bsdad/ sang nyin sgrags mda'i lding dpon gyis grwa rab kyi mdar gung tshigs bstar/ de nas zur mkhar du zhal ngo sku rten
pa lags/ drung 'tsho kun rgyal lags/ bka' kun don/ rab byung gnyer pa sogs bsu bar pheb 'dug cing / der gsol ja 'dug par bsil grib tu brgyangs par bzhugs/ rim gyis bteg
pas khams gsum na khar slebs dus su rtse thog nas dung chen rgya gling dang / grwa dmangs phyogs kyi chos gsan pa dang bcas shin tu mang bas mdun bsus te shar mar pe har
lcog tu phyin/ bla ma lha khang du sdod sa byas/ de'i sang nyin nas nyer bsdogs bgyis pa'i sa ga'i bcu bzhi'i nyin pe har lcog gis khyams su rab byung ba'i mkhan po/ mkhan
tshang rab 'byams pa/ dpon sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ zhal ngo sku rten

pa lags sogs rab byung yongs rdzogs kyi steng / bye rdzing tshogs mkhan pos thog drangs pa bcu gsum/ dol chos 'khor nas rab 'byams pa kun dga' bsam gtan sogs bco lnga/ gsang
phu gzhi pa nas dbu mdzad sogs drug /myong bran chu bzang nas rab 'byams pa ngag dbang grags pa sogs drug /khyung tshang bla ma zur pa/ kong po sku skye sogs bcu gcig /se
ra nas dpon slob chos mdzad sogs bzhi/ rme ru nas bla ma zur pa sogs bzhi/ gzhi sde pa gnyis/ zur mkhar mdo gling pa bcu/ rtses dong lnga mchod pa'i las chen gzhon pa/
gangs can mkhan po zur pa/ rab 'byams pa rgyal po sogs ri bo bde chen pa bco lnga/ sde pa khrus bu nas kun dga' rgya mtsho yab sras gnyis/ shel grong gsang sngags gling
pa em phyi kun dga' bstan 'phel can sogs gsum/ kun dga' dbang phyug /chos grags sogs rmor pa drug /bsam yas rdzong dpon sde pa/ dge slong ye shes rgya mtsho dang / em phyi
lags/ gung thang nas shing mang slob dpon zur pa dam chos kun bzang gnyis/ lcags zam nas padma kun gsal spun gnyis dang / blo gsal phrin las/ shing mang nas rab 'byams
pa bstan pa bkra shis sogs skya ser khyon bsdoms stong dang nyis brgya skor la grub pa'i slob dpon chen po a bha yA ka ra'i bzhed srol thun mong ma yin pa rdo rje phreng
ba nas bshad pa'i dkyil 'khor zhe gnyis kyi steng du/ paNDi ta chen po darpan a tsArYa'i bzhed pa dge legs su byed pa'i dkyil 'khor gsum bcas khyon zhe lnga'i sta gon dam
pa'i phyag bzhes ltar sla chos su ma song bar bgyis/

de'i sang nyin nam mthong zla ba'i dus chen sum 'dzom gyis 'jam dpal rdo rje lha bcu dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dbang don dag bya dag byed ngo 'phrod nges kyi dbang
bskur ba nas rim gyis phul bar rgyal yum gyi dgongs rdzogs su dmigs pa'i nyin rer mang ja bzang ba re dang bzhes thug re ma grol bar du gnang zhing / de steng du thog mar
sbyin bdag bka' bcu kun bzang don grub kyis 'dzugs ja bzang bar mdzad/ nyin bstar gyis phyogs 'dus rang grwa bcas pa thams cad kyis mang ja bzhes thug nyin rer gsum bzhi
re ma chag par byung zhing / so so nas bsngo rten bcas nyin bstar yum de nyid gtso bor gyur pa thams cad la bsngo ba rgyas par zhus/ sbyin bdag gi gtso bo ni bka' bcu
kun bzang don grub yin zhing / rtses dong kun dga' thabs mkhas kyis zhabs 'degs rgyas par mdzad pa'i rgyun gyi bsnyen bkur gya nom pa mdzad/ rang res kyang gong ma'i phyag
len ras bor du ma song ba'i nyin bstar dkyil 'khor phyi ma'i lha sta gon dang / bum pa sta gon dang bcas pa rgyas par byas/ zhag gis ma chod phyin sa lha dang slob ma sta
gon nyin dang po las 'og ma rnams la mi mdzad cing / dbang gi rim pa'ang pha rgyud bzhi la rus rgyan dang Da ma ru mi dgos pa sogs brgyud pa'i phyag len rung bar bgyis
sgang / mjug nas rtses dong rab 'byams pa ngag dbang bstan 'phel dang / sger pa rje drung rin po che/ 'on chos sdings nas rgya mtsho zla ba sogs pheb pa'i chos sdings phyag
phyi rnams dbang kha shas la'ang yod/ tshong 'dus tshogs pa grwa tshang yongs rdzogs kyang sku rim rgyab chos la pheb pa rnal 'byor rgyud man chad thams cad la yod cing
/

bka' kun bzang don grub kyis ring 'tsho'i rten 'byung grwa dmangs thams cad kyis gnang bar/ dpon slob sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan gyis rdzas brgyad 'bul ba sogs gsung bshad rgyas
par gnang / de mtshungs kun dga' thabs mkhas kyis kyang rgyas par byas pa sngar ltar gsung chog /tshong 'dus tshogs mkhan slob yongs rdzogs nas tshe dpag med kyi gsung
chog dang 'brel ba'i spyi sgos thams cad nas tshan grangs sogs rgyas pa'i sgo nas mkhan rin po ches gsung bshad/ rab byung ba spyi tshogs nas maNDal rgyas pa dang bcas
tshe dpag med kyi gsung chog dang 'brel ba rab byung mkhan rin po ches gsung bshad rgyas par gnang zhing / bkra shis chos sde nas 'a zhwa'i rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po dpon
slob bcu gsum pheb pas gzims chung du sgrol dkar dang 'brel ba'i rten 'byung / dpon rin po ches maNDal zhal bzhes kyi gsung bshad stsal bas snga rting thams cad du rten 'brel
'grigs par byung / khong dpon slob la lam dbang / mkha' spyod ma'i lung kha shas phul/ lha tshes la chos skyong chen po pheb par phrin bcol zhu bar phyin par kha btags
legs pa/ gser zho/ hu ja bar khag bcas stsal bas padma 'od kyi gzhal yas su slob dpon chen pos chos 'khor bskor ba dang 'dra bar byung zhes shin tu dgyes pa'i legs so
stsal/ rdor phreng grol bstun ngor pa'i bla ma sde dger pheb mi zhig la sde dge dpon gzungs rgyal nas dgos tshul gnang ba ltar bde mchog dkar po'i byin rlabs/ sgrub thabs
rgya mtsho'i rjes gnang brgya dang zhe gsum/ pod gzhung

gi lung bcas dang / sgrub thabs brgya rtsa rjes gnang don dgu /pod gzhung bcas sngar gyi chos gsan mi thams cad dang lhan du nyin lnga'i bar phul/ nyin gcig 'bras spungs pa/
ri bde ba/ dpal ri ba/ chos 'khor gnas rab 'byams pa kun dga' smon lam sogs sgrub tsho lnga la bsnyen rdzogs dang / dpal ri ba sogs dge tshul nyi shu skor bsgrubs/ 'di
nyin nas cung zhig grib 'khrugs lta bus khams ma bde ba dang skad 'gags pa byung bas ngal bso bgyid khul byas kyang rta ra mdo pa sde pa rab phun pheb/ rnal 'byor ma'i byin
rlabs sogs 'bul dgos byung / tshugs nas ma grol bar rab byung ba'i grwa pa ba sger du 'phrad mi shin tu mang bas bzhes spro'i rigs mang ba bcas yang yang byung zhing /
kun dga' bsam 'grub kyis nyin bstar zho ma chad par byung / sbyin bdag bka' kun don dang thabs mkhas gnyis kyis bla gos/ mthang gos sogs dang / bka' bcu pas dngul srang
bco lnga/ thabs mkhas nas ja 'khor drug gnyis/ mar ltar che ba sogs dpag med byung / tshes bcu gcig la bsam yas nas bteg pas grwa dmangs yongs rdzogs/ mkhan tshang rab 'byams
pa/ dbu chos/ sde pa rdzong dpon gnyis/ sde pa khrus phu nas bka' kun don/ thabs mkhas/ drung 'tsho kun dga' lags/ bkras rab lags/ spyi sa zhal ngo sku rten pa lags
dpon g.yog gnyis sogs skyel mi shin tu mang bar pheb pa grwa dmangs rnams khams gsum na kha bsgral ba nas pheb/

kha btags kyi g.yab mo gnang / rta kha bsgyur thengs gsum byas/ rab byung mkhan slob sde pa chos mdzad sogs ska cog mchod rten nas phyir pheb/ dmangs rnams dal la khongs su
bka' kun don gyis dbang dpal sngon du btang pa'i gung tshigs/ gsol ja/ zhal ngo sku rten lags kyis gsol zho sogs rgyas par byung zhing / de nas nged rnams yar thon/ khong
dpon slob rnams phyir pheb/ thugs 'phreng bar gnang / g.yab mo dang rta kha bsgyur ba lan gsum byas/ de nub sgrags mdar bsdad/ 'phrad mi mang bar byung / sang nyin snga
bar bteg pas rdor brag klu sdings su sde pa chos rje lags pheb pa'i thab bsu/ gung gro rgyas par gnang / gsung gleng 'phel bar byung / de nub rang gnas su snga bar slebs/
re zhig ngal bsos/ yang tshes bcu dgu skor la sger pa rje drung rin po che pheb par rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i khrid zhal shes kyis brgyan pa shin tu smin pa zhag bcu gcig
gi bar phul zhing / tshar lugs 'jigs byed bcu gsum ma'i dbang / mi g.yo ba dkar sngon/ chags lugs tshe dpag med dkar po dang / khro bo gtsug tor 'bar ba/ sum pa lo tsA ba
nas brgyud pa'i dbyangs can ma dkar mo/ dmar zor ma'i rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab 'khor lo khro lo nas brgyud pa/ 'jam dpal gang blo ma'i rjes
gnang rngog lo nas brgyud pa/ 'jam dbyangs smra seng yum dbyangs can sngon mo dang bcas pa'i rjes gnang pha dam pa nas brgyud pa/ so so'i yi ge lung bcas 'khrugs drag pa
rang ma byung kyang zhag bcu gcig bar du phul/ lcags zam pa bstan 'dzin

mchog grub kyang zhabs phyir yod/ de grol 'phral 'bras spungs gnas chung nas lhun grub chos 'byor can gsum pheb par kye rdo rje'i dbang ras bris la brten pa/ mkha' spyod ma'i
byin rlabs dang / khrid smin pa dang / gur lha brgyad dang / dmag zor ma'i rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa bgyis/ ra ba smad nas rab 'byams pa'i byams pa dang lding dpon
a mgon sogs bcu skor dang / mda' phu dgon nas stag ru ba'i chos lags sogs lnga bcas par bde mchog lha lnga'i dbang sta gon dngos gzhi bcas dang / kun rig gi dbang / 'ch-i
med dpal ster gyi tshe dbang / mda' phu rnams la dmar khrid tshem ca bu lugs kyi shar khrid rnams byas/ 'phags sde pa kun dga' 'byung gnas bcas bzhi/ rnam ser rab 'byams
pa lhun grub rgyal po bcas par dge tshul dang / 'byung 'dul dang / gur lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang byas/ bsam yas nas sleb 'phral yab sku zhabs dang / sde pa bka' blon gnyis
bcas nas lan drug gi bar bka' tham gnang ba'i 'ong dgos tshul pheb kyang khams ma drag pas bka' 'gyang zhus/ sde pa khrus phu nas yab lha sa nas tshur lam pheb pa'i
bka' blon zhal ngo gnyis sogs nas gang ci'i gsung 'phros rgyas par gnang 'dug tshul dang / khams bde mus byung na gang mgyogs phyin pa rang dga' ba 'dug tshul pheb cing /
'di skabs grwa pa rnams dang gtso bor bla brang nas khur blangs pa'i sku 'bum la zhig gso/ gzhi bdag gi mkhar sogs rgyas par bgyis pa'ang gegs med du grub/
